            "url": "https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/57986924", 
            "userName": "灰原哀的梨味算符", 
            "userLink": "https://www.zhihu.com/people/827e480e03c3cf7140d8b301144341d0", 
            "upvote": 19, 
            "title": "梨推（hei）的拓扑厨房（二）", 
            "content": "<p>本来想写 AQFT 的，但是没想好起什么标题，象征性地征求一下意见(o-ωｑ))。</p><p>实名酸一下能去上海 Fan Meeting 的大佬们，我是白天想，夜里翻，做梦都想上海滩，上海的梨推(hei)多又多，我们时刻准备着。庆祝逢田姐唱片solo出道以及新番组成立，做一天立派的真梨推，到 3 月 24 日 23:59 止 ωωω</p><hr/><p><b><i>数学篇：矢量丛、联络与曲率</i></b></p><ul><li><b>矢量丛</b></li></ul><p>在物理中一类重要的纤维丛便是矢量丛，矢量丛是以矢量空间为纤维的纤维丛，定义如下。</p><p>Definition 1: 秩为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=r\" alt=\"r\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的<b>矢量丛 (Vector bundle) </b>由光滑映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpi%3AE%5Crightarrow+M\" alt=\"\\pi:E\\rightarrow M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，流形 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 决定。</p><p>Remark 1: 如果 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cforall+x%5Cin+M\" alt=\"\\forall x\\in M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 都有开邻域 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U\" alt=\"U\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cexists%5Cvarphi%3A%5Cpi%5E%7B-1%7D%28U%29%5Crightarrow+U%5Ctimes%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%5E%7Br%7D\" alt=\"\\exists\\varphi:\\pi^{-1}(U)\\rightarrow U\\times\\mathbb{C}^{r}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 使得如下关系</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbegin%7Balign%7D%26%5Cpi%5E%7B-1%7D%28U_%7Bx%7D%29%5Cstackrel%7B%5Cvarphi%7D%5Crightarrow+U%5Ctimes%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%5E%7Br%7D%5Cstackrel%7Bpr_%7B1%7D%7D%5Crightarrow+U%5C%5C+%26%5Cstackrel%7B%5Cpi%7D%5Cdownarrow%5C%5C+%26U+%5Cend%7Balign%7D\" alt=\"\\begin{align}&amp;\\pi^{-1}(U_{x})\\stackrel{\\varphi}\\rightarrow U\\times\\mathbb{C}^{r}\\stackrel{pr_{1}}\\rightarrow U\\\\ &amp;\\stackrel{\\pi}\\downarrow\\\\ &amp;U \\end{align}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>可交换且这些映射在每个纤维上都是线性的，那么我们称纤维 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E_%7Bx%7D%3A%3D%5Cpi%5E%7B-1%7D%28x%29\" alt=\"E_{x}:=\\pi^{-1}(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=r\" alt=\"r\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 维矢量空间结构是<b>局域平凡 (Locally trivial) </b>的。</p><p>Remark 2: 如果纤维为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 或 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{C}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的矢量空间，那么我们相应的可以考虑实或复的矢量丛。对于量子力学中的情况，我们考虑的一般都是复矢量丛。</p><p>Example 1: 对任意流形 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，我们总有平凡矢量丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%5Ctimes%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%5E%7Br%7D\" alt=\"M\\times\\mathbb{C}^{r}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。其上存在一矢量丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 在局域上为平凡纤维丛但全局上并不是，称作<b>扭矢量丛 (Twisted vector bundle)</b>。一个最简单的例子就是 Mobius 线丛。考虑 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B1%7D%3D%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%2F%5Cmathbb%7BZ%7D\" alt=\"S^{1}=\\mathbb{R}/\\mathbb{Z}\" eeimg=\"1\"/>，可以构造平凡线丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的商线丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L\" alt=\"L\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 满足</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L%3A%3D%28%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5Ctimes%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%29%2F%5Cmathbb%7BZ%7D\" alt=\"L:=(\\mathbb{R}\\times\\mathbb{R})/\\mathbb{Z}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BZ%7D%3A%28x%2Cy%29%5Chookrightarrow+%28x%2Bn%2Cy%29\" alt=\"\\mathbb{Z}:(x,y)\\hookrightarrow (x+n,y)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 或 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28x%2Cy%29%5Chookrightarrow%28x%2Bn%2C%28-1%29%5E%7Bn%7Dy%29\" alt=\"(x,y)\\hookrightarrow(x+n,(-1)^{n}y)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>二者对 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=x\" alt=\"x\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 坐标的射影可以定义一个光滑映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L%5Crightarrow+S%5E%7B1%7D\" alt=\"L\\rightarrow S^{1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 使得 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L\" alt=\"L\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 变为环 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B1%7D\" alt=\"S^{1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的线丛。第一种情形实际上就是平凡线丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B1%7D%5Ctimes%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"S^{1}\\times\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，而第二种情形则定义了 Mobius 线丛。</p><p>Remark 3: 利用<b>上循环 (Cocycle) </b>可以为矢量丛给出一个更为准确的观点。令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%3D%5Cbigcup_%7B%5Calpha%7DU_%7B%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"M=\\bigcup_{\\alpha}U_{\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的覆盖，其上每一个 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U_%7B%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"U_{\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 都具有平凡化映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%7D%3A%5Cpi%5E%7B-1%7D%28U_%7B%5Calpha%7D%29%5Cstackrel%7B%5Ccong%7D%5Crightarrow+U_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5Ctimes%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%5E%7Br%7D\" alt=\"\\varphi_{\\alpha}:\\pi^{-1}(U_{\\alpha})\\stackrel{\\cong}\\rightarrow U_{\\alpha}\\times\\mathbb{C}^{r}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5Ccap+U_%7B%5Cbeta%7D\" alt=\"U_{\\alpha}\\cap U_{\\beta}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 处我们有两类平凡化映射：</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbegin%7Balign%7D%26%5Cpi%5E%7B-1%7D%28U_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%29%5Cstackrel%7B%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%7D%7D%5Crightarrow+U_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5Ctimes%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%5E%7Br%7D%5C%5C+%26%5Cstackrel%7B%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%7D%5Cdownarrow%5C%5C+%26U_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5Ctimes%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%5E%7Br%7D+%5Cend%7Balign%7D\" alt=\"\\begin{align}&amp;\\pi^{-1}(U_{\\alpha\\beta})\\stackrel{\\varphi_{\\alpha}}\\rightarrow U_{\\alpha\\beta}\\times\\mathbb{C}^{r}\\\\ &amp;\\stackrel{\\varphi_{\\beta}}\\downarrow\\\\ &amp;U_{\\alpha\\beta}\\times\\mathbb{C}^{r} \\end{align}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>其中 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"\\varphi_{\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Cbeta%7D\" alt=\"\\varphi_{\\beta}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是可相容的， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5Ccirc%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7B-1%7D%28x%2Cv%29%3D%28x%2C%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%28v%29%29%2C%5Cquad+x%5Cin+U_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%2Cv%5Cin%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%5E%7Br%7D\" alt=\"\\varphi_{\\alpha}\\circ\\varphi_{\\beta}^{-1}(x,v)=(x,\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}(v)),\\quad x\\in U_{\\alpha\\beta},v\\in\\mathbb{C}^{r}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%3AU_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5Crightarrow+GL%28r%2C%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%29\" alt=\"\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}:U_{\\alpha\\beta}\\rightarrow GL(r,\\mathbb{C})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。我们将映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D\" alt=\"\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 称作<b>转变函数 (Transition function)</b>，满足如下性质：</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Calpha%7D%3D1\" alt=\"\\varphi_{\\alpha\\alpha}=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Cbeta%5Calpha%7D%3D%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7B-1%7D\" alt=\"\\varphi_{\\beta\\alpha}=\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}^{-1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Cgamma%5Calpha%7D%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Cbeta%5Cgamma%7D%3D1\" alt=\"\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}\\varphi_{\\gamma\\alpha}\\varphi_{\\beta\\gamma}=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>矢量丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可以由转变函数完全确定，给定 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5C%7B%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5C%7D_%7B%5Calpha%2C%5Cbeta%5Cin+I%7D\" alt=\"\\{\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}\\}_{\\alpha,\\beta\\in I}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 满足上述三条性质，定义</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E%3A%3D%5Cleft%28%5Camalg_%7B%5Calpha%5Cin+I%7DU_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5Ctimes%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%5E%7Br%7D%5Cright%29%2F%5C%2C%5Csim\" alt=\"E:=\\left(\\amalg_{\\alpha\\in I}U_{\\alpha}\\times\\mathbb{C}^{r}\\right)/\\,\\sim\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>其中 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28x_%7B%5Calpha%7D%2Cv%29%5Csim%28x_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%2Cv%29%5CLeftrightarrow+x_%7B%5Calpha%7D%3Dx_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%5Cin+U_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5Ccap+U_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%2C%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%28v%29%3Dw\" alt=\"(x_{\\alpha},v)\\sim(x_{\\beta},v)\\Leftrightarrow x_{\\alpha}=x_{\\beta}\\in U_{\\alpha}\\cap U_{\\beta},\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}(v)=w\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。转变函数的性质保证了商群 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的等价关系是良好定义的。</p><p>Example 2: 我们的第二个例子实际上不完全算是矢量丛，但它对于纤维丛理论十分重要，它的纤维是一类群。这样的拓扑空间也是我们一般意义上所谓的<b>纤维丛 (Fibre bundle)</b> 的定义。假设有矢量丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，邻域 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U_%7B%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"U_{\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与转变函数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Cbeta%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"\\varphi_{\\beta\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。由于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Cbeta%5Calpha%7D%28x%29\" alt=\"\\varphi_{\\beta\\alpha}(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为结构群 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=G\" alt=\"G\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的元素，我们可以以 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=G\" alt=\"G\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为纤维通过局域平凡华 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5Ctimes+G\" alt=\"U_{\\alpha}\\times G\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 构造一类新的纤维丛，它们之间可以通过转变函数相关联：</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%28x_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%29%3D%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Cbeta%5Calpha%7D%28x_%7B%5Calpha%7D%29g_%7B%5Calpha%7D%28x_%7B%5Calpha%7D%29\" alt=\"g_{\\beta}(x_{\\beta})=\\varphi_{\\beta\\alpha}(x_{\\alpha})g_{\\alpha}(x_{\\alpha})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>这样构造得到的新纤维丛就称作 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的<b>主丛 (Principal bundle)</b>。如果我们知道作用在纤维上的结构群，那我们就可以由主丛重构 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。或者说，选取 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=G\" alt=\"G\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的一类不同的表示，我们就可以通过主丛构造一类不同的矢量丛，这也是为什么我们将其称之为主丛的原因。</p><p>Example 3: 对任意光滑流形 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，它的切丛总是一个实矢量丛。转变上循环由 Jacobi 矩阵的坐标变换给出。若切丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=TM\" alt=\"TM\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 平凡，我们则说流形 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是可平行化的。这意味着存在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=n\" alt=\"n\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 维矢量场 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2CX_%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"X_{1},\\cdots,X_{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 使得 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cforall%5C+x%5Cin+M\" alt=\"\\forall\\ x\\in M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 都构成切丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7Bx%7DM\" alt=\"T_{x}M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的基。</p><p>Remark 4: 令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%3AM%5Crightarrow+N\" alt=\"f:M\\rightarrow N\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为一光滑映射， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=p%3AE%5Crightarrow+N\" alt=\"p:E\\rightarrow N\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=N\" alt=\"N\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的矢量丛。不难得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%5E%7B%2A%7DE%3D%5C%7B%28x%2Ce%29%5Cin+M%5Ctimes+E%2Cf%28x%29%3Dp%28e%29%5C%7D\" alt=\"f^{*}E=\\{(x,e)\\in M\\times E,f(x)=p(e)\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X\" alt=\"X\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上得到一正则矢量丛结构。这可以看做是矢量丛的拉回映射。</p><p>Remark 5: 令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F\" alt=\"F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的矢量丛。可以利用线性代数拓展矢量丛的标准构造，从而定义如下复合矢量丛：</p><p>(1) 直和矢量丛： <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E%5Coplus+F\" alt=\"E\\oplus F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>(2) 张量积矢量丛： <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E%5Cotimes+F\" alt=\"E\\otimes F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>(3) <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ctextrm%7BHom%7D%28E%2CF%29%5Ccong+E%5E%7B%2A%7D%5Cotimes+F\" alt=\"\\textrm{Hom}(E,F)\\cong E^{*}\\otimes F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Definition 2: 给定矢量丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpi%3A+E%5Crightarrow+X\" alt=\"\\pi: E\\rightarrow X\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，有连续映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=s%3AM%5Crightarrow+E\" alt=\"s:M\\rightarrow E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 满足 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpi%5Ccirc+s%3D1\" alt=\"\\pi\\circ s=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，则该连续映射称为矢量丛的<b>截面 (Section)</b>。其中 1 表示 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X\" alt=\"X\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的常数函数。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的截面空间表示为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CGamma%28X%2CE%29\" alt=\"\\Gamma(X,E)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。当 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 光滑时，截面映射必须光滑，相应的截面空间也是光滑的，即存在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CGamma%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28X%2CE%29\" alt=\"\\Gamma^{\\infty}(X,E)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><ul><li><b>联络与曲率</b></li></ul><p>令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为一光滑流形， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E%5Crightarrow+M\" alt=\"E\\rightarrow M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为一光滑矢量丛。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%3BE%29\" alt=\"\\Omega^{k}(M;E)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 表示 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的<img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k\" alt=\"k\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 阶微分形式空间：</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%3BE%29%3A%3D%5CGamma%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%2CE%5Cotimes%5Cbigwedge%5E%7Bk%7DT%5E%7B%2A%7DM%29\" alt=\"\\Omega^{k}(M;E):=\\Gamma^{\\infty}(M,E\\otimes\\bigwedge^{k}T^{*}M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Definition 3: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上存在一线性映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla%3A%5CGamma%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%3BE%29%5Crightarrow+%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%3BE%29\" alt=\"\\nabla:\\Gamma^{\\infty}(M;E)\\rightarrow \\Omega^{1}(M;E)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 满足 Leibniz 法则，该映射称为<b>联络 (Connection)</b>。矢量丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E%5Crightarrow+M\" alt=\"E\\rightarrow M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的联络允许我们在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上沿着 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的光滑截面方向取方向导数。对任一矢量场 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X%5Cin%5Cmathcal%7BX%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"X\\in\\mathcal{X}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，方向导数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla_%7BX%7D%28s%29%3A%3Dl_%7BX%7D%28%5Cnabla+s%29\" alt=\"\\nabla_{X}(s):=l_{X}(\\nabla s)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 构成映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla_%7BX%7D%3A%5CGamma%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%3BE%29%5Crightarrow%5CGamma%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%3BE%29\" alt=\"\\nabla_{X}:\\Gamma^{\\infty}(M;E)\\rightarrow\\Gamma^{\\infty}(M;E)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Lemma 1: 矢量丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的联络空间是 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%2C%5Ctextrm%7BEnd%7D%28E%29%29\" alt=\"\\Omega^{1}(M,\\textrm{End}(E))\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的一仿射空间。</p><p>Proof 1: 令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla\" alt=\"\\nabla\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 和 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla%27\" alt=\"\\nabla&#39;\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上两联络。由 Leibniz 律有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28%5Cnabla-%5Cnabla%27%29fs%3Df%28%5Cnabla-%5Cnabla%27%29s%5C+%5Cforall+f%5Cin+C%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28X%29%2C%5C+s%5Cin%5CGamma%28M%3BE%29\" alt=\"(\\nabla-\\nabla&#39;)fs=f(\\nabla-\\nabla&#39;)s\\ \\forall f\\in C^{\\infty}(X),\\ s\\in\\Gamma(M;E)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。从而差算符 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla-%5Cnabla%27\" alt=\"\\nabla-\\nabla&#39;\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 满足 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla-%5Cnabla%27%3A%5CGamma%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%3BE%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%3BE%29\" alt=\"\\nabla-\\nabla&#39;:\\Gamma^{\\infty}(M;E)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{1}(M;E)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为无穷光滑，且 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla-%5Cnabla%27%5Cin+%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%3B%5Ctextrm%7BEnd%7D%28E%29%29\" alt=\"\\nabla-\\nabla&#39;\\in \\Omega^{1}(M;\\textrm{End}(E))\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Remark 6:</p><p>i) 对一平凡矢量丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E%3DM%5Ctimes%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%5E%7Br%7D\" alt=\"E=M\\times\\mathbb{C}^{r}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 我们总能使 de Rham 算符 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d\" alt=\"d\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 给出的平凡联络拓展为矢量值函数。由 Lemma 1，任意构造一联络 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla%3Dd%2BA\" alt=\"\\nabla=d+A\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ( <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%2CM_%7Br%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%29%29\" alt=\"A\\in\\Omega^{1}(M,M_{r}(\\mathbb{C}))\" eeimg=\"1\"/> )， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla\" alt=\"\\nabla\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为矩阵值的 1 形式。</p><p>ii) 对一般矢量丛，可以在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U_%7B%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"U_{\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的局部平凡化区域中定义 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla%3Dd%2BA_%7B%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"\\nabla=d+A_{\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。在两平凡化交集 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5Ccap+U_%7B%5Cbeta%7D\" alt=\"U_{\\alpha}\\cap U_{\\beta}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上存在两个 1 形式满足</p><p> (1) <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7B%5Calpha%7D%3D%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7DA_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%5Cvarphi%5E%7B-1%7D_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D-%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7B-1%7Dd%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D\" alt=\"A_{\\alpha}=\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}A_{\\beta}\\varphi^{-1}_{\\alpha\\beta}-\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}^{-1}d\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>其中 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%3AU_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5Crightarrow+GL%28r%2C%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%29\" alt=\"\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}:U_{\\alpha\\beta}\\rightarrow GL(r,\\mathbb{C})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为转变函数。类似 Remark 3 中上循环的观点，可以认为矢量丛上的联络构成矩阵值 1 形式的集合 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5C%7BA_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28U_%7B%5Calpha%7D%2CM_%7Br%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%29%29%5C%7D_%7B%5Calpha%5Cin+I%7D\" alt=\"\\{A_{\\alpha}\\in\\Omega^{1}(U_{\\alpha},M_{r}(\\mathbb{C}))\\}_{\\alpha\\in I}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，该集合内的 1 形式实际上就是物理中的局域规范变换形式。</p><p>Remark 7: 考虑矢量丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E%5Crightarrow+M\" alt=\"E\\rightarrow M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 秩为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=r\" alt=\"r\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。定义空间</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%28E%29%3A%3D%5Cbigcup_%7Bx%5Cin+M%7DF%28E_%7Bx%7D%29\" alt=\"F(E):=\\bigcup_{x\\in M}F(E_{x})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E_%7Bx%7D\" alt=\"E_{x}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 中所有基底构成的空间。e.g. <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=e_%7Bx%7D%3D%28e_%7Bx%7D%5E%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Ce_%7Bx%7D%5E%7Br%7D%29%5Cin+F%28E_%7Bx%7D%29\" alt=\"e_{x}=(e_{x}^{1},\\cdots,e_{x}^{r})\\in F(E_{x})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。利用局部平凡化不难在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%28E%29\" alt=\"F(E)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上定义一光滑流形结构，i.e. 投影<img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpi%3AF%28E%29%5Crightarrow+M\" alt=\"\\pi:F(E)\\rightarrow M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=GL%28r%2C%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%29\" alt=\"GL(r,\\mathbb{C})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%28E%29\" alt=\"F(E)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上保纤维不变（纤维结构与基底变换无关）的作用，即 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%28E%29%2FGL%28r%2C%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%29%5Ccong+M\" alt=\"F(E)/GL(r,\\mathbb{C})\\cong M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>现令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla\" alt=\"\\nabla\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的联络， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5C%7BA_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28U_%7B%5Calpha%7D%2CM_%7Br%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%29%29%5C%7D_%7B%5Calpha%5Cin+I%7D\" alt=\"\\{A_{\\alpha}\\in\\Omega^{1}(U_{\\alpha},M_{r}(\\mathbb{C}))\\}_{\\alpha\\in I}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为局部平凡化上矩阵值 1 形式的集合。对这一类微分形式做拉回，我们会得到 1 形式集合 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5C%7B%5Cpi%5E%7B%2A%7DA_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5C%7D_%7B%5Calpha%5Cin+I%7D\" alt=\"\\{\\pi^{*}A_{\\alpha}\\}_{\\alpha\\in I}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，该集合坐落在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%28E%29\" alt=\"F(E)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的一覆盖 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5C%7B%5Cpi%5E%7B-1%7D%28U_%7B%5Calpha%7D%29%5C%7D\" alt=\"\\{\\pi^{-1}(U_{\\alpha})\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上。对于覆盖在两类局部平凡化的交集， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpi%5E%7B-1%7D%28U_%7B%5Calpha%7D%29%5Ccap%5Cpi%5E%7B-a%7D%28U_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%29%3D%5Cpi%5E%7B-1%7D%28U_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%29\" alt=\"\\pi^{-1}(U_{\\alpha})\\cap\\pi^{-a}(U_{\\beta})=\\pi^{-1}(U_{\\alpha\\beta})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，从而拉回的结果为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpi%5E%7B%2A%7DA_%7B%5Calpha%7D%3D%5Cpi%5E%7B%2A%7D%28%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7DA_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%5Cvarphi%5E%7B-1%7D_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D-%5Cvarphi%5E%7B-1%7D_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7Dd%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%29%3D%5Cpi%5E%7B%2A%7DA_%7B%5Cbeta%7D\" alt=\"\\pi^{*}A_{\\alpha}=\\pi^{*}(\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}A_{\\beta}\\varphi^{-1}_{\\alpha\\beta}-\\varphi^{-1}_{\\alpha\\beta}d\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta})=\\pi^{*}A_{\\beta}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>即可以把 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7B%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"A_{\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> “粘”在一起得到完整的 1 形式 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28F%28E%29%2C%5Cmathfrak%7Bgl%7D%28r%2C%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%29%29\" alt=\"A\\in\\Omega^{1}(F(E),\\mathfrak{gl}(r,\\mathbb{C}))\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，赋值为 Lie 代数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathfrak%7Bgl%7D%28r%2C%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%29%3DM_%7Br%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%29\" alt=\"\\mathfrak{gl}(r,\\mathbb{C})=M_{r}(\\mathbb{C})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。可以证明该形式具有如下性质（留做习题）：</p><ul><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=l_%7B%5Cxi_%5Ctextrm%7BF%28E%29%7D%7DA%3D%5Cxi%5C+%5Cforall%5Cxi%5Cin%5Cmathfrak%7Bgl%7D%28r%2C%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%29\" alt=\"l_{\\xi_\\textrm{F(E)}}A=\\xi\\ \\forall\\xi\\in\\mathfrak{gl}(r,\\mathbb{C})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=R_%7Bg%7D%5E%7B%2A%7DA%3DgAg%5E%7B-1%7D%5C+%5Cforall+g%5Cin+GL%28r%2C%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%29\" alt=\"R_{g}^{*}A=gAg^{-1}\\ \\forall g\\in GL(r,\\mathbb{C})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </li></ul><p>综上，联络可以有三种等价表述：1. 截面上的第一阶微分算符 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla\" alt=\"\\nabla\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，2. 满足 (1) 的矩阵值 1 形式集合 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5C%7BA_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28U_%7B%5Calpha%7D%2CM_%7Br%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%29%29%5C%7D_%7B%5Calpha%5Cin+I%7D\" alt=\"\\{A_{\\alpha}\\in\\Omega^{1}(U_{\\alpha},M_{r}(\\mathbb{C}))\\}_{\\alpha\\in I}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> （也称作标架联络）；3. 满足上述两条性质的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%28E%29\" alt=\"F(E)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的矩阵值 1 形式 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A+\" alt=\"A \" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Example 4: 仍然考虑 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BP%7D%5E%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{P}^{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的均匀线丛，给定 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U_%7Bij%7D\" alt=\"U_{ij}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的转变函数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi_%7Bij%7D%28%5Bz_%7B0%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Cz_%7Bn%7D%5D%29%3Dz_%7Bi%7D%2Fz_%7Bj%7D\" alt=\"\\varphi_{ij}([z_{0},\\cdots,z_{n}])=z_{i}/z_{j}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，有</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28A_%7Bi%7D-A_%7Bj%7D%29%7C_%7BU_%7Bij%7D%7D%3D%28d%5Cvarphi_%7Bij%7D%29%5Cvarphi_%7Bij%7D%5E%7B-1%7D%3Dd%5Cln%5Cleft%28%5Cfrac%7Bz_%7Bi%7D%7D%7Bz_%7Bj%7D%7D%5Cright%29%3D%5Cfrac%7Bdz_%7Bi%7D%7D%7Bz_%7Bi%7D%7D-%5Cfrac%7Bdz_%7Bj%7D%7D%7Bz_%7Bj%7D%7D\" alt=\"(A_{i}-A_{j})|_{U_{ij}}=(d\\varphi_{ij})\\varphi_{ij}^{-1}=d\\ln\\left(\\frac{z_{i}}{z_{j}}\\right)=\\frac{dz_{i}}{z_{i}}-\\frac{dz_{j}}{z_{j}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>一个可能的解为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7Bi%7D%3A%3D%5Cpartial%5Cln%5Cleft%28%5Csum_%7Bl%3D0%7D%5E%7Bn%7D%5Cfrac%7B%7Cz_%7Bl%7D%7C%5E%7B2%7D%7D%7B%7Cz_%7Bi%7D%7C%5E%7B2%7D%7D%5Cright%29\" alt=\"A_{i}:=\\partial\\ln\\left(\\sum_{l=0}^{n}\\frac{|z_{l}|^{2}}{|z_{i}|^{2}}\\right)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>现在我们来考虑联络的曲率。可以拓展联络映射为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla%3A%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%3BE%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7Bk%2B1%7D%28M%3BE%29\" alt=\"\\nabla:\\Omega^{k}(M;E)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{k+1}(M;E)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，这里 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla%28s%5Cotimes%5Calpha%29%3D%5Cnabla+s%5Cwedge%5Calpha%2Bs%5Cotimes+d%5Calpha%2C%5C+s%5Cin%5CGamma%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%2CE%29%2C%5Calpha%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\nabla(s\\otimes\\alpha)=\\nabla s\\wedge\\alpha+s\\otimes d\\alpha,\\ s\\in\\Gamma^{\\infty}(M,E),\\alpha\\in\\Omega^{k}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。显然这时 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla%5E%7B2%7D%5Cneq0\" alt=\"\\nabla^{2}\\neq0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，这也是为什么在物理上我们说平行移动会产生差别的原因， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla%5E%7B2%7D%28fs%29%3Df%5Cnabla%5E%7B2%7D%28s%29\" alt=\"\\nabla^{2}(fs)=f\\nabla^{2}(s)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，从而可以由此出发定义曲率 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%28%5Cnabla%29%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7B2%7D%28M%2C%5Ctextrm%7BEnd%7D%28E%29%29\" alt=\"F(\\nabla)\\in\\Omega^{2}(M,\\textrm{End}(E))\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>Definition 4: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%28%5Cnabla%29%28s%29%3A%3D%5Cnabla%5E%7B2%7D%28s%29%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7B2%7D%28M%3B%5Ctextrm%7BEnd%7D%28E%29%29\" alt=\"F(\\nabla)(s):=\\nabla^{2}(s)\\in\\Omega^{2}(M;\\textrm{End}(E))\" eeimg=\"1\"/>为联络 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla\" alt=\"\\nabla\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的曲率。</p><p>对任一局部平凡化 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla%7C_%7BU_%7B%5Calpha%7D%7D%3Dd%2BA_%7B%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"\\nabla|_{U_{\\alpha}}=d+A_{\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可以得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F_%7B%5Calpha%7D%3D%28d%2BA_%7B%5Calpha%7D%29%5E%7B2%7D%3DdA_%7B%5Calpha%7D%2BA_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5Cwedge+A_%7B%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"F_{\\alpha}=(d+A_{\\alpha})^{2}=dA_{\\alpha}+A_{\\alpha}\\wedge A_{\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>如我们之前所述的，可以很容易地由这条结果给出局域规范变换 (1)，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbegin%7Balign%7D+F_%7B%5Calpha%7D%26%3Dd%28%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7DA_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7B-1%7D-%28d%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%29%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7B-1%7D%29%2B%28%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7DA_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7B-1%7D-%28d%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%29%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7B-1%7D%29%5Cwedge%28%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7DA_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7B-1%7D-%28d%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%29%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7B-1%7D%29%5C%5C+%26%3D%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7DdA_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7B-1%7D%2B%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%28A_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%5Cwedge+A_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%29%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7B-1%7D%5C%5C+%26%3D%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7DF_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7B-1%7D+%5Cend%7Balign%7D\" alt=\"\\begin{align} F_{\\alpha}&amp;=d(\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}A_{\\beta}\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}^{-1}-(d\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta})\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}^{-1})+(\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}A_{\\beta}\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}^{-1}-(d\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta})\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}^{-1})\\wedge(\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}A_{\\beta}\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}^{-1}-(d\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta})\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}^{-1})\\\\ &amp;=\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}dA_{\\beta}\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}^{-1}+\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}(A_{\\beta}\\wedge A_{\\beta})\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}^{-1}\\\\ &amp;=\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}F_{\\beta}\\varphi_{\\alpha\\beta}^{-1} \\end{align}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>所以虽然联络并不是 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的任意配丛的截面，但它的曲率却是满足截面性质的。由上述曲率的局域表示可以得到一个我们很熟悉的很有用的公式</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%28%5Cnabla%29%28X%2CY%29%3D%5B%5Cnabla_%7BX%7D%2C%5Cnabla_%7BY%7D%5D-%5Cnabla_%7B%5BX%2CY%5D%7D%2C%5C+X%2CY%5Cin%5Cmathcal%7BX%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"F(\\nabla)(X,Y)=[\\nabla_{X},\\nabla_{Y}]-\\nabla_{[X,Y]},\\ X,Y\\in\\mathcal{X}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>读者可能会注意到这和 Lie 导数的表示是很相似的，但如我们在广义相对论中接触到的一样，Lie 导数和协变导数是有很大的区别的，在纤维丛的观点下一个显著的差别就体现在截面上的微分形式集合是矩阵赋值还是 Lie 代数赋值的。</p><p>Example 5: 仍然回到线丛， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M_%7B1%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%29%3D%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D\" alt=\"M_{1}(\\mathbb{C})=\\mathbb{C}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是阿贝尔的，即 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%5Cwedge+A\" alt=\"A\\wedge A\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 在这时总为零。从而 Example 4 的联络曲率可以表示为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Comega_%7Bi%7D%3Dd%5Cpartial%5Cln%5Cleft%28%5Csum_%7Bl%3D0%7D%5E%7Bn%7D%5Cfrac%7B%7Cz_%7Bl%7D%7C%5E%7B2%7D%7D%7B%7Cz_%7Bi%7D%7C%5E%7B2%7D%7D%5Cright%29%3D%5Cbar%7B%5Cpartial%7D%5Cpartial%5Cln%5Cleft%28%5Csum_%7Bl%3D0%7D%5E%7Bn%7D%5Cfrac%7B%7Cz_%7Bl%7D%7C%5E%7B2%7D%7D%7B%7Cz_%7Bi%7D%7C%5E%7B2%7D%7D%5Cright%29\" alt=\"\\omega_{i}=d\\partial\\ln\\left(\\sum_{l=0}^{n}\\frac{|z_{l}|^{2}}{|z_{i}|^{2}}\\right)=\\bar{\\partial}\\partial\\ln\\left(\\sum_{l=0}^{n}\\frac{|z_{l}|^{2}}{|z_{i}|^{2}}\\right)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Lemma 2: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla%5E%7B%5Ctextrm%7BEnd%7D%28E%29%7D%28F%28%5Cnabla%5E%7BE%7D%29%29%3D0\" alt=\"\\nabla^{\\textrm{End}(E)}(F(\\nabla^{E}))=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> (Bianchi 恒等式)。</p><p>Proof 2:<img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla%5E%7B%5Ctextrm%7BEnd%7D%28E%29%7D%28F%28%5Cnabla%5E%7BE%7D%29%29%28s%29%3D%5Cnabla%5E%7BE%7D%28F%28%5Cnabla%29%28s%29%29-F%28%5Cnabla%5E%7BE%7D%29%28%5Cnabla%5E%7BE%7D%28s%29%29%3D%28%5Cnabla%5E%7BE%7D%29%5E%7B3%7D%28s%29-%28%5Cnabla%5E%7BE%7D%29%5E%7B3%7D%28s%29%3D0.\" alt=\"\\nabla^{\\textrm{End}(E)}(F(\\nabla^{E}))(s)=\\nabla^{E}(F(\\nabla)(s))-F(\\nabla^{E})(\\nabla^{E}(s))=(\\nabla^{E})^{3}(s)-(\\nabla^{E})^{3}(s)=0.\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>(吐槽一句，不用指标证明 Bianchi 实在过于舒服了，index-free 是最好的语言(暴论))</p><p><b><i>物理篇：瞬子与 Berry 相</i></b></p><ul><li><b>瞬子</b></li></ul><p>纤维丛在规范场论中是非常重要的工具，这里我们讨论两个具体例子。首先是 Yang--Mills 场中的瞬子，对于一般量子场论，我们考虑场位形时一般所做的就是对作用量求极值以得到 Euler--Langrange 方程，再解方程来判断场位形。但在很多情形，运动方程都不太容易得到解析解。但在 Yang--Mills 场中我们可以有不依赖最小作用量的方式来得到场位形的信息。考虑 Euclide 空间，其空间中场位形的解就称作<b>瞬子 (Instanton)</b>。对于作用量</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%3D%5Cint%5C%2CF%5Cwedge%5Cstar+F\" alt=\"S=\\int\\,F\\wedge\\star F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>这里我们省略了求迹符号。如何不通过最小作用量的方式得到作用量极值呢？这时需要注意到在 Euclide 空间中内积是非简并且总是正定的，考虑如下积分：</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7B%5Cpm%7D%3D%5Cint%28F%5Cpm%5Cstar+F%29%5Cwedge%5Cstar%28F%5Cpm%5Cstar+F%29\" alt=\"T_{\\pm}=\\int(F\\pm\\star F)\\wedge\\star(F\\pm\\star F)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>由于内积正定， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7B%5Cpm%7D%5Cgeq0\" alt=\"T_{\\pm}\\geq0\" eeimg=\"1\"/>总成立。利用内积的对称性可以得到</p><p> (2) <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=2S%5Cpm2%5Cint%5C%2CF%5Cwedge+F%5Cgeq0%5CLeftrightarrow+S%5Cgeq%5Cbigg%7B%7C%7D%5Cint%5C%2CF%5Cwedge+F%5Cbigg%7B%7C%7D\" alt=\"2S\\pm2\\int\\,F\\wedge F\\geq0\\Leftrightarrow S\\geq\\bigg{|}\\int\\,F\\wedge F\\bigg{|}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>不难发现等号在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%3D%5Cpm%5Cstar+F\" alt=\"F=\\pm\\star F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时取得。满足此条件的场位形称作（反）自对偶场位形，这里我们都考虑自对偶场位形 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%3D%5Cstar+F\" alt=\"F=\\star F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>在这一次 note 里我们不会谈太多的例子，但在之后的内容中我们会很多次见到这些有用的场位形，这些特殊场位形的存在让我们意识到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cint%5C%2CF%5Cwedge+F\" alt=\"\\int\\,F\\wedge F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是很有价值的一个东西，后来人们把它称作<b>示性类 (Characteristic class)</b>，人们后来也发现它是一类重要的拓扑不变量，这也就意味着只要找到 (2) 的解，它就一定是作用量的局域极值，换句话说，自对偶场位形就是瞬子：Euclide 空间中场方程的解。</p><p>接下来我们开始具体的讨论，考虑 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SU%282%29\" alt=\"SU(2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 规范群。从量子场论课上我们已经知道  <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SU%282%29%2F%5Cmathbb%7BZ%7D_%7B2%7D%5Ccong+SO%283%29%5Ccong+S%5E%7B3%7D\" alt=\"SU(2)/\\mathbb{Z}_{2}\\cong SO(3)\\cong S^{3}\" eeimg=\"1\"/>，所以从流形的观点来看可以认为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SU%282%29\" alt=\"SU(2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B3%7D\" alt=\"S^{3}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是等同的。场论中我们证明过 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SU%282%29\" alt=\"SU(2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 中任意元素可以写为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%3Dit%5E%7Bi%7D%5Csigma_%7Bi%7D%2Bt%5E%7B4%7DI_%7B2%5Ctimes2%7D\" alt=\"U=it^{i}\\sigma_{i}+t^{4}I_{2\\times2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>现在我们想要在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5E%7B4%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{R}^{4}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上构造一个确实的瞬子结构，为了让场位形在远离原点处转化为平凡流形，可以将时空分为两个区域：</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U_%7BN%7D%3D%5C%7Bx%5Cin%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5E%7B4%7D%7C%7Cx%7C%3CR%2B%5Cepsilon%5C%7D%2C%5Cquad+U_%7BS%7D%3D%5C%7Bx%5Cin%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5E%7B4%7D%7C%7Cx%7C%3ER-%5Cepsilon%5C%7D\" alt=\"U_{N}=\\{x\\in\\mathbb{R}^{4}||x|&lt;R+\\epsilon\\},\\quad U_{S}=\\{x\\in\\mathbb{R}^{4}||x|&gt;R-\\epsilon\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U_%7BN%7D\" alt=\"U_{N}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是平凡流形但 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U_%7BS%7D\" alt=\"U_{S}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 并不是，不过我们可以在无穷远处添加一个时空点并将其视作 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B4%7D\" alt=\"S^{4}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 位形的结果，从而两部分就是通常意义上的南半球与北半球。</p><p>在北半球，令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7BN%7D%3DU%28x%29%5E%7B-1%7DdU%28x%29\" alt=\"A_{N}=U(x)^{-1}dU(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 使得 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A\" alt=\"A\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是一个“纯规范”且在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U_%7BN%7D%5Ccap+U_%7BS%7D\" alt=\"U_{N}\\cap U_{S}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可以被良好定义为纤维丛上的联络。而 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SU%282%29\" alt=\"SU(2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B3%7D\" alt=\"S^{3}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的任一邻域是同胚的，可以定义</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%28x%29%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7Br%7D%28ix%5E%7Bi%7D%5Csigma_%7Bi%7D%2Bx%5E%7B4%7DI_%7B2%5Ctimes2%7D%29\" alt=\"U(x)=\\frac{1}{r}(ix^{i}\\sigma_{i}+x^{4}I_{2\\times2})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>这可以定义赤道上的联络，但对于整个北半球，我们还需要做一些修整，令</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7BN%7D%3Df%28r%29U%28x%29%5E%7B-1%7DdU%28x%29\" alt=\"A_{N}=f(r)U(x)^{-1}dU(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>其中 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%280%29%3D0%2Cf%28%5Cinfty%29%3D1\" alt=\"f(0)=0,f(\\infty)=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。再代入自对偶条件 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%3D%5Cstar+F\" alt=\"F=\\star F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%28r%29%3D%5Cfrac%7Br%5E%7B2%7D%7D%7Br%5E%7B2%7D%2Bc%5E%7B2%7D%7D\" alt=\"f(r)=\\frac{r^{2}}{r^{2}+c^{2}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=c\" alt=\"c\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为一自由参数，可以看做瞬子的“尺度”。</p><p>利用 Stokes 定理，首先可以证明</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cint_%7BS%5E%7B4%7D%7DF%5Cwedge+F%3D-%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B3%7D%5Cint_%7BS%5E%7B3%7D%7DA%5Cwedge+A+%5Cwedge+A\" alt=\"\\int_{S^{4}}F\\wedge F=-\\frac{1}{3}\\int_{S^{3}}A\\wedge A \\wedge A\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>等式右边的积分是对 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B4%7D\" alt=\"S^{4}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的赤道积的，选定规范（比如球坐标规范）后可以得到积分值与球体积 3 形式成正比，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cint_%7BS%5E%7B3%7D%7DA%5Cwedge+A%5Cwedge+A%3D12%5Cint_%7BS%5E%7B3%7D%7D%5Comega\" alt=\"\\int_{S^{3}}A\\wedge A\\wedge A=12\\int_{S^{3}}\\omega\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>从而</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cint_%7BS%5E%7B4%7D%7DF%5Cwedge+F%3D8%5Cpi%5E%7B2%7D\" alt=\"\\int_{S^{4}}F\\wedge F=8\\pi^{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>这是最简单的瞬子解，不难发现这与我们上一节提到的磁单极子的结果是一致的。通过修改 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%28x%29\" alt=\"U(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 我们也可以得到别的瞬子解。比如取 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%28x%29%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7Br%5E%7Bn%7D%7D%28ix%5E%7Bi%7D%5Csigma_%7Bi%7D%2Bx%5E%7B4%7DI_%7B2%5Ctimes+2%7D%29%5E%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"U(x)=\\frac{1}{r^{n}}(ix^{i}\\sigma_{i}+x^{4}I_{2\\times 2})^{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，我们就可以推广之前的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SU%282%29\" alt=\"SU(2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 瞬子解（将赤道“缠绕”了 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=n\" alt=\"n\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 次），相应得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cint_%7BS%5E%7B4%7D%7DF%5Cwedge+F%3D8%5Cpi%5E%7B2%7Dn\" alt=\"\\int_{S^{4}}F\\wedge F=8\\pi^{2}n\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>可以看到在这种情形下 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cint%5C%2CF%5Cwedge+F\" alt=\"\\int\\,F\\wedge F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 度量了某种拓扑结构，或者说给出了瞬子的某种“特征数”，在之后的内容中我们会详细讨论这种特征数的表现及其作用。</p><ul><li><b>Berry 相</b></li></ul><p>现在我们再来考虑一个凝聚态的例子，令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X\" alt=\"X\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为由某些参数决定的位形空间，对于一个与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X\" alt=\"X\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 相关的哈密顿量，假设 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X\" alt=\"X\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 随时间缓慢变化（绝热变化），它的能量本征值可以由 Schrodinger 方程给出：</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H%28X%28t%29%29%7C%5Cpsi%28t%29%5Crangle%3Di%5Cfrac%7Bd%7D%7Bdt%7D%7C%5Cpsi%28t%29%5Crangle\" alt=\"H(X(t))|\\psi(t)\\rangle=i\\frac{d}{dt}|\\psi(t)\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CRightarrow+H%28X%29%7Cn%2CX%5Crangle%3DE_%7Bn%7D%28X%29%7Cn%2CX%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\Rightarrow H(X)|n,X\\rangle=E_{n}(X)|n,X\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>假设 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X\" alt=\"X\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的变化极其微小，不会使得不同本征值 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E_%7Bn%7D%28X%29\" alt=\"E_{n}(X)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 发生简并。那么我们是否能够利用绝热条件的信息构造有效的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cpsi%28t%29%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\psi(t)\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 呢？</p><p>一般来说，指数化 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H%28R%28t%29%29\" alt=\"H(R(t))\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 并将其积分解 Schrodinger 方程即可得到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cpsi%28t%29%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\psi(t)\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，考虑到绝热近似，可以将本征态写为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cpsi%28t%29%5Crangle%5Capprox%5Cexp%7B%5Cleft%28-i%5Cint_%7B0%7D%5E%7Bt%7DE_%7Bn%7D%28X%28s%29%29ds%5Cright%29%7D%7Cn%2CX%28t%29%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\psi(t)\\rangle\\approx\\exp{\\left(-i\\int_{0}^{t}E_{n}(X(s))ds\\right)}|n,X(t)\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>然而这时该结果并不适用，因为求导时态也是含时的，即</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=i%5Cfrac%7Bd%7D%7Bdt%7D%7C%5Cpsi%28t%29%5Crangle%3DE_%7Bn%7D%28X%28t%29%29%7C%5Cpsi%28t%29%5Crangle%2Bi%5Cexp%5Cleft%28-i%5Cint_%7B0%7D%5E%7Bt%7DE_%7Bn%7D%28X%28s%29%29ds%5Cright%29%5Cfrac%7Bd%7D%7Bdt%7D%7Cn%2CX%28t%29%5Crangle\" alt=\"i\\frac{d}{dt}|\\psi(t)\\rangle=E_{n}(X(t))|\\psi(t)\\rangle+i\\exp\\left(-i\\int_{0}^{t}E_{n}(X(s))ds\\right)\\frac{d}{dt}|n,X(t)\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>这个问题在 1984 年由 Berry 提出并做了一些讨论，他在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cpsi%28t%29+%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\psi(t) \\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的构造中添入了一个相位因子 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ceta%28t%29\" alt=\"\\eta(t)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cpsi%28t%29%5Crangle%3D%5Cexp%5Cleft%28i%5Ceta%28t%29-i%5Cint_%7B0%7D%5E%7Bt%7DE_%7Bn%7D%28X%28s%29%29ds%5Cright%29%7Cn%2CX%28t%29%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\psi(t)\\rangle=\\exp\\left(i\\eta(t)-i\\int_{0}^{t}E_{n}(X(s))ds\\right)|n,X(t)\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>在对时间求导时该相位可以得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=0%3D-%5Cfrac%7Bd%5Ceta%28t%29%7D%7Bdt%7D%7C%5Cpsi%28t%29%5Crangle%2Bi%5Cexp%5Cleft%28i%5Ceta%28t%29-i%5Cint_%7B0%7D%5E%7Bt%7DE_%7Bn%7D%28X%28s%29%29ds%5Cright%29%7Cn%2CX%28t%29%5Crangle\" alt=\"0=-\\frac{d\\eta(t)}{dt}|\\psi(t)\\rangle+i\\exp\\left(i\\eta(t)-i\\int_{0}^{t}E_{n}(X(s))ds\\right)|n,X(t)\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>取内积得</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cfrac%7Bd%5Ceta%28t%29%7D%7Bdt%7D%3Di%5Clangle+n%2CX%28t%29%7C%5Cfrac%7Bd%7D%7Bdt%7D%7Cn%2CX%28t%29%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\frac{d\\eta(t)}{dt}=i\\langle n,X(t)|\\frac{d}{dt}|n,X(t)\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>从而</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ceta%28t%29%3Di%5Cint_%7B0%7D%5E%7Bt%7D%5Clangle+n%2CX%28s%29%7C%5Cfrac%7Bd%7D%7Bds%7D%7Cn%2CX%28s%29%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\eta(t)=i\\int_{0}^{t}\\langle n,X(s)|\\frac{d}{ds}|n,X(s)\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CRightarrow+i%5Cint_%7BX%280%29%7D%5E%7BX%28t%29%7D%5Clangle+n%2C+X%7C%5Cfrac%7Bd%7D%7BdX%7D%7Cn%2CX%5Crangle+dX\" alt=\"\\Rightarrow i\\int_{X(0)}^{X(t)}\\langle n, X|\\frac{d}{dX}|n,X\\rangle dX\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>注意该积分结果本身并不是全导数，即使 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X%280%29%3DX%28t%29\" alt=\"X(0)=X(t)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，相位也不会为零。也就是说这一点的相位变化不仅取决于位形空间，也与如何得到某种位形的方式有关。还有一点是，相位因子显然与能级 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=n\" alt=\"n\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是相关的，所以对于一个特定位形，考虑非平凡的拓扑圈时，不同能级将会得到不同的相位，这是一个纯几何或者说纯拓扑引起的相位变化。</p><p>最后我们再用纤维丛的语言来重释一下上述问题。首先对于态 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\psi\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，可以等价的直接附加一个指数相位得到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=e%5E%7Bi%5Cphi%7D%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle\" alt=\"e^{i\\phi}|\\psi\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。即对于态空间而言，某个对称性 (e.g. <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%281%29\" alt=\"U(1)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 丛)下总有更小的底空间 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 满足</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%3D%5C%7B%5Ctextrm%7Bstates%7D%5C%7D%2F%5Csim\" alt=\"M=\\{\\textrm{states}\\}/\\sim\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>在 Berry 相的问题中，我们可以认为系统就是一个 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%281%29\" alt=\"U(1)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 丛（显然是幺正演化的），态 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7Cn%2CX%5Crangle\" alt=\"|n,X\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 即为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%281%29\" alt=\"U(1)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 丛的截面。从而相位即为这个截面上联络的积分：</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Clangle+n%2CX%7C%5Ccdot+d%7Cn%2CX%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\langle n,X|\\cdot d|n,X\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>为了说明 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A\" alt=\"A\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 确实是主 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%281%29\" alt=\"U(1)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 丛的联络，我们需要注意到态矢 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Clangle+n%2CX%7C\" alt=\"\\langle n,X|\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与一般的左矢具有的相位是相反的，也就是说它确实是按照联络定义的方式变换的。</p><p>那么所谓的 Berry 联络对于描述理论有何作用呢？我们在讨论示性类时会详细阐述这种纤维丛语言的威力。实际上对于具体的问题比如 Dirac 磁单极子，系统中允许存在“快”或“慢”的自由度，“快”的自由度可以被积掉，但积掉“快”自由度的代价便是哈密顿量中将出现由协变导数表示的“慢”自由度，该协变导数相应的联络就是 Berry 联络。</p><p>而至于即使在周期性条件下“绕”了一圈也不为零反倒能给出一个“特征数”的拓扑结构，我们将在谈到示性类时详细讨论，对于 Berry 相的问题，所谓的特征数可以是 Chern 数也可以是缠绕数，前者为 Berry 曲率的壳积分而后者为 Berry 规范的边界积分（正如我们在之前对 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B3%7D\" alt=\"S^{3}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 赤道积分的得到的那样），二者本质都是一类特殊的拓扑不变量——示性数。</p><hr/><p>最近事情有点多鸽了挺久，之后慢慢填坑吧，还是有很多新东西想谈的~</p><p>最后代表逢田姐消灭全天下的梨黑(tui)o(≥▽≤o)</p>",
