"<p>喜迎新篇决定换个主题^w^本专题主要阐述基本的代数拓扑以及其在物理中的应用，为了让学数学和学物理的同学都能进行批判性的有效阅读，拓扑专题每一回我都会分两部分来写，第一部分是数学部分，用数学语言阐明代数拓扑的基本观点和结论，第二部分则是物理部分，有针对性的将数学部分的内容与物理模型相联系。数学书我看的很少，所以基本只能抄书了，而且因为这些内容从来没有接触过中文学习材料，有些名词不知道中文怎么说，遇到这些地方我都会标出来的。数学部分主要参考 Bott &amp; Tu <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5E%7B%5B1%5D%7D\" alt=\"^{[1]}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，GTM 139 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5E%7B%5B2%5D%7D\" alt=\"^{[2]}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，物理部分主要参考 Nakahara <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5E%7B%5B3%5D%7D\" alt=\"^{[3]}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><hr/><ul><li><b><i>数学篇：流形上的微积分与（上）同调</i></b></li></ul><p><b>一、微分形式</b></p><p>流形以及矢量丛的内容不再赘述，可见<a href=\"https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/44641601\" class=\"internal\">灰原哀的梨味算符：简介 &amp; 给梨推（hei）的广义相对论（一）</a>。首先从微分形式开始，</p><p>Definition 1: 给定流形 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 及其切丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=TM\" alt=\"TM\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 和余切丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T%5E%7B%2A%7DM\" alt=\"T^{*}M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，存在光滑映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpi%3AT%5E%7B%2A%7DM%5Crightarrow+M\" alt=\"\\pi:T^{*}M\\rightarrow M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，其截面称做 <b>1 形式微分 (differential 1--forms)</b>，有时也称做对偶矢量场。</p><p>Remark 1: 对于某个 1--形式微分 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ctheta\" alt=\"\\theta\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，由定义可知 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ctheta\" alt=\"\\theta\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 使得 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=x%5Cin+M\" alt=\"x\\in M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的点与线性映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7Bx%7DM%5Crightarrow%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"T_{x}M\\rightarrow\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 之间构建了一个映射。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ctheta\" alt=\"\\theta\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可由局域坐标表示为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ctheta%3D%5Csum_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5Ctheta_%7Bi%7D%5E%7B%5Calpha%7D%28x%29dx%5E%7Bi%7D\" alt=\"\\theta=\\sum_{\\alpha}\\theta_{i}^{\\alpha}(x)dx^{i}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Remark 2: 如果改变图册里的某个图为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi_%7B%5Cbeta%7D\" alt=\"\\varphi_{\\beta}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，微分形式之间的变换写为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ctheta_%7Bi%7D%5E%7B%5Cbeta%7D%3D%5Csum_%7Bj%7D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+x_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5E%7Bj%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial+x_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%7D%5Ctheta_%7Bj%7D%5E%7B%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"\\theta_{i}^{\\beta}=\\sum_{j}\\frac{\\partial x_{\\alpha}^{j}}{\\partial x_{\\beta}^{i}}\\theta_{j}^{\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>一般将 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的所有 1--形式微分构成的矢量空间记为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\Omega^{1}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。由此推广，存在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k\" alt=\"k\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 形式微分 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Comega\" alt=\"\\omega\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 使得 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=x%5Cin+M\" alt=\"x\\in M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 映射为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7Bx%7DM\" alt=\"T_{x}M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 中的某个反对称线性 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k\" alt=\"k\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 形式，即 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbigwedge%5E%7Bk%7DT_%7Bx%7D%5E%7B%2A%7DM\" alt=\"\\bigwedge^{k}T_{x}^{*}M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 中的元素。要定义 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Comega\" alt=\"\\omega\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的光滑性我们还需要定义 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbigwedge+T%5E%7B%2A%7DM\" alt=\"\\bigwedge T^{*}M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的流形结构。</p><p>Definition 2: 对于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%5Csubset%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5E%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"U\\subset\\mathbb{R}^{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5C%7Bdx%5E%7Bi_%7B1%7D%7D%5Cwedge%5Ccdots%5Cwedge+dx%5E%7Bi_%7Bk%7D%7D%5C%7D\" alt=\"\\{dx^{i_{1}}\\wedge\\cdots\\wedge dx^{i_{k}}\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbigwedge%5E%7Bk%7DT_%7Bx%7D%5E%7B%2A%7DU\" alt=\"\\bigwedge^{k}T_{x}^{*}U\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的一组基， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k\" alt=\"k\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 形式微分 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Comega\" alt=\"\\omega\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可由局域坐标表示为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Comega%3D%5Csum_%7Bi_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Ci_%7Bk%7D%7D%5Comega_%7Bi_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Ci_%7Bk%7D%7D%5E%7B%5Calpha%7Ddx%5E%7Bi_%7B1%7D%7D%5Cwedge%5Ccdots%5Cwedge+dx%5E%7Bi_%7Bk%7D%7D%2C\" alt=\"\\omega=\\sum_{i_{1},\\cdots,i_{k}}\\omega_{i_{1},\\cdots,i_{k}}^{\\alpha}dx^{i_{1}}\\wedge\\cdots\\wedge dx^{i_{k}},\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>其中 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Comega_%7Bi_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Ci_%7Bk%7D%7D%5E%7B%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"\\omega_{i_{1},\\cdots,i_{k}}^{\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U_%7B%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"U_{\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 中光滑函数的集合，其指标 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=i_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2C+i_%7Bk%7D\" alt=\"i_{1},\\cdots, i_{k}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 遵循反对称性。</p><p>Remark 3: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k\" alt=\"k\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 形式微分变换律为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Comega_%7Bi_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Ci_%7Bk%7D%7D%5E%7B%5Cbeta%7D%3D%5Csum_%7Bj_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Cj_%7Bk%7D%7D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial++x_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5E%7Bj_%7B1%7D%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial+x_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7Bi_%7B1%7D%7D%7D%5Ccdots%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+x_%7B%5Calpha%7D%5E%7Bj_%7Bk%7D%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial+x_%7B%5Cbeta%7D%5E%7Bi_%7Bk%7D%7D%7D%5Comega%5E%7B%5Calpha%7D_%7Bj_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Cj_%7Bk%7D%7D\" alt=\"\\omega_{i_{1},\\cdots,i_{k}}^{\\beta}=\\sum_{j_{1},\\cdots,j_{k}}\\frac{\\partial  x_{\\alpha}^{j_{1}}}{\\partial x_{\\beta}^{i_{1}}}\\cdots\\frac{\\partial x_{\\alpha}^{j_{k}}}{\\partial x_{\\beta}^{i_{k}}}\\omega^{\\alpha}_{j_{1},\\cdots,j_{k}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Properties:</p><ul><li>对于光滑映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%3AM%5Crightarrow+N\" alt=\"f:M\\rightarrow N\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f\" alt=\"f\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可以诱导产生拉回映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%5E%7B%2A%7D%3A%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28N%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"f^{*}:\\Omega^{k}(N)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{k}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，对 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cforall+x%5Cin+M%2CV_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2CV_%7Bk%7D%5Cin+T_%7Bx%7DM\" alt=\"\\forall x\\in M,V_{1},\\cdots,V_{k}\\in T_{x}M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，<img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%5E%7B%2A%7D\" alt=\"f^{*}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 满足 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%5E%7B%2A%7D%5Comega%28x%29%28V_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2CV_%7Bk%7D%29%3A%3D%5Comega%28f%28x%29%29%28T_%7Bx%7Df%28V_%7B1%7D%29%2C%5Ccdots+%2CT_%7Bx%7Df%28V_%7Bk%7D%29%29\" alt=\"f^{*}\\omega(x)(V_{1},\\cdots,V_{k}):=\\omega(f(x))(T_{x}f(V_{1}),\\cdots ,T_{x}f(V_{k}))\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li><li>存在配对（pairing） <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29%5Ctimes%5Cmathfrak%7BX%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%2C%5Cquad%28+%5Ctheta%2CX%29%5Cmapsto%5Ctheta%28X%29\" alt=\"\\Omega^{1}(M)\\times\\mathfrak{X}(M)\\rightarrow\\mathbb{R},\\quad( \\theta,X)\\mapsto\\theta(X)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathfrak%7BX%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\mathfrak{X}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为流形上所有矢量场构成的矢量空间。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%5Cin+C%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"f\\in C^{\\infty}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的全微分表示为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=df%7C_%7BU_%7B%5Calpha%7D%7D%3D%5Csum_%7Bi%7D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+f%7D%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7Bi%7D%7Ddx%5E%7Bi%7D\" alt=\"df|_{U_{\\alpha}}=\\sum_{i}\\frac{\\partial f}{\\partial x^{i}}dx^{i}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=df%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"df\\in\\Omega^{1}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。这时可将 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X%28f%29\" alt=\"X(f)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 改写为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=df%28X%29\" alt=\"df(X)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X%5Cin%5Cmathfrak%7BX%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"X\\in\\mathfrak{X}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%5Comega%7C_%7BU_%7B%5Calpha%7D%7D%3A%3D%5Csum_%7Bi%2Ci_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Ci_%7Bk%7D%7D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%5Comega%5E%7B%5Calpha%7D_%7Bi_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Ci_%7Bk%7D%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7Bi%7D%7Ddx%5E%7Bi%7D%5Cwedge+dx%5E%7Bi_%7B1%7D%7D%5Cwedge%5Ccdots%5Cwedge+dx%5E%7Bi_%7Bk%7D%7D\" alt=\"d\\omega|_{U_{\\alpha}}:=\\sum_{i,i_{1},\\cdots,i_{k}}\\frac{\\partial\\omega^{\\alpha}_{i_{1},\\cdots,i_{k}}}{\\partial x^{i}}dx^{i}\\wedge dx^{i_{1}}\\wedge\\cdots\\wedge dx^{i_{k}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 给定了扩充外微分的算符作用 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%3A%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7Bk%2B1%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"d:\\Omega^{k}(M)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{k+1}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，该算符称为外微分。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbegin%7Balign%7D+d%5Comega%28X_%7B0%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2CX_%7Bk%7D%29%26%3D%5Csum_%7Bi%3D0%7D%5E%7Bp%7D%28-1%29%5E%7Bi%7DX_%7Bi%7D%28%5Comega%28X_%7B0%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2C%5Chat%7BX%7D_%7Bi%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2CX_%7Bk%7D%29%29%5C%5C%26%2B%5Csum_%7Bi%3Cj%7D%28-1%29%5E%7Bi%2Bj%7D%5Comega%28%5BX_%7Bi%7D%2CX_%7Bj%7D%5D%2CX_%7B0%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2C%5Chat%7BX%7D_%7Bi%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2C%5Chat%7BX%7D_%7Bj%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2CX_%7Bk%7D%29%2C+%5Cend%7Balign%7D\" alt=\"\\begin{align} d\\omega(X_{0},\\cdots,X_{k})&amp;=\\sum_{i=0}^{p}(-1)^{i}X_{i}(\\omega(X_{0},\\cdots,\\hat{X}_{i},\\cdots,X_{k}))\\\\&amp;+\\sum_{i&lt;j}(-1)^{i+j}\\omega([X_{i},X_{j}],X_{0},\\cdots,\\hat{X}_{i},\\cdots,\\hat{X}_{j},\\cdots,X_{k}), \\end{align}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </li></ul><p>这里 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Chat%7BX%7D\" alt=\"\\hat{X}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 表示忽略掉该项。由此不难得到对 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cforall%5Comega%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\forall\\omega\\in\\Omega^{k}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，<img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%5E%7B2%7D%5Comega%3D0\" alt=\"d^{2}\\omega=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><ul><li>对任意矢量场 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X%5Cin%5Cmathfrak%7BX%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"X\\in\\mathfrak{X}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 有算符作用 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=i_%7BX%7D%3A%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7Bk-1%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"i_{X}:\\Omega^{k}(M)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{k-1}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 满足 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28i_%7BX%7D%5Comega%29%3A%3D%5Comega%28x%29%28X%2C%5C_%2C%5Ccdots%2C%5C_%29%3A%5Cbigwedge%5E%7Bk-1%7DT_%7Bx%7DM%5Crightarrow%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"(i_{X}\\omega):=\\omega(x)(X,\\_,\\cdots,\\_):\\bigwedge^{k-1}T_{x}M\\rightarrow\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=i_%7BX%7D\" alt=\"i_{X}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 称做内导数（interior product，也有叫contraction 的），显然它与外微分的作用是相反的。</li><li>Cartan 公式： <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7BX%7D%3A%3Di_%7BX%7D%5Ccirc+d%2Bd%5Ccirc+i_%7BX%7D%3A%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"L_{X}:=i_{X}\\circ d+d\\circ i_{X}:\\Omega^{k}(M)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{k}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。这定义了矢量场对 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k\" alt=\"k\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 形式的作用。</li><li>给定了 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d\" alt=\"d\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的微分作用后， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=n\" alt=\"n\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 维流形上 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=n\" alt=\"n\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 形式的积分作用 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cint_%7BM%7D%5Calpha\" alt=\"\\int_{M}\\alpha\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 也能很好的定义了，这时 Stokes 定理改写为</li></ul><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cint_%7BM%7Dd%5Cbeta%3D%5Cint_%7B%5Cpartial+M%7D%5Cbeta%2C%5Cquad%5Cforall%5Cbeta%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7Bk-1%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\int_{M}d\\beta=\\int_{\\partial M}\\beta,\\quad\\forall\\beta\\in\\Omega^{k-1}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>再引入给出流形上微分形式的对偶的 Hodge 算符 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cstar\" alt=\"\\star\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Definition 3: 令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28M%2Cg%29\" alt=\"(M,g)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为具有（伪）Riemann 度规 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g\" alt=\"g\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d\" alt=\"d\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 维光滑流形，存在唯一的线性映射<img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cstar%3A%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7Bd-k%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\star:\\Omega^{k}(M)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{d-k}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/>。称为 Hodge 算符。</p><p>Properties:</p><ul><li>若 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=dx_%7B%5Cmu_%7B1%7D%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2C+dx_%7B%5Cmu_%7Bk%7D%7D\" alt=\"dx_{\\mu_{1}},\\cdots, dx_{\\mu_{k}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为局域基底， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=dx%5E%7B%5Cmu_%7B1%7D%7D%2C%5Ccdots.dx%5E%7B%5Cmu_%7Bk%7D%7D\" alt=\"dx^{\\mu_{1}},\\cdots.dx^{\\mu_{k}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为对偶基底，对任一微分形式 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7Bk%21%7D%5Calpha_%7B%5Cmu_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2C%5Cmu_%7Bk%7D%7Ddx%5E%7B%5Cmu_%7B1%7D%7D%5Cwedge%5Ccdots%5Cwedge+dx%5E%7B%5Cmu_%7Bk%7D%7D\" alt=\"\\alpha=\\frac{1}{k!}\\alpha_{\\mu_{1},\\cdots,\\mu_{k}}dx^{\\mu_{1}}\\wedge\\cdots\\wedge dx^{\\mu_{k}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 有<img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cstar%5Calpha%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7Bk%21%28n-k%29%21%7D%5Cepsilon_%7B%5Cmu_%7B1%7D%5Ccdots%5Cmu_%7Bk%7D%7D%5Csqrt%7B%7C%5Cdet+g%7C%7D%5Calpha_%7B%5Cnu_%7B1%7D%5Ccdots%5Cnu_%7Bk%7D%7Dg%5E%7B%5Cmu_%7B1%7D%5Cnu_%7B1%7D%7D%5Ccdots+g%5E%7B%5Cmu_%7Bk%7D%5Cnu_%7Bk%7D%7Ddx%5E%7B%5Cmu_%7Bk%2B1%7D%7D%5Cwedge%5Ccdots%5Cwedge+dx%5E%7B%5Cmu_%7Bd%7D%7D\" alt=\"\\star\\alpha=\\frac{1}{k!(n-k)!}\\epsilon_{\\mu_{1}\\cdots\\mu_{k}}\\sqrt{|\\det g|}\\alpha_{\\nu_{1}\\cdots\\nu_{k}}g^{\\mu_{1}\\nu_{1}}\\cdots g^{\\mu_{k}\\nu_{k}}dx^{\\mu_{k+1}}\\wedge\\cdots\\wedge dx^{\\mu_{d}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li><li>对于伪 Riemann 流形， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cstar%5E%7B2%7D%3D-%28-1%29%5E%7Bp%28d-p%29%7D\" alt=\"\\star^{2}=-(-1)^{p(d-p)}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28%5Calpha%2C%5Cbeta%29%3D%5Cint_%7BM%7D%5C%2C%5Calpha%5Cwedge%5Cstar%5Cbeta%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7Bk%21%7D%5Cint_%7BM%7D%5C%2C%5Csqrt%7B%7C%5Cdet%7Bg%7D%7C%7D%5Calpha_%7B%5Cmu_%7B1%7D%5Ccdots%5Cmu_%7Bk%7D%7D%5Cbeta%5E%7B%5Cmu_%7B1%7D%5Ccdots%5Cmu_%7Bk%7D%7Dd%5E%7Bk%7Dx\" alt=\"(\\alpha,\\beta)=\\int_{M}\\,\\alpha\\wedge\\star\\beta=\\frac{1}{k!}\\int_{M}\\,\\sqrt{|\\det{g}|}\\alpha_{\\mu_{1}\\cdots\\mu_{k}}\\beta^{\\mu_{1}\\cdots\\mu_{k}}d^{k}x\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 给出了 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k\" alt=\"k\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 形式的内积。</li><li>由微分算符 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d\" alt=\"d\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 Hodge 算符 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cstar\" alt=\"\\star\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可以定义自伴算符 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%5E%7B%5Cdagger%7D%5Cequiv%5Cstar+d%5Cstar%3A%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7Bk-1%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"d^{\\dagger}\\equiv\\star d\\star:\\Omega^{k}(M)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{k-1}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 以及简谐算符 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CDelta%5Cequiv+dd%5E%7B%5Cdagger%7D%2Bd%5E%7B%5Cdagger%7Dd%3A%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\Delta\\equiv dd^{\\dagger}+d^{\\dagger}d:\\Omega^{k}(M)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{k}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。它们的作用我们会在后续的章节详谈。</li></ul><p><b>Special Topic: 复流形上的微积分</b></p><p>如果流形 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 具有复结构，或者说其上的切矢量丛及余切丛有复化，那么 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的微分形式会出现一些额外的结构。考虑 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%5Csubset%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%5E%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"U\\subset\\mathbb{C}^{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，给定坐标 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=z%5E%7Bi%7D%3Dx%5E%7Bi%7D%2B%5Csqrt%7B-1%7Dy%5E%7Bi%7D\" alt=\"z^{i}=x^{i}+\\sqrt{-1}y^{i}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ( <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=i%3D1%2C%5Ccdots%2Cn\" alt=\"i=1,\\cdots,n\" eeimg=\"1\"/> )，切空间 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7Bz%7DU\" alt=\"T_{z}U\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的一组实基底为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5C%7B%5Cpartial%2F%5Cpartial+x%5E%7Bi%7D%2C%5Cpartial%2F%5Cpartial+y%5E%7Bi%7D%5C%7D_%7Bi%3D1%7D%5E%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"\\{\\partial/\\partial x^{i},\\partial/\\partial y^{i}\\}_{i=1}^{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%5E%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{C}^{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上也可以使用复坐标 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28z%5E%7Bi%7D%2C%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%29\" alt=\"(z^{i},\\bar{z}^{i})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，这时可以给定 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7Bz%7DU\" alt=\"T_{z}U\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的一对复基底。</p><p>Definition 4: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%7D%7B%5Cpartial+z%5E%7Bi%7D%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Cleft%28%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%7D%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7Bi%7D%7D-%5Csqrt%7B-1%7D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%7D%7B%5Cpartial+y%5E%7Bi%7D%7D%5Cright%29%2C%5Cquad%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%7D%7B%5Cpartial%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Cleft%28%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%7D%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7Bi%7D%7D%2B%5Csqrt%7B-1%7D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%7D%7B%5Cpartial+y%5E%7Bi%7D%7D%5Cright%29\" alt=\"\\frac{\\partial}{\\partial z^{i}}=\\frac{1}{2}\\left(\\frac{\\partial}{\\partial x^{i}}-\\sqrt{-1}\\frac{\\partial}{\\partial y^{i}}\\right),\\quad\\frac{\\partial}{\\partial\\bar{z}^{i}}=\\frac{1}{2}\\left(\\frac{\\partial}{\\partial x^{i}}+\\sqrt{-1}\\frac{\\partial}{\\partial y^{i}}\\right)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为局域集合 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%5Csubset%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%5E%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"U\\subset\\mathbb{C}^{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上切空间 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7Bz%7DU\" alt=\"T_{z}U\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的一组复基底。一般定义 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=i%5Cequiv%5Csqrt%7B-1%7D\" alt=\"i\\equiv\\sqrt{-1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。复切空间可以定义为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7Bz%7D%5E%7B%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%7DU%3D%5Ctextrm%7Bspan%7D_%7B%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%7D%5C%7B%5Cpartial%2F%5Cpartial+z%5E%7Bi%7D%2C%5Cpartial%2F%5Cpartial%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%2Ci%3D1%2C%5Ccdots%2Cn%5C%7D\" alt=\"T_{z}^{\\mathbb{C}}U=\\textrm{span}_{\\mathbb{C}}\\{\\partial/\\partial z^{i},\\partial/\\partial\\bar{z}^{i},i=1,\\cdots,n\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>从而也可以定义复切丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T%5E%7B%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%7DM\" alt=\"T^{\\mathbb{C}}M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>由上可知 Cauchy--Riemann 方程可写为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+f%7D%7B%5Cpartial%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%7D%3D0\" alt=\"\\frac{\\partial f}{\\partial\\bar{z}}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。由定义知，复流形的转变函数(transition function) <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvarphi%3Az%5E%7Bi%7D%5Cmapsto+w%5E%7Bi%7D%28z%5E%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Cz%5E%7Bn%7D%29\" alt=\"\\varphi:z^{i}\\mapsto w^{i}(z^{1},\\cdots,z^{n})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 总是全纯的，故 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+w%7D%7B%5Cpartial%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%7D%3D0\" alt=\"\\frac{\\partial w}{\\partial\\bar{z}^{i}}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。从而</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7Bz%7D%5Cvarphi%5Cleft%28%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%7D%7B%5Cpartial+z%5E%7Bi%7D%7D%5Cright%29%3D%5Csum_%7Bj%3D1%7D%5E%7Bn%7D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+w%5E%7Bj%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial+z%5E%7Bi%7D%7D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%7D%7B%5Cpartial+w%5E%7Bj%7D%7D%2C%5Cquad+T_%7Bz%7D%5Cvarphi%5Cleft%28%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%7D%7B%5Cpartial%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%7D%5Cright%29%3D%5Csum_%7Bj%3D1%7D%5E%7Bn%7D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%5Cbar%7Bw%7D%5E%7Bj%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%7D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%7D%7B%5Cpartial%5Cbar%7Bw%7D%5E%7Bj%7D%7D\" alt=\"T_{z}\\varphi\\left(\\frac{\\partial}{\\partial z^{i}}\\right)=\\sum_{j=1}^{n}\\frac{\\partial w^{j}}{\\partial z^{i}}\\frac{\\partial}{\\partial w^{j}},\\quad T_{z}\\varphi\\left(\\frac{\\partial}{\\partial\\bar{z}^{i}}\\right)=\\sum_{j=1}^{n}\\frac{\\partial\\bar{w}^{j}}{\\partial\\bar{z}^{i}}\\frac{\\partial}{\\partial\\bar{w}^{j}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>由此可以看出复切丛 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T%5E%7B%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%7DM\" alt=\"T^{\\mathbb{C}}M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的转变函数具有如下形式</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cleft%28%5Cbegin%7Barray%7D%7Bcc%7D+%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+w%5E%7Bj%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial+z%5E%7Bi%7D%7D+%26+0%5C%5C+0+%26+%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%5Cbar%7Bw%7D%5E%7Bj%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%7D+%5Cend%7Barray%7D%5Cright%29\" alt=\"\\left(\\begin{array}{cc} \\frac{\\partial w^{j}}{\\partial z^{i}} &amp; 0\\\\ 0 &amp; \\frac{\\partial\\bar{w}^{j}}{\\partial\\bar{z}^{i}} \\end{array}\\right)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>所以复切丛可以分解为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T%5E%7B%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%7DM%3DT%5E%7B%281%2C0%29%7DM%5Coplus+T%5E%7B%280%2C1%29%7DM\" alt=\"T^{\\mathbb{C}}M=T^{(1,0)}M\\oplus T^{(0,1)}M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，即分别由 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial%2F%5Cpartial+z%5E%7Bi%7D\" alt=\"\\partial/\\partial z^{i}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial%2F%5Cpartial%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bi%7D\" alt=\"\\partial/\\partial\\bar{z}^{i}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为基分解。与之对应的，复微分 1 形式空间可以分解为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D_%7B%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%7D%28M%29%3D%5COmega%5E%7B%281%2C0%29%7D%28M%29%5Coplus%5COmega%5E%7B%280%2C1%29%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\Omega^{1}_{\\mathbb{C}}(M)=\\Omega^{(1,0)}(M)\\oplus\\Omega^{(0,1)}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>其中对于任意 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7B%281%2C0%29%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\alpha\\in\\Omega^{(1,0)}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可以写为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha%3D%5Csum_%7Bi%7D%5Calpha_%7Bi%7D%28z%2C%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%29dz%5E%7Bi%7D\" alt=\"\\alpha=\\sum_{i}\\alpha_{i}(z,\\bar{z})dz^{i}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，任意 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbeta%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7B%280%2C1%29%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\beta\\in\\Omega^{(0,1)}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可以写为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbeta%3D%5Csum_%7Bi%7D%5Cbeta_%7Bi%7D%28z%2C%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%29d%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bi%7D\" alt=\"\\beta=\\sum_{i}\\beta_{i}(z,\\bar{z})d\\bar{z}^{i}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。很容易推广到更高阶的微分形式，这里不加证明的写出结果</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D_%7B%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D%7D%28M%29%3D%5Cbigoplus_%7Bp%2Bq%3Dk%7D%5COmega%5E%7B%28p%2Cq%29%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\Omega^{k}_{\\mathbb{C}}(M)=\\bigoplus_{p+q=k}\\Omega^{(p,q)}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>在全纯坐标系 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=z%3D%28z%5E%7B1%7D%2Cz%5E%7B2%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Cz%5E%7Bn%7D%29\" alt=\"z=(z^{1},z^{2},\\cdots,z^{n})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 表示下，对于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7B%28p%2Cq%29%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\alpha\\in\\Omega^{(p,q)}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，我们有</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha%3D%5Csum_%7Bi_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Ci_%7Bp%7D%2Cj_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Cj_%7Bq%7D%7D%28z%2C%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%29dz%5E%7Bi_%7B1%7D%7D%5Cwedge%5Ccdots%5Cwedge+dz%5E%7Bi_%7Bp%7D%7D%5Cwedge+d%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bj_%7B1%7D%7D%5Cwedge%5Ccdots%5Cwedge+d%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bj_%7Bq%7D%7D\" alt=\"\\alpha=\\sum_{i_{1},\\cdots,i_{p},j_{1},\\cdots,j_{q}}(z,\\bar{z})dz^{i_{1}}\\wedge\\cdots\\wedge dz^{i_{p}}\\wedge d\\bar{z}^{j_{1}}\\wedge\\cdots\\wedge d\\bar{z}^{j_{q}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>外微分则为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%5Calpha%3D%5Csum_%7Bi%2Ci_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Ci_%7Bp%7D%2Cj_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Cj_%7Bq%7D%7D%5Cleft%28%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%5Calpha_%7Bi_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Ci_%7Bp%7D%2Cj_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Cj_%7Bq%7D%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial+z%5E%7Bi%7D%7Ddz%5E%7Bi%7D%2B%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%5Calpha_%7Bi_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Ci_%7Bp%7D%2Cj_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Cj_%7Bq%7D%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bj%7D%7Dd%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%5Cright%29%5Cwedge+dz%5E%7Bi_%7B1%7D%7D%5Cwedge%5Ccdots%5Cwedge+dz%5E%7Bi_%7Bp%7D%7D%5Cwedge+d%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bj_%7B1%7D%7D%5Cwedge%5Ccdots%5Cwedge+d%5Cbar%7Bz%7D%5E%7Bj_%7Bq%7D%7D\" alt=\"d\\alpha=\\sum_{i,i_{1},\\cdots,i_{p},j_{1},\\cdots,j_{q}}\\left(\\frac{\\partial\\alpha_{i_{1},\\cdots,i_{p},j_{1},\\cdots,j_{q}}}{\\partial z^{i}}dz^{i}+\\frac{\\partial\\alpha_{i_{1},\\cdots,i_{p},j_{1},\\cdots,j_{q}}}{\\partial\\bar{z}^{j}}d\\bar{z}^{i}\\right)\\wedge dz^{i_{1}}\\wedge\\cdots\\wedge dz^{i_{p}}\\wedge d\\bar{z}^{j_{1}}\\wedge\\cdots\\wedge d\\bar{z}^{j_{q}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>即d= <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%3D%5Cpartial%2B%5Cbar%7B%5Cpartial%7D\" alt=\"d=\\partial+\\bar{\\partial}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial%3A%5COmega%5E%7B%28p%2Cq%29%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7B%28p%2B1%2Cq%29%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\partial:\\Omega^{(p,q)}(M)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{(p+1,q)}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbar%7B%5Cpartial%7D%3A%5COmega%5E%7B%28p%2Cq%29%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7B%28p%2Cq%2B1%29%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\bar{\\partial}:\\Omega^{(p,q)}(M)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{(p,q+1)}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。这时 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%5E%7B2%7D%3D0\" alt=\"d^{2}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 衍生为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial%5E%7B2%7D%3D%5Cbar%7B%5Cpartial%7D%5E%7B2%7D%3D0\" alt=\"\\partial^{2}=\\bar{\\partial}^{2}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial%5Cbar%7B%5Cpartial%7D%2B%5Cbar%7B%5Cpartial%7D%5Cpartial%3D0\" alt=\"\\partial\\bar{\\partial}+\\bar{\\partial}\\partial=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p><b>二、De Rham 复形与（上）同调流形</b></p><p>现在考虑微分形式与外微分的系统：</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=C%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bd%7D%5Chookrightarrow%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bd%7D%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7B2%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bd%7D%5Crightarrow%5Ccdots\" alt=\"C^{\\infty}(M)\\stackrel{d}\\hookrightarrow\\Omega^{1}(M)\\stackrel{d}\\rightarrow\\Omega^{2}(M)\\stackrel{d}\\rightarrow\\cdots\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\alpha\\in\\Omega^{k}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%5Calpha%3D0\" alt=\"d\\alpha=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的微分形式（由 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%5E%7B2%7D%3D0\" alt=\"d^{2}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 保证），也称做<b>闭形式(closed form)</b>，如果存在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbeta%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7Bk-1%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\beta\\in\\Omega^{k-1}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 满足 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%5Cbeta%3D%5Calpha\" alt=\"d\\beta=\\alpha\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，那么 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha\" alt=\"\\alpha\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 称为<b>恰当形式(exact form)</b>。</p><p>Property: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%5E%7B2%7D%3D0\" alt=\"d^{2}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 保证了如果一微分形式恰当，那么它一定是闭的。但闭不一定恰当。</p><p>这条性质体现出微分形式的链是一类<b>上链复形(cochain complex)</b>，有</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=Img%5C%7Bd%3A%5COmega%5E%7Bk-1%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%5C%7D%5Csubset+Ker%5C%7Bd%3A%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7Bk%2B1%7D%28M%29%5C%7D\" alt=\"Img\\{d:\\Omega^{k-1}(M)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{k}(M)\\}\\subset Ker\\{d:\\Omega^{k}(M)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{k+1}(M)\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Definition 5: 给定流形 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，可以定义一类描述闭形式与恰当形式之间联系的群</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%3A%3DKer%5C%7Bd%3A%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7Bk%2B1%7D%28M%29%5C%7D%2FImg%5C%7Bd%3A%5COmega%5E%7Bk-1%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%5C%7D\" alt=\"H_{dR}^{k}(M):=Ker\\{d:\\Omega^{k}(M)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{k+1}(M)\\}/Img\\{d:\\Omega^{k-1}(M)\\rightarrow\\Omega^{k}(M)\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>该群具有上链结构，称做 de Rham 上同调群。</p><p>Properties:</p><ul><li>分配(assignment，这个我是真不知道怎么用中文说) <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%5Cmapsto+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B%5Cbullet%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"M\\mapsto H_{dR}^{\\bullet}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 对应（阶化）矢量空间到一流形的映射。</li><li>楔积可以诱导乘法 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cwedge%3AH_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bp%7D%28M%29%5Ctimes+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bq%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bp%2Bq%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\wedge:H_{dR}^{p}(M)\\times H_{dR}^{q}(M)\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{p+q}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> （因为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%28%5Calpha%5Cwedge%5Cbeta%29%3Dd%5Calpha%5Cwedge%5Cbeta%2B%28-1%29%5E%7B%7C%5Calpha%7C%7D%5Calpha%5Cwedge+d%5Cbeta\" alt=\"d(\\alpha\\wedge\\beta)=d\\alpha\\wedge\\beta+(-1)^{|\\alpha|}\\alpha\\wedge d\\beta\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ）。</li><li>微分形式的拉回与外微分是可兼容的（ <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%5E%7B%2A%7Dd%5Calpha%3Ddf%5E%7B%2A%7D%5Calpha%5Cquad%5Cforall%5Calpha%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7Bk%7D%28N%29\" alt=\"f^{*}d\\alpha=df^{*}\\alpha\\quad\\forall\\alpha\\in\\Omega^{k}(N)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ），所以由光滑映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%3AM%5Crightarrow+N\" alt=\"f:M\\rightarrow N\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可以诱导映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%5E%7B%2A%7D%3AH_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B%5Cbullet%7D%28N%29%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B%5Cbullet%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"f^{*}:H_{dR}^{\\bullet}(N)\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{\\bullet}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/>。此映射亦与楔积可兼容。</li><li>Theorem 1: 令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B0%7D\" alt=\"f_{0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B1%7D%3AM%5Crightarrow+N\" alt=\"f_{1}:M\\rightarrow N\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为两个光滑同伦的光滑映射。在 de Rham 上同调群的观点下它们诱导生成的映射是相同的，即 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Bf_%7B0%7D%5E%7B%2A%7D%5D%3D%5Bf_%7B1%7D%5E%7B%2A%7D%5D%3AH_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B%5Cbullet%7D%28N%29%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B%5Cbullet%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"[f_{0}^{*}]=[f_{1}^{*}]:H_{dR}^{\\bullet}(N)\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{\\bullet}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。该定理称做 <b>de Rham 上同调同伦不变性定理(Homotopy invariance of de Rham cohomology)</b>。证略，详见 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5E%7B%5B2%5D%7D\" alt=\"^{[2]}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li></ul><p>由 theorem 1 出发可以得到一条很有用的推论。</p><p>Definition 6: 给定定义域 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%5Cin%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5E%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"U\\in\\mathbb{R}^{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，若存在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=x_%7B0%7D%5Cin+U\" alt=\"x_{0}\\in U\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 使得除 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=x_%7B0%7D\" alt=\"x_{0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 外任意其他点 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=x%5Cin+U\" alt=\"x\\in U\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，它们之间的连线 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=tx%2B%281-t%29x_%7B0%7D\" alt=\"tx+(1-t)x_{0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 都在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U\" alt=\"U\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 内。那么 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U\" alt=\"U\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 称做星形域(star-shaped domain)。也可以看做局域的单连通区域。</p><p>Remark 4: 单连通区域一定是星形域。反之不然。</p><p>Example 1: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5E%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{R}^{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为一星形域。</p><p>Corollary 1: 令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%5Csubset%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5E%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"U\\subset\\mathbb{R}^{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为一星形域。则</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B%5Cbullet%7D%28U%29%3D%5C%7B%5Cbegin%7Barray%7D%7Bc%7D+%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5Cquad%5Cbullet%3D0%5C%5C+0%5Cquad%5Cbullet%3E0+%5Cend%7Barray%7D\" alt=\"H_{dR}^{\\bullet}(U)=\\{\\begin{array}{c} \\mathbb{R}\\quad\\bullet=0\\\\ 0\\quad\\bullet&gt;0 \\end{array}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>称做 Poincare 引理。即如果 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U\" alt=\"U\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是星形域，任意闭形式均是恰当的。这说明对于一流形 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，其上的局域非零阶微分形式总是闭且恰当的。</p><p>上述定义也可以对单纯形(simplex)定义，这时微分算符 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial%3AS_%7Bk%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow+S_%7Bk-1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\partial:S_{k}^{\\infty}(M)\\rightarrow S_{k-1}^{\\infty}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 描述的是单纯形截面到边界面的映射，同样有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial%5E%7B2%7D%3D0\" alt=\"\\partial^{2}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，但这时体系是链复形，核与像间的关系由同调群</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H_%7Bk%7D%5E%7B%5Ctextrm%7Bsing%7D%7D%28M%2C%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%29%3A%3DKer%5C%7B%5Cpartial%3A+S_%7Bk%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow+S_%7Bk-1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%29%5C%7D%2FImg%5C%7B%5Cpartial%3AS_%7Bk%2B1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow+S_%7Bk%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%29%5C%7D\" alt=\"H_{k}^{\\textrm{sing}}(M,\\mathbb{R}):=Ker\\{\\partial: S_{k}^{\\infty}(M)\\rightarrow S_{k-1}^{\\infty}(M)\\}/Img\\{\\partial:S_{k+1}^{\\infty}(M)\\rightarrow S_{k}^{\\infty}(M)\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>给出。其余的基本性质与上同调群类似，上同调群与同调群当然是存在一些深刻的联系的，之后我们会阐述与其相关的一条重要定理。</p><p>如果想要从单纯形的链复形结构出发得到上链复形，需要考虑链复形的对偶， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S_%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%3A%3D%5Ctextrm%7BHom%7D_%7B%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%7D%28S_%7Bk%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%29%2C%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%29\" alt=\"S_{\\infty}^{k}(M):=\\textrm{Hom}_{\\mathbb{R}}(S_{k}^{\\infty}(M),\\mathbb{R})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。这样与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial\" alt=\"\\partial\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 对偶的微分算符就具有升高微分形式阶数的能力，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%3AS_%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow+S_%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7Bk%2B1%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"d:S_{\\infty}^{k}(M)\\rightarrow S_{\\infty}^{k+1}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%5Cvarphi%28%5Csigma%29%3A%3D%5Cvarphi%28%5Cpartial%5Csigma%29%2C%5Cquad%5Cvarphi%5Cin+S_%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%2C%5Csigma%5Cin+S_%7Bk%2B1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"d\\varphi(\\sigma):=\\varphi(\\partial\\sigma),\\quad\\varphi\\in S_{\\infty}^{k}(M),\\sigma\\in S_{k+1}^{\\infty}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>显然 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%5E%7B2%7D%3D0\" alt=\"d^{2}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。从而得到了单纯形的上链复形及其上同调群</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H_%7B%5Ctextrm%7Bsing%7D%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%2C%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%29%3A%3DKer%5C%7Bd%3AS_%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow+S_%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7Bk%2B1%7D%28M%29%5C%7D%2FImg%5C%7Bd%3AS_%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7Bk-1%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow+S_%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28M%29%5C%7D\" alt=\"H_{\\textrm{sing}}^{k}(M,\\mathbb{R}):=Ker\\{d:S_{\\infty}^{k}(M)\\rightarrow S_{\\infty}^{k+1}(M)\\}/Img\\{d:S_{\\infty}^{k-1}(M)\\rightarrow S_{\\infty}^{k}(M)\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>给定 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k\" alt=\"k\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 形式与光滑 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k\" alt=\"k\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 阶单纯形 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Csigma%3A%5CDelta%5E%7Bk%7D%5Crightarrow+M\" alt=\"\\sigma:\\Delta^{k}\\rightarrow M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，可以定义内积</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Clangle%5Calpha%2C%5Csigma%5Crangle%3A%3D%5Cint_%7B%5CDelta%5E%7Bk%7D%7D%5C%2C%5Csigma%5E%7B%2A%7D%5Calpha\" alt=\"\\langle\\alpha,\\sigma\\rangle:=\\int_{\\Delta^{k}}\\,\\sigma^{*}\\alpha\" eeimg=\"1\"/>   (1)。</p><p>需要注意要求单纯形光滑是很重要的条件，这是为了保证拉回映射使微分形式能够拉回到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CDelta%5E%7Bk%7D\" alt=\"\\Delta^{k}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。由 Stokes 定理不难得到：</p><p>Lemma 1: 对 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7Bk-1%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\alpha\\in\\Omega^{k-1}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Csigma%5Cin+S_%7Bk%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\sigma\\in S_{k}^{\\infty}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Clangle+d%5Calpha%2C%5Csigma%5Crangle%3D%5Clangle%5Calpha%2C%5Cpartial%5Csigma%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\langle d\\alpha,\\sigma\\rangle=\\langle\\alpha,\\partial\\sigma\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>从而 (1) 可以由映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CPsi%3A%5COmega%5E%7B%5Cbullet%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow+S_%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7B%5Cbullet%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\Psi:\\Omega^{\\bullet}(M)\\rightarrow S_{\\infty}^{\\bullet}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 描述， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CPsi\" alt=\"\\Psi\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 满足 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CPsi%5Ccirc+d%3Dd%5Ccirc%5CPsi\" alt=\"\\Psi\\circ d=d\\circ\\Psi\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。这样的映射称做上链复形的<b>态射(morphism)</b>。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CPsi\" alt=\"\\Psi\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可以诱导得到上同调群的映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5B%5CPsi%5D%3AH_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B%5Cbullet%7D%28M%29%5Crightarrow+H%5E%7B%5Cbullet%7D_%7B%5Ctextrm%7Bsing%7D%7D%28M%2C%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%29\" alt=\"[\\Psi]:H_{dR}^{\\bullet}(M)\\rightarrow H^{\\bullet}_{\\textrm{sing}}(M,\\mathbb{R})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Theorem 2: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5B%5CPsi%5D\" alt=\"[\\Psi]\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为同构映射。这便是著名的<b> de Rham 定理</b>。</p><p>这里不赘述其证明，几乎任何一本有关代数拓扑或者上同调的书都一定会写的。这里只介绍在证明过程中会用到的一个重要定理，它也是 de Rham 上同调的核心性质之一。</p><p>Definition 7: 具有为零的上同调群的复形称为<b>恰当序列(exact sequence或long exact sequence)</b>。</p><p>Theorem 3: 假设 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%3DU%5Ccup+V\" alt=\"M=U\\cup V\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为存在两个开子集 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U\" alt=\"U\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V\" alt=\"V\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的流形。其上存在恰当序列</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ccdots%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28U%5Ccup+V%29%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28U%29%5Coplus+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28V%29%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28U%5Ccup+V%29%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bk%2B1%7D%28U%5Ccup+V%29%5Crightarrow%5Ccdots\" alt=\"\\cdots\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{k}(U\\cup V)\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{k}(U)\\oplus H_{dR}^{k}(V)\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{k}(U\\cup V)\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{k+1}(U\\cup V)\\rightarrow\\cdots\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。该定理称为<b> Mayer--Vietoris 定理</b>。</p><p>Theorem 3 的证明是很简单的，在两个开子集内部分别定义一个微分形式再证明它们在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%5Ccap+V\" alt=\"U\\cap V\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 边界上为零即可（亦即证明了两个微分形式在边界上&#34;粘接&#34;为一个闭形式），证明该序列恰当也是一样的思路，但要分别证明一一及到上。</p><p>de Rham 上同调定理说明奇异上同调 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H_%7B%5Ctextrm%7Bsing%7D%7D%5E%7B%5Cbullet%7D%28M%2C%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%29\" alt=\"H_{\\textrm{sing}}^{\\bullet}(M,\\mathbb{R})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 de Rham 上同调 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B%5Cbullet%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"H_{dR}^{\\bullet}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 满足相同的性质：泛函性，同伦不变性以及 Mayer--Vietoris 序列的存在性。所以如果在流形上选取一个局域单连通的开覆盖，定理的证明即化为证明该开覆盖的 de Rham 同构性，这由 Poincare 引理便可得到，详细证明可见 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5E%7B%5B2%5D%7D\" alt=\"^{[2]}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Remark 5: 回到 Definition 4 的 Properties，de Rham 定理也说明了上同调群即底拓扑空间的<b>拓扑不变量</b>。从范畴论的观点来看，Properties 的前三条也可以描述为：de Rham 上同调定义了一个逆变函子(contravariant functor) <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathfrak%7Bf%7D\" alt=\"\\mathfrak{f}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 满足 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathfrak%7Bf%7D%3A\" alt=\"\\mathfrak{f}:\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 光滑流形（具有光滑映射得到的态射）的范畴 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Crightarrow\" alt=\"\\rightarrow\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 阶化代数的范畴。</p><p>Example 2: Theorem 3 在代数拓扑的计算上是很有用的，以（实）射影平面为例，de Rham 上同调给定如下恰当序列</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ccdots%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BP%7D%5E%7Bn%7D%29%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BP%7D%5E%7Bn-1%7D%29%5Crightarrow+H%5E%7Bk%7D_%7BdR%7D%28S%5E%7B2n-1%7D%29%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bk%2B1%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BP%7D%5E%7Bn%7D%29%5Crightarrow%5Ccdots\" alt=\"\\cdots\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{k}(\\mathbb{P}^{n})\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{k}(\\mathbb{P}^{n-1})\\rightarrow H^{k}_{dR}(S^{2n-1})\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{k+1}(\\mathbb{P}^{n})\\rightarrow\\cdots\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>由于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28S%5E%7B2n-1%7D%29%3D0\" alt=\"H_{dR}^{k}(S^{2n-1})=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cforall+k%5Cneq2n-1\" alt=\"\\forall k\\neq2n-1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 且 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B2n-1%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BP%7D%5E%7Bn-1%7D%29%3D0\" alt=\"H_{dR}^{2n-1}(\\mathbb{P}^{n-1})=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。上述序列破缺为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=0%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BP%7D%5E%7Bn%7D%29%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BP%7D%5E%7Bn-1%7D%29%5Crightarrow0%5C+%5Cforall+k%3C2n-1\" alt=\"0\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{k}(\\mathbb{P}^{n})\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{k}(\\mathbb{P}^{n-1})\\rightarrow0\\ \\forall k&lt;2n-1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=0%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B2n-1%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BP%7D%5E%7Bn-1%7D%29%5Crightarrow0\" alt=\"0\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{2n-1}(\\mathbb{P}^{n-1})\\rightarrow0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=0%5Crightarrow%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B2n%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BP%7D%5E%7Bn%7D%29%5Crightarrow0\" alt=\"0\\rightarrow\\mathbb{R}\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{2n}(\\mathbb{P}^{n})\\rightarrow0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>从而 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%28%5Cmathbb%7BP%7D%5E%7Bn%7D%29%3D%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%280%29%5C+%5Cforall+k%3D\" alt=\"H_{dR}^{k}(\\mathbb{P}^{n})=\\mathbb{R}(0)\\ \\forall k=\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 偶数（奇数） <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%280%5Cleq+k%5Cleq+2n%29\" alt=\"(0\\leq k\\leq 2n)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><hr/><ul><li><b><i>物理篇：电磁场、规范场及 Yang--Mills 场</i></b></li></ul><p><b>一、电磁场的微分形式</b></p><p>首先从 Maxwell 的电动力学出发，我们都知道 Maxwell 方程组可以用张量形式写为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7DF%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%3Dj%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D\" alt=\"\\partial_{\\mu}F^{\\mu\\nu}=j^{\\nu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D+%5Ctilde%7BF%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%3D0\" alt=\"\\partial_{\\mu} \\tilde{F}^{\\mu\\nu}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>这里 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%3D%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7DA_%7B%5Cnu%7D-%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cnu%7DA_%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"F^{\\mu\\nu}=\\partial_{\\mu}A_{\\nu}-\\partial_{\\nu}A_{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为一个反对称的二阶张量（从场论观点来看就是场强），而 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ctilde%7BF%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Cepsilon_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%5Clambda%5Crho%7DF%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D\" alt=\"\\tilde{F}^{\\mu\\nu}=\\frac{1}{2}\\epsilon_{\\mu\\nu\\lambda\\rho}F^{\\mu\\nu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为其对偶张量， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D\" alt=\"F^{\\mu\\nu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可由电场强度 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"E^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与磁感应强度 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=B%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"B^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 表示为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%3D%5Cleft%28%5Cbegin%7Barray%7D%7Bcccc%7D+0+%26+E%5E%7Bx%7D%26E%5E%7By%7D%26E%5E%7Bz%7D%5C%5C+-E%5E%7Bx%7D%260%26-B%5E%7Bz%7D%26B%5E%7By%7D%5C%5C+-E%5E%7By%7D%26B%5E%7Bz%7D%260%26-B%5E%7Bx%7D%5C%5C+-E%5E%7Bz%7D%26-B%5E%7By%7D%26B%5E%7Bx%7D%260+%5Cend%7Barray%7D+%5Cright%29\" alt=\"F^{\\mu\\nu}=\\left(\\begin{array}{cccc} 0 &amp; E^{x}&amp;E^{y}&amp;E^{z}\\\\ -E^{x}&amp;0&amp;-B^{z}&amp;B^{y}\\\\ -E^{y}&amp;B^{z}&amp;0&amp;-B^{x}\\\\ -E^{z}&amp;-B^{y}&amp;B^{x}&amp;0 \\end{array} \\right)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>从而 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%3DF_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7Ddx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cwedge+dx%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D\" alt=\"F=F_{\\mu\\nu}dx^{\\mu}\\wedge dx^{\\nu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 就是一个 2 形式张量，同时 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=dx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cwedge+dx%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%3D-+dx%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%5Cwedge+dx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"dx^{\\mu}\\wedge dx^{\\nu}=- dx^{\\nu}\\wedge dx^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的反对称构造保证了该微分形式的构造是自然的，没有隐藏任何信息的。对于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=dx%5Cwedge+dy%5Cwedge+dz\" alt=\"dx\\wedge dy\\wedge dz\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的 3 形式，不难发现</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla%5Ccdot+E%3D%5Crho\" alt=\"\\nabla\\cdot E=\\rho\" eeimg=\"1\"/><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28dF%29_%7Bxyz%7D%3D%5Cpartial_%7Bx%7DF_%7Byz%7D%2B%5Cpartial_%7By%7DF_%7Bzx%7D%2B%5Cpartial_%7Bz%7DF_%7Bxy%7D%3D-%5Cpartial_%7Bx%7DB%5E%7Bx%7D-%5Cpartial_%7By%7DB%5E%7By%7D-%5Cpartial_%7Bz%7DB%5E%7Bz%7D%3D-%5Cnabla%5Ccdot+B%3D0\" alt=\"(dF)_{xyz}=\\partial_{x}F_{yz}+\\partial_{y}F_{zx}+\\partial_{z}F_{xy}=-\\partial_{x}B^{x}-\\partial_{y}B^{y}-\\partial_{z}B^{z}=-\\nabla\\cdot B=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28dF%29_%7Btxy%7D%3D%5Cpartial_%7Bt%7DF_%7Bxy%7D%2B%5Cpartial_%7Bx%7DF_%7Byt%7D%2B%5Cpartial_%7By%7DF_%7Btx%7D%3D-%5Cpartial_%7Bt%7DB%5E%7Bz%7D-%5Cpartial_%7Bx%7DE%5E%7By%7D%2B%5Cpartial_%7By%7DE%5E%7Bx%7D%3D%28%5Cpartial_%7Bt%7DB%2B%5Cnabla%5Ctimes+E%29_%7Bz%7D%3D0\" alt=\"(dF)_{txy}=\\partial_{t}F_{xy}+\\partial_{x}F_{yt}+\\partial_{y}F_{tx}=-\\partial_{t}B^{z}-\\partial_{x}E^{y}+\\partial_{y}E^{x}=(\\partial_{t}B+\\nabla\\times E)_{z}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>剩下的也与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28dF%29_%7Btxy%7D\" alt=\"(dF)_{txy}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 结果相似，即无源 Maxwell 方程可以由微分形式写为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=dF%3D0\" alt=\"dF=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>无源方程的微分形式与时空流形 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上坐标的选取是无关的，这保证了 2 形式的外导数自动为零（ <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%5E%7B2%7D%3D0\" alt=\"d^{2}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ）。</p><p>而对于有源 Maxwell 方程 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla%5Ccdot+E%3D%5Crho\" alt=\"\\nabla\\cdot E=\\rho\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cnabla%5Ctimes+B-%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+E%7D%7B%5Cpartial+t%7D%3Dj\" alt=\"\\nabla\\times B-\\frac{\\partial E}{\\partial t}=j\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，由于背景荷的存在，我们也需要将四维电流密度 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=j%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"j^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 写为微分形式，利用 Hodge 对偶可以将上述方程改写为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=d%5Cstar+F%3D%5Cstar+j\" alt=\"d\\star F=\\star j\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>注意这里 Hodge 符号的出现意味着该方程是与时空度规有关的。换句话说，无论 Maxwell 方程组的显式形式依赖于何种坐标， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F\" alt=\"F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cstar+F\" alt=\"\\star F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 之间的关系仅由度规的选取决定。</p><p>将方程组写成微分形式除了紧凑优雅的功能性外，还有一点很重要的便是微分形式能够更清晰地告诉我们系统的几何或拓扑性质。，对于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=dF%3D0\" alt=\"dF=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，我们知道 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F\" alt=\"F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是闭的 2 形式，如果考虑时空流形平坦（i.e. Minkowski 时空），那么 Poincare 引理意味着 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F\" alt=\"F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 也一定是恰当的，即</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%3DdA\" alt=\"F=dA\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%3DA_%7B%5Cmu%7Ddx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"A=A_{\\mu}dx^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为一个 1 形式，将上述形式显式地展开得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ctextbf%7BE%7D%3D%5Cpartial_%7Bt%7D%5Ctextbf%7BA%7D-%5Cnabla+A_%7B0%7D%2C%5Cquad%5Ctextbf%7BB%7D%3D-%5Cnabla%5Ctimes%5Ctextbf%7BA%7D\" alt=\"\\textbf{E}=\\partial_{t}\\textbf{A}-\\nabla A_{0},\\quad\\textbf{B}=-\\nabla\\times\\textbf{A}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>即 1 形式 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A\" alt=\"A\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 就是四维矢势，Lorenz 规范条件实质上也就等价于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=dA%3D0\" alt=\"dA=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。而对于矢势的变换 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%5Crightarrow+A%2Bd%5CLambda\" alt=\"A\\rightarrow A+d\\Lambda\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，显然在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%3DdA\" alt=\"F=dA\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时是不改变电磁场的物理结构的。这也自然给出了电磁场的规范对称，我们在电动力学中导出的基本结论都是电磁场微分形式的平凡表现。</p><p>最后再考虑背景时空是一个非平凡拓扑—— <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B2%7D\" alt=\"S^{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，假设量子场存在奇点，或者说我们在空间中抹去了一个点，这时便会有磁单极子的出现。由 Maxwell 方程知道，考虑 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cstar+F\" alt=\"\\star F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的积分即得到通过球面的电通量，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cint_%7BS%5E%7B2%7D%7D%5Cstar+F%3Dq_%7Be%7D\" alt=\"\\int_{S^{2}}\\star F=q_{e}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>其中 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=q_%7Be%7D\" alt=\"q_{e}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 即通常意义上的电荷。相应的我们会想到，是否可以按照相似的方式给出磁荷呢？Hodge 算符恰好是让 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=E\" alt=\"E\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=B\" alt=\"B\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 对偶的变换，那么可以考虑 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F\" alt=\"F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的积分</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cint_%7BS%5E%7B2%7D%7DF%3Dq_%7Bm%7D\" alt=\"\\int_{S^{2}}F=q_{m}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>这样便给出了磁荷的定义。但又考虑到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B2%7D\" alt=\"S^{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 实际上是三维球体 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=B%5E%7B3%7D\" alt=\"B^{3}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的边界，那么由 Stokes 定理应该有</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cint_%7BB%5E%7B3%7D%7DdF%3Dq_%7Bm%7D\" alt=\"\\int_{B^{3}}dF=q_{m}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>而这显然与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=dF%3D0\" alt=\"dF=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 相矛盾。所以要使磁荷的定义是 well-defined 的，我们必须保证 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B2%7D\" alt=\"S^{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 不能是某个子流形的边界。要做到这点并不困难，在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B2%7D\" alt=\"S^{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上挖去一个点便可以，这也是 Dirac 磁单极子想法的来源。我们会在下一部分详细讨论这个问题。</p><p><b>二、规范场的拓扑结构</b></p><p>从上一节中可以看到电磁场的微分形式不仅可以给出更简洁的形式，同时也让我们理解到时空拓扑结构在电磁场中的重要性，这是我们用电场与磁场表示时所看不到的。这里我们再谈两个有关电磁场拓扑结构的典型例子：Dirac 磁单极子与 Aharonov--Bohm 效应。但在这之前，我们先讨论一处细节。</p><p>Maxwell 方程保证了 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=dF%3D0\" alt=\"dF=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，相应的 Poincare 引理则保证了 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%3DdA\" alt=\"F=dA\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，所以任意场强 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F\" alt=\"F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 都可以由一个规范势导出。而另一边，显然不同的规范给出的物理应当都是相同的，这会导致存在规范变换 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%3DA%2Bd%5CLambda\" alt=\"A=A+d\\Lambda\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。从而在平凡拓扑空间上，对于场位形我们有两种等价的描述：</p><p>闭形式场强的 2 形式集合 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%3A%5COmega_%7Bcl%7D%5E%7B2%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"F:\\Omega_{cl}^{2}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与服从规范变换的规范场 1 形式集合 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%3A%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29%2Fd%5COmega%5E%7B0%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"A:\\Omega^{1}(M)/d\\Omega^{0}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>对于平凡情形这两种等价描述好像并没有什么问题，但如果考虑非平凡的拓扑空间，我们会很快发现这两种表述不再等价，那么哪种表述是正确的呢？答案是两种皆否。</p><p>考虑如下恰当序列：</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=0%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B0%7D%7D%5Chookrightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B1%7D%7D%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29%2Fd%5COmega%5E%7B0%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B2%7D%7D%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7B2%7D_%7Bcl%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B3%7D%7D%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B2%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B4%7D%7D%5Crightarrow0\" alt=\"0\\stackrel{f_{0}}\\hookrightarrow H_{dR}^{1}(M)\\stackrel{f_{1}}\\rightarrow\\Omega^{1}(M)/d\\Omega^{0}(M)\\stackrel{f_{2}}\\rightarrow\\Omega^{2}_{cl}(M)\\stackrel{f_{3}}\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{2}(M)\\stackrel{f_{4}}\\rightarrow0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>其中的映射定义如下：</p><ul><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B0%7D\" alt=\"f_{0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为<b>包含映射(inclusion map)</b>，</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B1%7D%3A%5Csim%5BA%5D%5Crightarrow%5BA%5D%5C+%5Cforall+dA%3D0\" alt=\"f_{1}:\\sim[A]\\rightarrow[A]\\ \\forall dA=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 也是包含映射，</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B2%7D%3A%5BA%5D%5Crightarrow+dA\" alt=\"f_{2}:[A]\\rightarrow dA\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为外导数的导出映射，</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B3%7D%3AF%5Crightarrow%5BF%5D\" alt=\"f_{3}:F\\rightarrow[F]\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为闭形式到上同调的<b>标准映射(standard map)，</b></li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B4%7D\" alt=\"f_{4}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为到 0 的映射。</li></ul><p>可以证明 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=img%28f_%7Bn%7D%29%3Dker%28f_%7Bn%2B1%7D%29\" alt=\"img(f_{n})=ker(f_{n+1})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 对所有映射对都成立，即该序列确实是恰当的。</p><p>下面我们会利用该恰当序列的观点详细讨论平凡拓扑，AB 效应与 Dirac 磁单极子的情形。</p><ol><li>平凡拓扑空间</li></ol><p>平凡拓扑空间中，上述恰当序列的上同调群均为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5C%7B0%5C%7D\" alt=\"\\{0\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，从而有</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=0%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B1%7D%7D%5Chookrightarrow%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29%2Fd%5COmega%5E%7B0%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B2%7D%7D%5Crightarrow%5COmega_%7Bcl%7D%5E%7B2%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B3%7D%7D%5Crightarrow0\" alt=\"0\\stackrel{f_{1}}\\hookrightarrow\\Omega^{1}(M)/d\\Omega^{0}(M)\\stackrel{f_{2}}\\rightarrow\\Omega_{cl}^{2}(M)\\stackrel{f_{3}}\\rightarrow0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>该序列恰当意味着：</p><ul><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B1%7D\" alt=\"f_{1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的像与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B2%7D\" alt=\"f_{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的核相等。由于这里 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B1%7D\" alt=\"f_{1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的像显然是 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5C%7B0%5C%7D\" alt=\"\\{0\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，故 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B2%7D\" alt=\"f_{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的核也为零。即 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B2%7D\" alt=\"f_{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是单射（一一的）。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B2%7D\" alt=\"f_{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的像与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B3%7D\" alt=\"f_{3}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的核相等。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B3%7D\" alt=\"f_{3}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的核是整个 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5COmega_%7Bcl%7D%5E%7B2%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\Omega_{cl}^{2}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，相应的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B2%7D\" alt=\"f_{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的像也是如此。从而每个元素都是在像内的，即 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B2%7D\" alt=\"f_{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是满射（到上的）。</li></ul><p>从而 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B2%7D\" alt=\"f_{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为双射（一一到上的），两空间互为同构，即 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29%2Fd%5COmega%5E%7B0%7D%28M%29%5Ccong%5COmega%5E%7B2%7D_%7Bcl%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"\\Omega^{1}(M)/d\\Omega^{0}(M)\\cong\\Omega^{2}_{cl}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。在二者同构的情况下，显然两种空间的表述是等价的，无论是考虑规范场 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BA%5D%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29%2Fd%5COmega%5E%7B0%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"[A]\\in\\Omega^{1}(M)/d\\Omega^{0}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 还是场强 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%5Cin%5COmega%5E%7B2%7D_%7Bcl%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"F\\in\\Omega^{2}_{cl}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，结果都是一致的。</p><p>2. Aharonov--Bohm 位形</p><p>对于 AB 效应， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"H_{dR}^{1}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是非平凡的（ <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%3D%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5E%7B3%7D%5Ctimes+S%5E%7B1%7D\" alt=\"M=\\mathbb{R}^{3}\\times S^{1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ）。不妨假设磁场 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=B\" alt=\"B\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是沿着 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=z\" alt=\"z\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 方向的，大小为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=B%5E%7Bz%7D\" alt=\"B^{z}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。从而对于截面半径为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=R\" alt=\"R\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的 AB 效应磁场，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=r%5Cleq+R%3A+F%3D-B%5E%7Bz%7Ddx%5Cwedge+dy%2C\" alt=\"r\\leq R: F=-B^{z}dx\\wedge dy,\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=r%3ER%3AF%3D0.\" alt=\"r&gt;R:F=0.\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>将第一个式子转换成极坐标并利用 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%3DdA\" alt=\"F=dA\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=r%5Cleq+R%3A+A%3D-%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7DB%5E%7Bz%7Dr%5E%7B2%7Dd%5Ctheta\" alt=\"r\\leq R: A=-\\frac{1}{2}B^{z}r^{2}d\\theta\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>可以令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%3D-%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7DB%5E%7Bz%7DR%5E%7B2%7Dd%5Ctheta%5C+%5Cforall+r%3ER\" alt=\"A=-\\frac{1}{2}B^{z}R^{2}d\\theta\\ \\forall r&gt;R\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 使得 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%3DdA%3D0\" alt=\"F=dA=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 对于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=r%3ER\" alt=\"r&gt;R\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 总成立。不难发现只有穿过奇点 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28x%2Cy%29%3D%280%2C0%29\" alt=\"(x,y)=(0,0)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的那条线（也可以说是 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=z\" alt=\"z\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 轴）在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%5Csim+d%5Ctheta\" alt=\"A\\sim d\\theta\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是不能良好定义的。可以将这条线从空间中直接剔除使得 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A\" alt=\"A\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 能够良好定义，但这样就会使拓扑空间存在非平凡的结构， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H%5E%7B1%7D_%7BdR%7D%28M%29%5Cneq0\" alt=\"H^{1}_{dR}(M)\\neq0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B2%7D%28M%29%3D0\" alt=\"H_{dR}^{2}(M)=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，从而恰当序列为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=0%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B0%7D%7D%5Chookrightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B1%7D%7D%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29%2Fd%5COmega%5E%7B0%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B2%7D%7D%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7B2%7D_%7Bcl%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B3%7D%7D%5Crightarrow0\" alt=\"0\\stackrel{f_{0}}\\hookrightarrow H_{dR}^{1}(M)\\stackrel{f_{1}}\\rightarrow\\Omega^{1}(M)/d\\Omega^{0}(M)\\stackrel{f_{2}}\\rightarrow\\Omega^{2}_{cl}(M)\\stackrel{f_{3}}\\rightarrow0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>故</p><ul><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=img%28f_%7B2%7D%29%3Dker%28f_%7B3%7D%29%3D%5COmega_%7Bcl%7D%5E%7B2%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"img(f_{2})=ker(f_{3})=\\Omega_{cl}^{2}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=img%28f_%7B1%7D%29%3Dker%28f_%7B2%7D%29%3DH_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"img(f_{1})=ker(f_{2})=H_{dR}^{1}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li></ul><p>所以利用恰当性以及 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=img%28f%29%5Ccong+dom%28f%29%2Fker%28f%29\" alt=\"img(f)\\cong dom(f)/ker(f)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5COmega_%7Bcl%7D%5E%7B2%7D%28M%29%5Ccong%5Cfrac%7B%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29%2Fd%5COmega%5E%7B0%7D%28M%29%7D%7BH_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29%7D\" alt=\"\\Omega_{cl}^{2}(M)\\cong\\frac{\\Omega^{1}(M)/d\\Omega^{0}(M)}{H_{dR}^{1}(M)}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>即在 AB 位形中闭 2 形式 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F\" alt=\"F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的空间比规范场的空间要更“小”一些，这也很好理解，因为我们剔除掉了 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%5Csim+d%5Ctheta\" alt=\"A\\sim d\\theta\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 处的场强。在 AB 效应中场强存在不可观测的一条轴，所以这时测量规范场将给予我们更完整的物理信息。但对于 Dirac 磁单极子则恰恰相反。</p><p>3. Dirac 磁单极子</p><p>对于磁单极子，我们所考虑的位形空间是在 3 维空间中挖去一个点而不是一条线，这时所有的闭形式 1 循环 (closed 1--cycle) 都可以看做是 2 循环的边界（在 AB 效应中则不然），但闭形式 2 循环不再是 3 循环的边界，相当于在球面上有一点缺失。</p><p>从而由 De Rham 定理可以得到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H%5E%7B1%7D_%7BdR%7D%28M%29%3D0\" alt=\"H^{1}_{dR}(M)=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B2%7D%28M%29%3D%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"H_{dR}^{2}(M)=\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。这时 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%3D%5Csin%5Ctheta+d%5Ctheta%5Cwedge+d%5Cphi\" alt=\"F=\\sin\\theta d\\theta\\wedge d\\phi\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。可以写出恰当序列如下</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=0%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B1%7D%7D%5Chookrightarrow%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29%2Fd%5COmega%5E%7B0%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B2%7D%7D%5Crightarrow%5COmega%5E%7B2%7D_%7Bcl%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B3%7D%7D%5Crightarrow+H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B2%7D%28M%29%5Cstackrel%7Bf_%7B4%7D%7D%5Crightarrow0\" alt=\"0\\stackrel{f_{1}}\\hookrightarrow\\Omega^{1}(M)/d\\Omega^{0}(M)\\stackrel{f_{2}}\\rightarrow\\Omega^{2}_{cl}(M)\\stackrel{f_{3}}\\rightarrow H_{dR}^{2}(M)\\stackrel{f_{4}}\\rightarrow0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>按照与之前相似的步骤得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B2%7D%28M%29%5Ccong%5Cfrac%7B%5COmega%5E%7B2%7D_%7Bcl%7D%28M%29%7D%7B%5COmega%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29%2Fd%5COmega%5E%7B0%7D%28M%29%7D\" alt=\"H_{dR}^{2}(M)\\cong\\frac{\\Omega^{2}_{cl}(M)}{\\Omega^{1}(M)/d\\Omega^{0}(M)}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>显然这时 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F\" alt=\"F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的空间比规范场的空间要“大”一些了，场强比规范场包含了更完整的物理信息。出现这样的情况是由于拓扑空间非平凡导致 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=dF%3D0\" alt=\"dF=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 不再保证 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%3DdA\" alt=\"F=dA\" eeimg=\"1\"/> （Poincare 引理不再成立），从而这时 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A\" alt=\"A\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 仅仅描述了规范变换部分的场位形。当然，在磁单极子的系统中我们可以考虑不同的规范场使得其对应的场位形更大一些，详见 Davis Tong Instanton。在之后谈纤维丛时我们也会说到，规范场 1 形式还不是特别深刻的定义，利用纤维丛的语言以及联络形式我们能够给出规范场的“正确”表述（即使 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H_%7BdR%7D%5E%7B1%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"H_{dR}^{1}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=H%5E%7B2%7D_%7BdR%7D%28M%29\" alt=\"H^{2}_{dR}(M)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 均非平凡表述亦成立）。为了给之后纤维丛的讨论做铺垫，我们不再用简单的电磁场作为例子，而是考虑稍为复杂的 Yang--Mills 场。</p><p><b>三、Yang--Mills 场</b></p><p>（本部分具体推导可见 Schwartz 或 Weinberg 的 QFT，想了解更多在粒子物理里的细节可见<a href=\"https://zhuanlan.zhihu.com/p/22126107\" class=\"internal\">这本书</a>）这里首先考虑一个 toy model，由此出发讨论物理中规范场的出现方式。对于一个复标量场，其作用量可以自然的写为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5Csim%5Cint%5Cleft%28%5Ceta%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cphi%5E%7B%2A%7D%28x%29%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cnu%7D%5Cphi%28x%29-m%5Cphi%5E%7B%2A%7D%28x%29%5Cphi%28x%29%5Cright%29d%5E%7B4%7Dx\" alt=\"S\\sim\\int\\left(\\eta^{\\mu\\nu}\\partial_{\\mu}\\phi^{*}(x)\\partial_{\\nu}\\phi(x)-m\\phi^{*}(x)\\phi(x)\\right)d^{4}x\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=m\" alt=\"m\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为具有质量量纲的常数，通常意义而言就是我们所说的质量。而在场论框架中，使用对称性的方法来讨论场变换是很自然的想法，给定局域变换 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cphi%28x%29%5Crightarrow+e%5E%7Bi%5CLambda%28x%29%7D%5Cphi%28x%29\" alt=\"\\phi(x)\\rightarrow e^{i\\Lambda(x)}\\phi(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，那么</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cphi%28x%29%5Crightarrow+e%5E%7Bi%5CLambda%28x%29%7D%28%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cphi%28x%29%2Bi%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5CLambda%28x%29%5Cphi%28x%29%29\" alt=\"\\partial_{\\mu}\\phi(x)\\rightarrow e^{i\\Lambda(x)}(\\partial_{\\mu}\\phi(x)+i\\partial_{\\mu}\\Lambda(x)\\phi(x))\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>这时为了保证体系规范不变，需要引入协变导数</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cphi%28x%29%5Cequiv%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cphi%28x%29-iA_%7B%5Cmu%7D%28x%29%5Cphi%28x%29\" alt=\"D_{\\mu}\\phi(x)\\equiv\\partial_{\\mu}\\phi(x)-iA_{\\mu}(x)\\phi(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>这时我们自然地引出了一个新的场 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"A_{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，并且只知道这个场是协变的，对协变导数做局域变换</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cphi%28x%29%5Crightarrow+e%5E%7Bi%5CLambda%28x%29%7D%28%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cphi%28x%29%2Bi%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5CLambda%28x%29%5Cphi%28x%29-i%5Ctilde%7BA%7D_%7B%5Cmu%7D%28x%29%5Cphi%28x%29%29\" alt=\"D_{\\mu}\\phi(x)\\rightarrow e^{i\\Lambda(x)}(\\partial_{\\mu}\\phi(x)+i\\partial_{\\mu}\\Lambda(x)\\phi(x)-i\\tilde{A}_{\\mu}(x)\\phi(x))\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>这里使用 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ctilde%7BA%7D_%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"\\tilde{A}_{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 做标记是因为现在还不知道 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"A_{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 服从怎样的变换，但从上式不难发现，若给定变换 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7B%5Cmu%7D%28x%29%5Crightarrow%5Ctilde%7BA%7D_%7B%5Cmu%7D%28x%29%5Cequiv+A_%7B%5Cmu%7D%2B%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5CLambda%28x%29\" alt=\"A_{\\mu}(x)\\rightarrow\\tilde{A}_{\\mu}(x)\\equiv A_{\\mu}+\\partial_{\\mu}\\Lambda(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，则得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D_%7B%5Cmu%7D+%5Cphi%28x%29%5Crightarrow+e%5E%7Bi%5CLambda%28x%29%7DD_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cphi%28x%29\" alt=\"D_{\\mu} \\phi(x)\\rightarrow e^{i\\Lambda(x)}D_{\\mu}\\phi(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>从而动能项是 Lorentz 不变的。而为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"A_{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 选取的变换实际上就是所谓的规范变换。即如果给定微分形式 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%3DA_%7B%5Cmu%7D%28x%29dx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"A=A_{\\mu}(x)dx^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，规范变换就可以表示为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%5Crightarrow+A%2Bd%5CLambda\" alt=\"A\\rightarrow A+d\\Lambda\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>这里 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CLambda%28x%29\" alt=\"\\Lambda(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 0 形式。同时如果复标量场与规范场存在耦合，那么可以认为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7B%5Cmu%7D%28x%29\" alt=\"A_{\\mu}(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的动能项也可以看做是动力学场且满足规范不变，相应的自然想到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%3DdA\" alt=\"F=dA\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是一个合理的构造，而量纲分析要求具有两项 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F\" alt=\"F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 同量纲的乘积， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%5Cwedge+F\" alt=\"F\\wedge F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 显然是平凡的，所有可以在作用量中引入 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%5Cwedge%5Cstar+F\" alt=\"F\\wedge\\star F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 项得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5BA%2C%5Cphi%5D%3D%5Cint%28F%5Cwedge%5Cstar+F%2B%5Ceta%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7DD_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cphi%5E%7B%2A%7DD_%7B%5Cnu%7D%5Cphi%2BV%28%5Cphi%5E%7B%2A%7D%5Cphi%29%29\" alt=\"S[A,\\phi]=\\int(F\\wedge\\star F+\\eta^{\\mu\\nu}D_{\\mu}\\phi^{*}D_{\\nu}\\phi+V(\\phi^{*}\\phi))\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>这也是电磁场（规范场与电荷共轭的复标量场耦合）的自然结果。</p><ol><li>协变导数与平行移动</li></ol><p>考虑到规范场以协变导数的形式进行耦合，从微分几何的定义来看这要求我们引入平行移动的概念。我们会在下一次仔细讨论这部分的数学，这里首先给出基本的物理概念。考虑一流形 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/>，其上曲线由坐标参数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=x\" alt=\"x\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 给出。一般导数作用可以看做是函数平移的“生成元”。即</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cphi%28x%2B%5Cepsilon%29%3D%5Cphi%28x%29%2B%5Cepsilon%5Cfrac%7Bd%5Cphi%7D%7Bdx%7D%2B%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Cepsilon%5E%7B2%7D%5Cfrac%7Bd%5E%7B2%7D%5Cphi%7D%7Bdx%5E%7B2%7D%7D%2B%5Ccdots%3De%5E%7B%5Cepsilon%5Cfrac%7Bd%7D%7Bdx%7D%7D%5Cphi%28x%29\" alt=\"\\phi(x+\\epsilon)=\\phi(x)+\\epsilon\\frac{d\\phi}{dx}+\\frac{1}{2}\\epsilon^{2}\\frac{d^{2}\\phi}{dx^{2}}+\\cdots=e^{\\epsilon\\frac{d}{dx}}\\phi(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>这就好像是导数“移动”了函数值。然后我们考虑如何将这种表述类比到协变导数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cphi%28x%29%3D0\" alt=\"D_{\\mu}\\phi(x)=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上去。定义函数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cphi%3A%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5Crightarrow%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D\" alt=\"\\phi:\\mathbb{R}\\rightarrow\\mathbb{C}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为子集 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CSigma%5Csubset%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5Ctimes%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D\" alt=\"\\Sigma\\subset\\mathbb{R}\\times\\mathbb{C}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的元素，对任意 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=x%5Cin%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"x\\in\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 都有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28x%2Cy%29%5Cin%5CSigma\" alt=\"(x,y)\\in\\Sigma\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，我们定义 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=y%5Cequiv%5Cphi%28x%29\" alt=\"y\\equiv\\phi(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。这与我们一般的定义并没有本质差别，但这时所有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=x\" alt=\"x\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的邻域都有相匹配的复平面 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D_%7Bx%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{C}_{x}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 且 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=x\" alt=\"x\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 到复平面上一点存在一映射。从纤维丛的语言来说，这种构造使得底空间 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%29\" alt=\"(\\mathbb{R})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 中每一点都有给定纤维 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D_%7Bx%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{C}_{x}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，纤维可由纤维丛生成。</p><p>现在考虑平行移动，从 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28x_%7B0%7D%2Cy_%7B0%7D%29%5Cin%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5Ctimes%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D\" alt=\"(x_{0},y_{0})\\in\\mathbb{R}\\times\\mathbb{C}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 开始，函数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%28x%29%3Dy_%7B0%7D\" alt=\"f(x)=y_{0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的集合 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CSigma\" alt=\"\\Sigma\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 包含了其上所有点 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28x%2Cy_%7B0%7D%29\" alt=\"(x,y_{0})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，这告诉了我们平行移动是如何使 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28x_%7B0%7D%2Cy_%7B0%7D%29\" alt=\"(x_{0},y_{0})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 在不同纤维 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BC%7D_%7Bx%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{C}_{x}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 沿着 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 方向到达 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28x%2Cy_%7B0%7D%29\" alt=\"(x,y_{0})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的。同时需要注意 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%28x%29\" alt=\"f(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是一个常数函数仅在特定的移动方向下成立，比如对于局域变换 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=z%27_%7Bx%7D%5Crightarrow+e%5E%7Bi%5CLambda%28x%29%7Dz_%7Bx%7D\" alt=\"z&#39;_{x}\\rightarrow e^{i\\Lambda(x)}z_{x}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> （ <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=z_%7Bx%7D\" alt=\"z_{x}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为复平面上一变量），函数就不再是常数了，即 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cfrac%7Bd%7D%7Bdx%7Df%28x%29%3D0\" alt=\"\\frac{d}{dx}f(x)=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 实际上是与坐标相关的。但在协变导数下 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D_%7Bx%7D%5Cphi%28x%29%3D0\" alt=\"D_{x}\\phi(x)=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 却总是与坐标选取无关，数学上这种与人为选择无关的平行移动方式就称为联络。</p><p>最后说说为什么需要引入这种规范场的表述。假设我们的底空间为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B1%7D\" alt=\"S^{1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，场的取值为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D_%7Bx%7D%5C+%5Cforall+x%5Cin+S%5E%7B1%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{R}_{x}\\ \\forall x\\in S^{1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，但如果将 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28x%2Cy%29\" alt=\"(x,y)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 平行移动至 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28x%2C-y%29\" alt=\"(x,-y)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，那么可以得到一个拓扑结构 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5B0%2C1%5D%5Ctimes%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"[0,1]\\times\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，这时 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%280%2Cy%29%5Csimeq%281%2C-y%29\" alt=\"(0,y)\\simeq(1,-y)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，这种拓扑结构就是 Mobius 环，即 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B1%7D%5Ctimes%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"S^{1}\\times\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。在物理中这样的场位形并不罕见，它们不是简单地由底空间与给定纤维直接构造而成，而是丛的截面。这时我们便必须澄清平行移动的定义，从而需要引入联络：规范场。</p><p>2. 场强与曲率</p><p>现在让底空间的维数更高一些，相应的平行移动也可以沿着任一方向。但不同的平行移动操作显然不是对易的。广义相对论告诉我们二者的差异由 Riemann 张量来度量，假设有两个方向的平行移动，分别沿着切矢量 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X%5E%7B%5Crho%7D\" alt=\"X^{\\rho}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=Y%5E%7B%5Csigma%7D\" alt=\"Y^{\\sigma}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，则</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D_%7B%5C+%5Cnu%7D%3DR%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D_%7B%5C+%5Cnu%5Crho%5Csigma%7DX%5E%7B%5Crho%7DY%5E%7B%5Csigma%7D\" alt=\"A^{\\mu}_{\\ \\nu}=R^{\\mu}_{\\ \\nu\\rho\\sigma}X^{\\rho}Y^{\\sigma}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>对于一个二维球面来说，这就表示一矢量 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=Z%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D\" alt=\"Z^{\\nu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 先后沿着 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X\" alt=\"X\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=Y\" alt=\"Y\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 方向平行移动与其沿着 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=Y\" alt=\"Y\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X\" alt=\"X\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 方向平行移动的差别的结果。对于一般的规范场，这两类操作的差异就可以写为 </p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BD_%7B%5Cmu%7D%2CD_%7B%5Cnu%7D%5D%5Cphi%28z%29%3D-iF_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%5Cphi%28x%29\" alt=\"[D_{\\mu},D_{\\nu}]\\phi(z)=-iF_{\\mu\\nu}\\phi(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>即场强与曲率在度量规范场（联络）平行移动的差别时的效果是一致的。在之后的 Yang--Mills 场以及下一次的纤维丛理论中我们会看到这一点是多么的重要。</p><p>3. Yang--Mills 理论</p><p>现在我们考虑稍微复杂一些的情况，对于矢量场 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cphi%5E%7Bi%7D%28x%29\" alt=\"\\phi^{i}(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，使其服从一般 Lie 群的变换（e.g. <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%28N%29\" alt=\"SO(N)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%28N%29\" alt=\"U(N)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=Sp%282N%29\" alt=\"Sp(2N)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ）</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cphi%5E%7Bi%7D%28x%29%5Crightarrow%28e%5E%7Bic%5E%7Ba%7D%28x%29T_%7Ba%7D%7D%29%5E%7Bi%7D_%7B%5C+j%7D%5Cphi%5E%7Bj%7D%28x%29\" alt=\"\\phi^{i}(x)\\rightarrow(e^{ic^{a}(x)T_{a}})^{i}_{\\ j}\\phi^{j}(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>这里 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7Ba%7D\" alt=\"T_{a}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为所考虑的 Lie 代数的生成元， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=c%5E%7Ba%7D%28x%29\" alt=\"c^{a}(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为与坐标无关的因子。对于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%281%29\" alt=\"U(1)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 群，不难得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cphi%5E%7Bi%7D%28x%29%3D%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cphi%5E%7Bi%7D%28x%29-iA_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5E%7Ba%7D%28x%29%28T_%7Ba%7D%29%5E%7Bi%7D_%7B%5C+j%7D%5Cphi%5E%7Bj%7D%28x%29%5Crightarrow%28e%5E%7Bic%5E%7Ba%7D%28x%29T_%7Ba%7D%7D%29%5E%7Bi%7D_%7B%5C+j%7DD_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cphi%5E%7Bj%7D%28x%29\" alt=\"D_{\\mu}\\phi^{i}(x)=\\partial_{\\mu}\\phi^{i}(x)-iA_{\\mu}^{a}(x)(T_{a})^{i}_{\\ j}\\phi^{j}(x)\\rightarrow(e^{ic^{a}(x)T_{a}})^{i}_{\\ j}D_{\\mu}\\phi^{j}(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>从而规范场 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5E%7Ba%7D%28x%29\" alt=\"A_{\\mu}^{a}(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 服从变换 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5E%7Ba%7D%28x%29%5Crightarrow+A_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5E%7Ba%7D%28x%29%2B%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7Dc%5E%7Ba%7D%28x%29\" alt=\"A_{\\mu}^{a}(x)\\rightarrow A_{\\mu}^{a}(x)+\\partial_{\\mu}c^{a}(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。这允许我们将 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A\" alt=\"A\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的指标缩并并写成微分形式 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%28x%29%5Cequiv+A_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5E%7Ba%7D%28x%29T_%7Ba%7Ddx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"A(x)\\equiv A_{\\mu}^{a}(x)T_{a}dx^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。即 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A\" alt=\"A\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 1 形式，但不同逆变基底的系数这时不再是与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=x\" alt=\"x\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 有关的常数而是 Lie 代数元素了。这样的规范场称为具有 Lie 代数赋值(Lie algebra valued)的 1 形式。这种形式在之后纤维丛理论中我们会经常见到，它们可以描述联络。</p><p>利用协变导数可以再次构造局域 Lie 变 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BD_%7B%5Cmu%7D%2CD_%7B%5Cnu%7D%5D%5Cphi%5E%7Bi%7D%28x%29%3D-iF_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%5E%7Ba%7D%28x%29T_%7Ba%7D%5Cphi%28x%29\" alt=\"[D_{\\mu},D_{\\nu}]\\phi^{i}(x)=-iF_{\\mu\\nu}^{a}(x)T_{a}\\phi(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 换不变的场论作用量。首先假设存在一类双线型形式</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=Q%28%5Cphi%2C%5Cchi%29%5Cequiv+G_%7Bab%7D%5Cphi%5E%7Ba%7D%5Cchi%5E%7Bb%7D\" alt=\"Q(\\phi,\\chi)\\equiv G_{ab}\\phi^{a}\\chi^{b}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>该形式在 Lie 变换 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=Q%28U%5Cphi%2CU%5Cchi%29%3DQ%28%5Cphi%2C%5Cchi%29\" alt=\"Q(U\\phi,U\\chi)=Q(\\phi,\\chi)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 下不变。这里我们只考虑 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%28N%29\" alt=\"SO(N)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 形式的 Lie 群，这时 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=G_%7Bab%7D%3D%5Cdelta_%7Bab%7D\" alt=\"G_{ab}=\\delta_{ab}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U\" alt=\"U\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 变换下不变。从而写出作用量</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cint%5C%2Cd%5E%7B4%7Dx%28G_%7Bab%7D%5Ceta%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7DD_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cphi%5E%7Ba%7DD_%7B%5Cnu%7D%5Cphi%5E%7Bb%7D-V%28G_%7Bab%7D%5Cphi%5E%7Ba%7D%5Cphi%5E%7Bb%7D%29%29\" alt=\"\\int\\,d^{4}x(G_{ab}\\eta^{\\mu\\nu}D_{\\mu}\\phi^{a}D_{\\nu}\\phi^{b}-V(G_{ab}\\phi^{a}\\phi^{b}))\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>该作用量在局域 Lie 变换下是不变的。</p><p>那么能否对规范场本身也构造一个 Lie 不变的动能项呢（就像我们对 Maxwell 方程考虑 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%281%29\" alt=\"U(1)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 变换一样）？答案当然是肯定的，类比 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%281%29\" alt=\"U(1)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 变换，可以将平行移动的差别写为 </p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BD_%7B%5Cmu%7D%2CD_%7B%5Cnu%7D%5D%5Cphi%28z%29%3D-iF%5E%7Ba%7D_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%28x%29T_%7Ba%7D%5Cphi%28x%29\" alt=\"[D_{\\mu},D_{\\nu}]\\phi(z)=-iF^{a}_{\\mu\\nu}(x)T_{a}\\phi(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>这时场强也需要改写为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%5E%7Ba%7D%28x%29%3D%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7DA_%7B%5Cnu%7D%28x%29-%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cnu%7DA_%7B%5Cmu%7D%28x%29%3Dif_%7B%5C+bc%7D%5E%7Ba%7DA_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5E%7Bb%7D%28x%29A_%7B%5Cnu%7D%5E%7Bc%7D%28x%29\" alt=\"F_{\\mu\\nu}^{a}(x)=\\partial_{\\mu}A_{\\nu}(x)-\\partial_{\\nu}A_{\\mu}(x)=if_{\\ bc}^{a}A_{\\mu}^{b}(x)A_{\\nu}^{c}(x)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f_%7B%5C+bc%7D%5E%7Ba%7D\" alt=\"f_{\\ bc}^{a}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 Lie 代数的结构常数，源于一般 Lie 代数结构中生成元的对易关系 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BT_%7Bb%7D%2CT_%7Bc%7D%5D%3Df_%7B%5C+bc%7D%5E%7Ba%7DT_%7Ba%7D\" alt=\"[T_{b},T_{c}]=f_{\\ bc}^{a}T_{a}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。一样地可以将 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F\" alt=\"F\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 写为 Lie 代数赋值的 2 形式 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%28x%29%3DF_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%5E%7Ba%7D%28x%29T_%7Ba%7Ddx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cwedge+dx%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D\" alt=\"F(x)=F_{\\mu\\nu}^{a}(x)T_{a}dx^{\\mu}\\wedge dx^{\\nu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，用微分形式还可以写得更紧凑些</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=F%3DdA-iA%5Cwedge+A\" alt=\"F=dA-iA\\wedge A\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>不难发现这时由于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7Ba%7D\" alt=\"T_{a}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的存在导致生成元之间不对易， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%5Cwedge+A\" alt=\"A\\wedge A\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 不再为零。最后构造规范场作用量如下</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5Csim%5Cint%5C%2C%5Ctextrm%7Btr%7D%28F%5Cwedge%5Cstar+F%29\" alt=\"S\\sim\\int\\,\\textrm{tr}(F\\wedge\\star F)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> （分量表示即为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cint%5C%2C%5Ctextrm%7Btr%7D%28F_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D+F%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%29\" alt=\"\\int\\,\\textrm{tr}(F_{\\mu\\nu} F^{\\mu\\nu})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ）。</p><p>这与之前唯一的差别就在于求迹作用，这是为了使作用量中的 Lie 代数赋值形式化为常数。该作用量就是我们所说的 Yang--Mills 作用量，它描述了除引力外所有基本相互作用力下规范场的行为。</p><p class=\"ztext-empty-paragraph\"><br/></p><p><b>References</b></p><p>[1] R. Butt, L W. Tu. Differential forms in algebraic topology, volume 82 of Graduate Texts in Mathematics. Springer-Verlag, 1982.</p><p>[2] G E. Bredon. Topology and geometry, volume 139 of Graduate Texts in Mathematics. Springer-Verlag, 1993.</p><p>[3] M. Nakahara. Geometry, Topology and Physics. Institute of Physics Publishing, 2003.</p><hr/><p>最后代表逢田姐消灭全天下的梨黑(tui)o(≥▽≤o)</p>",
