alt=\"\\begin{align}\\frac{1}{2\\alpha&#39; p^{+}}\\sum_{i}(\\partial_{+}X^{i})^{2}&amp;=\\frac{1}{4p^{+}}\\sum_{i,k,m}\\alpha_{k}^{i}\\alpha_{m}^{i}e^{-i(k+m)(\\tau+\\sigma)}=\\frac{1}{4p^{+}}\\sum_{n,i,m}\\alpha_{n-m}^{i}\\alpha_{m}^{i}e^{-in(\\tau+\\sigma)} \\end{align}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>代回 (3) 得到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B-%7D\" alt=\"\\alpha_{n}^{-}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的展开解</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B-%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B%5Csqrt%7B2%5Calpha%27%7Dp%5E%7B%2B%7D%7D%5Cleft%28%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Csum_%7Bi%3D1%7D%5E%7BD-2%7D%5Csum_%7Bm%7D%3A%5Calpha_%7Bn-m%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%3A-a%5Cdelta_%7Bn%2C0%7D%5Cright%29\" alt=\"\\alpha_{n}^{-}=\\frac{1}{\\sqrt{2\\alpha&#39;}p^{+}}\\left(\\frac{1}{2}\\sum_{i=1}^{D-2}\\sum_{m}:\\alpha_{n-m}^{i}\\alpha_{m}^{i}:-a\\delta_{n,0}\\right)\" eeimg=\"1\"/>   (5)</p><p>对于闭弦，依照同样的方式可以变换得到左行与右行的模态解</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbegin%7Balign%7D+X%5E%7B%2B%7D%28%5Ctau%2C%5Csigma%29%26%3Dx%5E%7B%2B%7D%2B%5Calpha%27+p%5E%7B%2B%7D%5Ctau%2C%5C%5C+X%5E%7B-%7D%28%5Ctau%2C%5Csigma%29%26%3Dx%5E%7B-%7D%2B%5Calpha%27+p%5E%7B-%7D%5Ctau%2B%5Csqrt%7B%5Calpha%27%7D%7B2%7D%5Csum_%7Bn%5Cneq0%7D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7Bn%7D%5B%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B-%7De%5E%7B-in%28%5Ctau%2B%5Csigma%29%7D%2B%5Ctilde%7B%5Calpha%7D_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B-%7De%5E%7B-in%28%5Ctau-%5Csigma%29%7D%5D+%5Cend%7Balign%7D\" alt=\"\\begin{align} X^{+}(\\tau,\\sigma)&amp;=x^{+}+\\alpha&#39; p^{+}\\tau,\\\\ X^{-}(\\tau,\\sigma)&amp;=x^{-}+\\alpha&#39; p^{-}\\tau+\\sqrt{\\alpha&#39;}{2}\\sum_{n\\neq0}\\frac{1}{n}[\\alpha_{n}^{-}e^{-in(\\tau+\\sigma)}+\\tilde{\\alpha}_{n}^{-}e^{-in(\\tau-\\sigma)}] \\end{align}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>其中</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B-%7D%3D%5Csqrt%7B%5Cfrac%7B2%7D%7B%5Calpha%27%7D%7D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7Bp%5E%7B%2B%7D%7D%5Cleft%28%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Csum_%7Bi%3D1%7D%5E%7BD-2%7D%5Csum_%7Bm%7D%3A%5Calpha_%7Bn-m%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%3A-a%5Cdelta_%7Bn%2C0%7D%5Cright%29%5C%5C+%5Ctilde%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B-%7D%3D%5Csqrt%7B%5Cfrac%7B2%7D%7B%5Calpha%27%7D%7D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7Bp%5E%7B%2B%7D%7D%5Cleft%28%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Csum_%7Bi%3D1%7D%5E%7BD-2%7D%5Csum_%7Bm%7D%3A%5Ctilde%5Calpha_%7Bn-m%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%5Ctilde%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%3A-a%5Cdelta_%7Bn%2C0%7D%5Cright%29\" alt=\"\\alpha_{n}^{-}=\\sqrt{\\frac{2}{\\alpha&#39;}}\\frac{1}{p^{+}}\\left(\\frac{1}{2}\\sum_{i=1}^{D-2}\\sum_{m}:\\alpha_{n-m}^{i}\\alpha_{m}^{i}:-a\\delta_{n,0}\\right)\\\\ \\tilde\\alpha_{n}^{-}=\\sqrt{\\frac{2}{\\alpha&#39;}}\\frac{1}{p^{+}}\\left(\\frac{1}{2}\\sum_{i=1}^{D-2}\\sum_{m}:\\tilde\\alpha_{n-m}^{i}\\tilde\\alpha_{m}^{i}:-a\\delta_{n,0}\\right)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>所以在光锥规范量子化下， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X%5E%7B-%7D\" alt=\"X^{-}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 和 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X%5E%7B%2B%7D\" alt=\"X^{+}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 都是可以消去的自由度，只有类空坐标 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=X%5E%7Bi%7D\" alt=\"X^{i}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 对应真正的粒子激发态。</p><ul><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a\" alt=\"a\" eeimg=\"1\"/> <b>的约束</b></li></ul><p>由于只有类空模态 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7Bi%7D\" alt=\"\\alpha_{n}^{i}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 产生真正的激发态，第一激发态 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\alpha_{-1}^{i}|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可以构成 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%28D-2%29\" alt=\"SO(D-2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D-2\" alt=\"D-2\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 维矢量表示。从场论观点看这是很显然的，Lorentz 不变性总会诱导物理态为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%28D-2%29\" alt=\"SO(D-2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 无质量态（或 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%28D-1%29\" alt=\"SO(D-1)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 有质量态）的表示。以 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D%3D4\" alt=\"D=4\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的 Lorentz 群单粒子态为例，</p><ul><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=p%5E%7B2%7D%3D-M%5E%7B2%7D%3C0%2C%5C+p%5E%7B0%7D%3E0\" alt=\"p^{2}=-M^{2}&lt;0,\\ p^{0}&gt;0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为有质量正能态，服从 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%283%29\" alt=\"SO(3)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 变换，小群 (little group，貌似有些翻译是迷向子群) 为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28M%2C0%2C0%2C0%29\" alt=\"(M,0,0,0)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=p%5E%7B2%7D%3D-M%5E%7B2%7D%3C0%2C%5C+p%5E%7B0%7D%3C0\" alt=\"p^{2}=-M^{2}&lt;0,\\ p^{0}&lt;0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为有质量负能态，服从 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%283%29\" alt=\"SO(3)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 变换，小群为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28-M%2C0%2C0%2C0%29\" alt=\"(-M,0,0,0)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=p%5E%7B2%7D%3D0%2C%5C+p%5E%7B0%7D%3E0\" alt=\"p^{2}=0,\\ p^{0}&gt;0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为无质量正能态，服从 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=ISO%282%29\" alt=\"ISO(2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 变换，小群为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28%5Ckappa%2C0%2C0%2C%5Ckappa%29\" alt=\"(\\kappa,0,0,\\kappa)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=p%5E%7B2%7D%3D0%2C%5C+p%5E%7B0%7D%3C0\" alt=\"p^{2}=0,\\ p^{0}&lt;0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为无质量负能态，服从 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=ISO%282%29\" alt=\"ISO(2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 变换，小群为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28-%5Ckappa%2C0%2C0%2C%5Ckappa%29\" alt=\"(-\\kappa,0,0,\\kappa)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=p%5E%7B2%7D%3DN%5E%7B2%7D%3E0\" alt=\"p^{2}=N^{2}&gt;0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为快子态，服从 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%282%2C1%29\" alt=\"SO(2,1)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 变换，小群为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%280%2C0%2C0%2CN%29\" alt=\"(0,0,0,N)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=p%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%3D0\" alt=\"p^{\\mu}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为真空态，服从 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%283%2C1%29\" alt=\"SO(3,1)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 变换，小群为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%280%2C0%2C0%2C0%29\" alt=\"(0,0,0,0)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li></ul><p>从而要使光锥量子化下的玻色弦理论为 Lorentz 不变的， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\alpha_{-1}^{i}|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 必须是无质量态。即</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%5E%7B2%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B1-a%7D%7B%5Calpha%27%7D%3D0%5CRightarrow+a%3D1\" alt=\"M^{2}=\\frac{1-a}{\\alpha&#39;}=0\\Rightarrow a=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>这与我们在正则量子化时给出的结果是一致的。</p><ul><li><b>临界维度</b></li></ul><p>接下来再给出维数的要求，我们从 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B0%7D\" alt=\"L_{0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 中心扩张给出正则排序常数的步骤出发，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Csum_%7Bi%3D1%7D%5E%7BD-2%7D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D-%5Cinfty%7D%5E%5Cinfty%5Calpha_%7B-n%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Csum_%7Bi%3D1%7D%5E%7BD-2%7D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D-%5Cinfty%7D%5E%5Cinfty%5Cleft%28%3A%5Calpha_%7B-n%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%3A%2B%5B%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%2C%5Calpha_%7B-n%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%5D%5Cright%29%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Csum_%7Bi%3D1%7D%5E%7BD-2%7D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D-%5Cinfty%7D%5E%5Cinfty%3A%5Calpha_%7B-n%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%3A%2B%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%28D-2%29%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7Dn\" alt=\"\\frac{1}{2}\\sum_{i=1}^{D-2}\\sum_{n=-\\infty}^\\infty\\alpha_{-n}^{i}\\alpha_{n}^{i}=\\frac{1}{2}\\sum_{i=1}^{D-2}\\sum_{n=-\\infty}^\\infty\\left(:\\alpha_{-n}^{i}\\alpha_{n}^{i}:+[\\alpha_{n}^{i},\\alpha_{-n}^{i}]\\right)=\\frac{1}{2}\\sum_{i=1}^{D-2}\\sum_{n=-\\infty}^\\infty:\\alpha_{-n}^{i}\\alpha_{n}^{i}:+\\frac{1}{2}(D-2)\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}n\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>其中 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7Dn\" alt=\"\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}n\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 显然是发散的，利用场论中的正规化，将该级数表示为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Czeta\" alt=\"\\zeta\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 函数。</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Czeta%28s%29%3D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7Dn%5E%7B-s%7D\" alt=\"\\zeta(s)=\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}n^{-s}\" eeimg=\"1\"/>   (6)</p><p>从场论里 Casimir 效应 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5E%7B%5B1%5D%7D\" alt=\"^{[1]}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 知道 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Czeta%28-1%29%3D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7Dn%3D-%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B12%7D\" alt=\"\\zeta(-1)=\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}n=-\\frac{1}{12}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。这里我们仿照一般正规化的步骤简单推导该结论。</p><p> 为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7Dn\" alt=\"\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}n\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 赋予一项收敛因子 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=e%5E%7B-%5Cepsilon+n%7D\" alt=\"e^{-\\epsilon n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ( <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cepsilon%5Cll1\" alt=\"\\epsilon\\ll1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ) 得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7Dn+e%5E%7B-%5Cepsilon+n%7D%3D-%5Cfrac%7Bd%7D%7Bd%5Cepsilon%7D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7De%5E%7B-%5Cepsilon+n%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7Be%5E%7B-%5Cepsilon%7D%7D%7B%281-e%5E%7B-%5Cepsilon%7D%29%5E%7B2%7D%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B%5Cepsilon%5E%7B2%7D%7D-%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B12%7D%2B%5Cmathcal%7BO%7D%28%5Cepsilon%5E%7B2%7D%29\" alt=\"\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}n e^{-\\epsilon n}=-\\frac{d}{d\\epsilon}\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}e^{-\\epsilon n}=\\frac{e^{-\\epsilon}}{(1-e^{-\\epsilon})^{2}}=\\frac{1}{\\epsilon^{2}}-\\frac{1}{12}+\\mathcal{O}(\\epsilon^{2})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>而至于为什么可以在令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cepsilon%5Crightarrow0\" alt=\"\\epsilon\\rightarrow0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时丢掉 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B%5Cepsilon%5E%7B2%7D%7D\" alt=\"\\frac{1}{\\epsilon^{2}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 项，则需要考虑到 Weyl 不变性，对于一般弦理论，收敛因子的幂往往还与弦长 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=l\" alt=\"l\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 有关，而这样一项会由作用量中的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cint%5C%2Cd%5E%7BD%7Dx%5Csqrt%7B-g%7D\" alt=\"\\int\\,d^{D}x\\sqrt{-g}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 抵消，详见 Polchinski 1.3。所以</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%28D-2%29%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7Dn%3D-%5Cfrac%7BD-2%7D%7B24%7D\" alt=\"\\frac{1}{2}(D-2)\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}n=-\\frac{D-2}{24}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>这一项需要抵消 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%3D1\" alt=\"a=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的效应，从而</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cfrac%7BD-2%7D%7B24%7D%3D1%5CRightarrow+D%3D26\" alt=\"\\frac{D-2}{24}=1\\Rightarrow D=26\" eeimg=\"1\"/>   (7)</p><p>即在不考虑相互作用的玻色弦理论中，两种量子化方式是互相自洽的。除了这两种基本的量子化以及路径积分量子化外，还有一种纯粹的代数方式可以用于确定玻色弦要求的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a\" alt=\"a\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D\" alt=\"D\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。其基本思路是通过验证满足 Lorentz 代数的 Lorentz 生成元，从最基本的 Lorentz 对称性出发来确定 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a\" alt=\"a\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 和 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D\" alt=\"D\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的值。详见 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5E%7B%5B2%5D%7D\" alt=\"^{[2]}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> (David Tong 2.4 也有简单介绍)。</p><ul><li><b>开弦的谱分析</b></li></ul><p>最后来讨论自洽玻色弦的谱性质。开弦质量谱为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%5E%7B2%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7BN-a%7D%7B%5Calpha%27%7D\" alt=\"M^{2}=\\frac{N-a}{\\alpha&#39;}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=N%3D%5Csum_%7Bi%3D1%7D%5E%7BD-1%7D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5Calpha_%7B-n%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7Bi%7D\" alt=\"N=\\sum_{i=1}^{D-1}\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}\\alpha_{-n}^{i}\\alpha_{n}^{i}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p> Examples 1: </p><ul><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=N%3D0\" alt=\"N=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 态， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%5E%7B2%7D%3D-%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B%5Calpha%27%7D\" alt=\"M^{2}=-\\frac{1}{\\alpha&#39;}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。该负质量对应快子态。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=N%3D1\" alt=\"N=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\alpha_{-1}^{i}|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 态， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%5E%7B2%7D%3D0\" alt=\"M^{2}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 对应矢量玻色子，构成 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%2824%29\" alt=\"SO(24)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的矢量表示。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=N%3D2\" alt=\"N=2\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时给出正质量 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%5E%7B2%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B%5Calpha%27%7D\" alt=\"M^{2}=\\frac{1}{\\alpha&#39;}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的第一激发态。分别有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7B-2%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\alpha_{-2}^{i}|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%5Calpha%5E%7Bj%7D_%7B-1%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\alpha_{-1}^{i}\\alpha^{j}_{-1}|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 两类可能的态。它们共同构成 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%2825%29\" alt=\"SO(25)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28D-2%29%2B%5Cfrac%7B%28D-2%29%28D-1%29%7D%7B2%7D%3D24%2B300%3D324\" alt=\"(D-2)+\\frac{(D-2)(D-1)}{2}=24+300=324\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 个态表示。注意到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28D-2%29%2B%5Cfrac%7B%28D-2%29%28D-1%29%7D%7B2%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B%28D-1%29D%7D%7B2%7D-1\" alt=\"(D-2)+\\frac{(D-2)(D-1)}{2}=\\frac{(D-1)D}{2}-1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，这意味着 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%2825%29\" alt=\"SO(25)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的表示中存在对称无迹的 2 阶张量。从而在此质量层级，谱中一定会产生一个有质量的自旋为 2 的粒子态。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=N%3D3\" alt=\"N=3\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时质量谱 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%5E%7B2%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B2%7D%7B%5Calpha%27%7D\" alt=\"M^{2}=\\frac{2}{\\alpha&#39;}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 给出的可能态有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7B-3%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\alpha_{-3}^{i}|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7B-2%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%5E%7Bj%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\alpha_{-2}^{i}\\alpha_{-1}^{j}|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%5Calpha%5E%7Bj%7D_%7B-1%7D%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%5E%7Bk%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\alpha_{-1}^{i}\\alpha^{j}_{-1}\\alpha_{-1}^{k}|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，共有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=24%2B576%2B2600%3D3200\" alt=\"24+576+2600=3200\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 个不同表示。</li></ul><p>所有态均为正模长态，因为在光锥量子化中它们完全由类空模式构成，都存在于正定 Hilbert 空间中。</p><ul><li><b>闭弦的谱分析</b></li></ul><p>对于闭弦，我们需要考虑两套模态的谱性质，但从开弦态的基础出发讨论这点并不困难，因为闭弦的态可以看做左行与右行开弦态的张量积。</p><p>Examples 2: </p><ul><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=N%3D0\" alt=\"N=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时，基态 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 对应 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%5E%7B2%7D%3D-%5Cfrac%7B4%7D%7B%5Calpha%27%7D\" alt=\"M^{2}=-\\frac{4}{\\alpha&#39;}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，为快子态。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=N%3D1\" alt=\"N=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%5E%7B2%7D%3D0\" alt=\"M^{2}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 给出的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%5E%7Bi%7D%5Ctilde%7B%5Calpha%7D_%7B-1%7D%5E%7Bj%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\alpha_{-1}^{i}\\tilde{\\alpha}_{-1}^{j}|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 对应两类无质量矢量玻色子的张量积，共同构成 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%2824%29\" alt=\"SO(24)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ctextbf%7B24%7D%5Cotimes%5Ctextbf%7B24%7D\" alt=\"\\textbf{24}\\otimes\\textbf{24}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 表示。这些态可以分解为三类不可约表示：</li></ul><p>(1) 无迹对称张量 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=G_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%28X%29\" alt=\"G_{\\mu\\nu}(X)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>(2)反对称张量 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=B_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%28X%29\" alt=\"B_{\\mu\\nu}(X)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与</p><p>(3) 单态 (迹部分) <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CPhi%28X%29\" alt=\"\\Phi(X)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=G_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%28X%29\" alt=\"G_{\\mu\\nu}(X)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 对应的是引力场激发态， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=B_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%28X%29\" alt=\"B_{\\mu\\nu}(X)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 对应一类反对称张量场激发态， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CPhi%28X%29\" alt=\"\\Phi(X)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 对应一类标量场激发态。在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%2824%29\" alt=\"SO(24)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的表示中它们分别具有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%28D-1%29%28D-2%29-1%3D299\" alt=\"\\frac{1}{2}(D-1)(D-2)-1=299\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%28D-2%29%28D-3%29%3D276\" alt=\"\\frac{1}{2}(D-2)(D-3)=276\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=1\" alt=\"1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 个态表示。</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=G_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%28X%29\" alt=\"G_{\\mu\\nu}(X)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的激发态描述的是一个无质量的自旋为 2 的粒子，而如果理论中存在产生相互作用的无质量自旋为 2 的粒子，它的效应与广义相对论的效应必是等价的 (详见 David Tong 2.3)。即 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=G_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%28X%29\" alt=\"G_{\\mu\\nu}(X)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 描述的就是<b>引力子</b>。</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=B_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%28X%29\" alt=\"B_{\\mu\\nu}(X)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 实际上是无质量标量的 2 形式规范场，所描述的激发态称作<b>轴子(Axion)</b>。</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CPhi%28X%29\" alt=\"\\Phi(X)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是纯粹由 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SO%2824%29\" alt=\"SO(24)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 表示的迹部分给出的标量场，所描述的激发态称作<b>胀子(Dilaton)</b>。</p><p>最后引用文献 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5E%7B%5B3%5D%7D\" alt=\"^{[3]}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=N%3D0%5Csim4\" alt=\"N=0\\sim4\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的开弦谱与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=N%3D0%5Csim2\" alt=\"N=0\\sim2\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的闭弦谱给出简单的图示总结。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7e26b0cab96504394eabddd6bd3b3b0e_b.jpg\" data-caption=\"\" data-size=\"normal\" data-rawwidth=\"617\"             "title": "给梨推（hei）的玻色弦概述（四）", 
            "content": "<p>接上回正则协变量子化剩下的部分。已经写完的小节分别为 (1) 算符化，(2) 物理态和 (3) 质量谱。这次写的是 (4) 无鬼定理和 (5) 伪态。</p><hr/><ul><li>无鬼定理（No-ghost theorem）</li></ul><p>在力学量算符化的过程中我们已经看到会出现非物理的负模长，在 QFT 的规范理论中实际上也会出现类似的现象，我们称之为鬼场 (ghost field)。这部分要做的事情就是如何将鬼场消除并给出消除它们的条件。</p><p>以 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a\" alt=\"a\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D\" alt=\"D\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为变量，它们的变化将使 Hilbert 空间中的半定区域变为拥有负模长态的区域，同时零模长的态将处于两区域的边界。以开弦为例，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%5E%7B2%7D%3D-k%5E%7B2%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7BN-a%7D%7B%5Calpha%27%7D\" alt=\"M^{2}=-k^{2}=\\frac{N-a}{\\alpha&#39;}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=N%3D1\" alt=\"N=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时有第一激发态： <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cepsilon%2Ck%5Crangle%3D%5Cepsilon%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle%5Cquad+k%5E%7B2%7D%5Csim+a-1\" alt=\"|\\epsilon,k\\rangle=\\epsilon\\cdot\\alpha_{-1}|0;k\\rangle\\quad k^{2}\\sim a-1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，而 Virasoro 代数告诉我们 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B1%7D%7C%5Cepsilon%3Bk%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"L_{1}|\\epsilon;k\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ：</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbegin%7Balign%7D+%26L_%7B1%7D%7C%5Cepsilon%2Ck%5Crangle%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D-%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5Calpha_%7B1-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5Cepsilon%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle%3D%28%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5Ccdot%5Cepsilon%29%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle%3D0%5C%5C+%5CRightarrow%26%5Cepsilon%5Ccdot+k%3D0+%5Cend%7Balign%7D\" alt=\"\\begin{align} &amp;L_{1}|\\epsilon,k\\rangle=\\frac{1}{2}\\sum_{n=-\\infty}^{\\infty}\\alpha_{1-n}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}\\epsilon\\cdot\\alpha_{-1}|0;k\\rangle=(\\alpha_{0}\\cdot\\epsilon)|0;k\\rangle=0\\\\ \\Rightarrow&amp;\\epsilon\\cdot k=0 \\end{align}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>从而模长可表示为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Clangle%5Cepsilon%2Ck%7C%5Cepsilon%2Ck%5Crangle%3D%5Cepsilon%5Ccdot%5Cepsilon\" alt=\"\\langle\\epsilon,k|\\epsilon,k\\rangle=\\epsilon\\cdot\\epsilon\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><ul><li>当 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%3C1\" alt=\"a&lt;1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k%5E%7B2%7D%3C0\" alt=\"k^{2}&lt;0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为类时动量，模长为正。</li><li>当 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%3D1\" alt=\"a=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k%5E%7B2%7D%3D0\" alt=\"k^{2}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为类光动量，模长非负（模长并不直接为零，因为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cepsilon\" alt=\"\\epsilon\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 中有一部分随 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k\" alt=\"k\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 类光，但还有一部分处于类空状态）。</li><li>当 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%3E1\" alt=\"a&gt;1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k%5E%7B2%7D%3E0\" alt=\"k^{2}&gt;0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为类空动量，模长为负。</li></ul><p>从而得到消除鬼场的第一个条件</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%5Cleq1\" alt=\"a\\leq1\" eeimg=\"1\"/>   （1）</p><p>对于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%3D1\" alt=\"a=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的边界情形，产生的矢量粒子总是无质量的（ <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=m%5E%7B2%7D%3D-k%5E%7B2%7D%3D0\" alt=\"m^{2}=-k^{2}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ），而标量粒子为快子。这里 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B1%7D%7C%5Cepsilon%3Bk%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"L_{1}|\\epsilon;k\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 在电动力学中实际上就反映为规范条件 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7DA%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%3D0\" alt=\"\\partial_{\\mu}A^{\\mu}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，但值得注意的是在弦论中这个条件是由代数结构直接给出的，无需人为的赋予条件。同时该条件意味着弦论中的矢量粒子具有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D-2\" alt=\"D-2\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 个具有横向极化的正模长态和一个具有纵向极化 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cepsilon%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%3Dk%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"\\epsilon^{\\mu}=k^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的零模态。</p><ul><li>伪态</li></ul><p>伪态是一类满足质壳定理但不产生任何物理贡献的物理态。</p><p>Definition 1: 在 Hilbert 空间中若存在态矢 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\psi\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 满足下列条件：</p><p>1) <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28L_%7B0%7D-a%29%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"(L_{0}-a)|\\psi\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/>，</p><p>2) <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Clangle%5Cphi%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"\\langle\\phi|\\psi\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> （ <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\phi\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为物理态）。</p><p>我们考虑一个典型的伪态 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle%3D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7DL_%7B-n%7D%7C%5Cchi_%7Bn%7D%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\psi\\rangle=\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}L_{-n}|\\chi_{n}\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，其中 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28L_%7B0%7D-a%2Bn%29%7C%5Cchi_%7Bn%7D%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"(L_{0}-a+n)|\\chi_{n}\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，可以证明它满足 Definition 1 给出的条件。</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbegin%7Balign%7D+%28L_%7B0%7D-a%29%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle%26%3D%28L_%7B0%7D-a%29%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7DL_%7B-n%7D%7C%5Cchi_%7Bn%7D%5Crangle%5C%5C+%26%3D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28L_%7B0%7DL_%7B-n%7D-aL_%7B-n%7D%29%7C%5Cchi_%7Bn%7D%5Crangle%5C%5C+%26%3D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%28L_%7B-n%7DL_%7B0%7D%2BnL_%7B-n%7D-aL_%7B-n%7D%29%7C%5Cchi_%7Bn%7D%5Crangle%5C%5C+%26%3D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7DL_%7B-n%7D%28L_%7B0%7D%2Bn-a%29%7C%5Cchi_%7Bn%7D%5Crangle%5C%5C+%26%3D0+%5Cend%7Balign%7D\" alt=\"\\begin{align} (L_{0}-a)|\\psi\\rangle&amp;=(L_{0}-a)\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}L_{-n}|\\chi_{n}\\rangle\\\\ &amp;=\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}(L_{0}L_{-n}-aL_{-n})|\\chi_{n}\\rangle\\\\ &amp;=\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}(L_{-n}L_{0}+nL_{-n}-aL_{-n})|\\chi_{n}\\rangle\\\\ &amp;=\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}L_{-n}(L_{0}+n-a)|\\chi_{n}\\rangle\\\\ &amp;=0 \\end{align}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>另外， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Clangle%5Cphi%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle%3D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5Clangle%5Cphi%7CL_%7B-n%7D%7C%5Cchi_%7Bn%7D%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"\\langle\\phi|\\psi\\rangle=\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}\\langle\\phi|L_{-n}|\\chi_{n}\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>考虑到 Virasoro 代数结构 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BL_%7Bm%7D%2CL_%7Bn%7D%5D%3D%28m-n%29L_%7Bm%2Bn%7D\" alt=\"[L_{m},L_{n}]=(m-n)L_{m+n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/>，上述级数总可以写为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B-1%7D\" alt=\"L_{-1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B-2%7D\" alt=\"L_{-2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的表出形式，即 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle%3DL_%7B-1%7D%7C%5Cchi_%7B1%7D%5Crangle%2BL_%7B-2%7D%7C%5Cchi_%7B2%7D%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\psi\\rangle=L_{-1}|\\chi_{1}\\rangle+L_{-2}|\\chi_{2}\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。如果一个态既是伪态又是物理态，其模长总是零。若取 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%3D1\" alt=\"a=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，我们会发现得到的伪态总是零模长的，这也意味着 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%3D1\" alt=\"a=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的确是正模长物理态与负模长物理态的边界特征 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5E%7B%5B1%5D%7D\" alt=\"^{[1]}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>接下来我们考虑维数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D\" alt=\"D\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 在消除负模长时的约束。这里构造零模长伪态如下（这之后我们都取 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a\" alt=\"a\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 1），</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle%3D%28L_%7B-2%7D%2B%5Cgamma+L_%7B-1%7D%5E%7B2%7D%29%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\psi\\rangle=(L_{-2}+\\gamma L_{-1}^{2})|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>对于特定的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cgamma\" alt=\"\\gamma\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 取值，可以保证 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\psi\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 必为零模，下面先讨论如何确定 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cgamma\" alt=\"\\gamma\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。态矢 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 满足</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28L_%7B0%7D%2B1%29%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle%3DL_%7Bm%7D%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"(L_{0}+1)|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle=L_{m}|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>而 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28L_%7B0%7D-1%29%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle%3D%28L_%7B0%7D-1%29%28L_%7B-2%7D%2B%5Cgamma+L_%7B-1%7D%5E%7B2%7D%29%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"(L_{0}-1)|\\psi\\rangle=(L_{0}-1)(L_{-2}+\\gamma L_{-1}^{2})|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，从而得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cgamma+L_%7B-1%7D%5E%7B2%7D%28L_%7B0%7D%2B1%29%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"\\gamma L_{-1}^{2}(L_{0}+1)|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>再引入物理态的条件 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7Bn%7D%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle%3D0%28n%5Cin%5Cmathbb%7BN%7D%5E%7B%2B%7D%29\" alt=\"L_{n}|\\psi\\rangle=0(n\\in\\mathbb{N}^{+})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，如前所述，我们仍然只需要考虑 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B1%7D\" alt=\"L_{1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 和 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B2%7D\" alt=\"L_{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的情况，注意到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BL_%7B1%7D%2CL_%7B-1%7D%5E%7B2%7D%5D%3DL_%7B-1%7D%5BL_%7B1%7D%2CL_%7B-1%7D%5D%2B%5BL_%7B1%7D%2CL_%7B-1%7D%5DL_%7B-1%7D%3D4L_%7B0%7DL_%7B-1%7D-2L_%7B-1%7D\" alt=\"[L_{1},L_{-1}^{2}]=L_{-1}[L_{1},L_{-1}]+[L_{1},L_{-1}]L_{-1}=4L_{0}L_{-1}-2L_{-1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/>，我们有</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbegin%7Balign%7DL_%7B1%7D%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle%26%3DL_%7B1%7D%28L_%7B-2%7D%2B%5Cgamma+L_%7B-1%7D%5E%7B2%7D%29%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle%5C%5C+%26%3D%5Cleft%5BL_%7B-1%7DL_%7B1%7D%2B3L_%7B-1%7D%2B%5Cgamma%28L_%7B-1%7D%5E%7B2%7DL_%7B1%7D%2B4L_%7B0%7DL_%7B-1%7D-2L_%7B-1%7D%29%5Cright%5D%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle%5C%5C+%26%3D%5B3L_%7B-1%7D%2B%5Cgamma%284L_%7B0%7DL_%7B-1%7D-2L_%7B-1%7D%29%5D%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle%5C%5C+%26%3D%5B%283-2%5Cgamma%29L_%7B-1%7D%2B4%5Cgamma+L_%7B0%7DL_%7B-1%7D%5D%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle%5C%5C+%26%3D%283-2%5Cgamma%29L_%7B-1%7D%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle%2B4%5Cgamma%28L_%7B-1%7DL_%7B0%7D%2BL_%7B-1%7D%29%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle%5C%5C+%26%3D%283-2%5Cgamma%29L_%7B-1%7D%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle%3D0+%5Cend%7Balign%7D\" alt=\"\\begin{align}L_{1}|\\psi\\rangle&amp;=L_{1}(L_{-2}+\\gamma L_{-1}^{2})|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle\\\\ &amp;=\\left[L_{-1}L_{1}+3L_{-1}+\\gamma(L_{-1}^{2}L_{1}+4L_{0}L_{-1}-2L_{-1})\\right]|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle\\\\ &amp;=[3L_{-1}+\\gamma(4L_{0}L_{-1}-2L_{-1})]|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle\\\\ &amp;=[(3-2\\gamma)L_{-1}+4\\gamma L_{0}L_{-1}]|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle\\\\ &amp;=(3-2\\gamma)L_{-1}|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle+4\\gamma(L_{-1}L_{0}+L_{-1})|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle\\\\ &amp;=(3-2\\gamma)L_{-1}|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle=0 \\end{align}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>从而 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cgamma%3D%5Cfrac%7B3%7D%7B2%7D\" alt=\"\\gamma=\\frac{3}{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。然后对于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B2%7D\" alt=\"L_{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，由 Virasoro 代数，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BL_%7B2%7D%2CL_%7B-2%7D%5D%3D4L_%7B0%7D%2B%5Cfrac%7Bc%7D%7B2%7D\" alt=\"[L_{2},L_{-2}]=4L_{0}+\\frac{c}{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BL_%7B2%7D%2CL_%7B-1%7D%5E%7B2%7D%5D%3D6%28L_%7B0%7D%2BL_%7B-1%7DL_%7B1%7D%29\" alt=\"[L_{2},L_{-1}^{2}]=6(L_{0}+L_{-1}L_{1})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>从而</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbegin%7Balign%7D0%3DL_%7B2%7D%7C%5Cpsi%5Crangle%26%3DL_%7B2%7D%5Cleft%28L_%7B-2%7D%2B%5Cfrac%7B3%7D%7B2%7DL_%7B-1%7D%5E%7B2%7D%5Cright%29%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle%5C%5C+%26%3D%5Cleft%5B4L_%7B0%7D%2B%5Cfrac%7Bc%7D%7B2%7D%2B9%28L_%7B0%7D%2BL_%7B-1%7DL_%7B1%7D%29%5Cright%5D%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle%5C%5C+%26%3D%5Cleft%5B13L_%7B0%7D%2B%5Cfrac%7Bc%7D%7B2%7D%2B9L_%7B-1%7DL_%7B1%7D%5Cright%5D%5C%5C+%26%3D%5Cleft%28-13%2B%5Cfrac%7Bc%7D%7B2%7D%5Cright%29%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle+%5Cend%7Balign%7D\" alt=\"\\begin{align}0=L_{2}|\\psi\\rangle&amp;=L_{2}\\left(L_{-2}+\\frac{3}{2}L_{-1}^{2}\\right)|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle\\\\ &amp;=\\left[4L_{0}+\\frac{c}{2}+9(L_{0}+L_{-1}L_{1})\\right]|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle\\\\ &amp;=\\left[13L_{0}+\\frac{c}{2}+9L_{-1}L_{1}\\right]\\\\ &amp;=\\left(-13+\\frac{c}{2}\\right)|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle \\end{align}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>故 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D%3Dc%3D26\" alt=\"D=c=26\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。这便是为何玻色弦仅在 $D=26$ 时才是自洽的。对于维数的要求是源自于负模长或快子态的出现，这在一般的场论中是罕见的。</p><p>最后我们再做一些推广，对于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D%3E26\" alt=\"D&gt;26\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的情形，考虑物理态为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D%5Cleft%5BA%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%2BB%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-2%7D%2BC%28%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%29%5E%7B2%7D%5Cright%5D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\phi\\rangle=\\left[A\\alpha_{-1}\\cdot\\alpha_{-1}+B\\alpha_{0}\\cdot\\alpha_{-2}+C(\\alpha_{0}\\cdot\\alpha_{-1})^{2}\\right]|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><ul><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%3D1\" alt=\"a=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 给出 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28L_%7B0%7D-1%29%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D%5Cleft%28%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5E%7B2%7D%2B%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5Calpha_%7B-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5Cright%29%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"(L_{0}-1)|\\phi\\rangle=\\left(\\frac{1}{2}\\alpha_{0}^{2}+\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}\\alpha_{-n}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}\\right)|\\phi\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，另外由物理态的定义有</li></ul><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28L_%7B0%7D-1%29%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-2%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle%3D%5Cleft%28%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5E%7B2%7D%2B2-1%5Cright%29%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-2%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"(L_{0}-1)\\alpha_{0}\\cdot\\alpha_{-2}|0;k\\rangle=\\left(\\frac{1}{2}\\alpha_{0}^{2}+2-1\\right)\\alpha_{0}\\cdot\\alpha_{-2}|0;k\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CRightarrow\" alt=\"\\Rightarrow\" eeimg=\"1\"/> <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5E%7B2%7D%3D-2\" alt=\"\\alpha_{0}^{2}=-2\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><ul><li>而 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B1%7D%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"L_{1}|\\phi\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 给出</li></ul><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Csum_%7Bn%3D-%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5Calpha_%7B1-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle%3D4%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\sum_{n=-\\infty}^{\\infty}\\alpha_{1-n}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}\\alpha_{-1}\\cdot\\alpha_{-1}|0;k\\rangle=4\\alpha_{0}\\cdot\\alpha_{-1}|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Csum_%7Bn%3D-%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5Calpha_%7B1-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-2%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle%3D4%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\sum_{n=-\\infty}^{\\infty}\\alpha_{1-n}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}\\alpha_{0}\\cdot\\alpha_{-2}|0;k\\rangle=4\\alpha_{0}\\cdot\\alpha_{-1}|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Csum_%7Bn%3D-%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5Calpha_%7B1-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%28%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%29%5E%7B2%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle%3D-8%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\sum_{n=-\\infty}^{\\infty}\\alpha_{1-n}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}(\\alpha_{0}\\cdot\\alpha_{-1})^{2}|0;k\\rangle=-8\\alpha_{0}\\cdot\\alpha_{-1}|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CRightarrow\" alt=\"\\Rightarrow\" eeimg=\"1\"/> <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B1%7D%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D2%28A%2BB-2C%29%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"L_{1}|\\phi\\rangle=2(A+B-2C)\\alpha_{0}\\cdot\\alpha_{-1}|0;k\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CRightarrow+A%2BB-2C%3D0\" alt=\"\\Rightarrow A+B-2C=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><ul><li>又有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B2%7D%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"L_{2}|\\phi\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，可以得到</li></ul><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Csum_%7Bn%3D-%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5Calpha_%7B2-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle%3D2D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\sum_{n=-\\infty}^{\\infty}\\alpha_{2-n}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}\\alpha_{-1}\\cdot\\alpha_{-1}|0;k\\rangle=2D|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Csum_%7Bn%3D-%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5Calpha_%7B2-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-2%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle%3D-8%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\sum_{n=-\\infty}^{\\infty}\\alpha_{2-n}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}\\alpha_{0}\\cdot\\alpha_{-2}|0;k\\rangle=-8|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Csum_%7Bn%3D-%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5Calpha_%7B2-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%28%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%29%5E%7B2%7D%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle%3D-8%7C0%3Bk%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\sum_{n=-\\infty}^{\\infty}\\alpha_{2-n}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}(\\alpha_{0}\\cdot\\alpha_{-1})^{2}|0;k\\rangle=-8|0;k\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CRightarrow+DA-4B-2C%3D0\" alt=\"\\Rightarrow DA-4B-2C=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>综上， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=B%3D%5Cfrac%7BD-1%7D%7B5%7DA%2C%5Cquad+C%3D%5Cfrac%7BD%2B4%7D%7B10%7DA\" alt=\"B=\\frac{D-1}{5}A,\\quad C=\\frac{D+4}{10}A\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>这时模长可以写为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Clangle%5Cphi%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D%5Cfrac%7B2A%5E%7B2%7D%7D%7B25%7D%28D-1%29%2826-D%29\" alt=\"\\langle\\phi|\\phi\\rangle=\\frac{2A^{2}}{25}(D-1)(26-D)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>即当 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D%3E26\" alt=\"D&gt;26\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时必定会出现负模长，物理谱中会有鬼场的存在。</p><p>实际上伪态的存在正是为了保证它们能与真实的物理过程相分离，这样所有的真实物理态均具有非负模长。综上所述，出现鬼场的条件为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%5Cleq1\" alt=\"a\\leq1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 以及 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D%3C26\" alt=\"D&lt;26\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><ul><li><b>小结</b></li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D%3E26\" alt=\"D&gt;26\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 或 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%3E1\" alt=\"a&gt;1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时，物理态空间始终包含负模长态，</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D%3D26\" alt=\"D=26\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 且 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%3C1\" alt=\"a&lt;1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时，物理态空间可以存在负模长态，</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D%3D26\" alt=\"D=26\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 且 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%3D1\" alt=\"a=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时，物理态空间仅包含非负模长态，或者说这时真实态空间 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathcal%7BF%7D%5E%7B%5Coplus%7D%5Cequiv%5Cmathcal%7BF%7D%5E%7B%5Ctextrm%7Bphys%7D%7D%2F%5Cmathcal%7BF%7D%5E%7B0%7D\" alt=\"\\mathcal{F}^{\\oplus}\\equiv\\mathcal{F}^{\\textrm{phys}}/\\mathcal{F}^{0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 总是具有正定模长，但 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathcal%7BF%7D%5E%7B%5Ctextrm%7Bphys%7D%7D\" alt=\"\\mathcal{F}^{\\textrm{phys}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathcal%7BF%7D%5E%7B0%7D%3D%5Cleft%5C%7B%28L_%7B-2%7D%5Cfrac%7B3%7D%7B2%7DL_%7B-1%7D%5E%7B2%7D%29%7C%5Ctilde%7B%5Cchi%7D%5Crangle%5Coplus+L_%7B-1%7D%7C%5Cchi_%7B1%7D%5Crangle%5Cright%5C%7D\" alt=\"\\mathcal{F}^{0}=\\left\\{(L_{-2}\\frac{3}{2}L_{-1}^{2})|\\tilde{\\chi}\\rangle\\oplus L_{-1}|\\chi_{1}\\rangle\\right\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 均为类光态空间。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D%3C26\" alt=\"D&lt;26\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 且 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%5Cleq1\" alt=\"a\\leq1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时，物理态空间仅包含 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%3C1\" alt=\"a&lt;1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的正模长态与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%3D1\" alt=\"a=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的零模长态。</li></ul><p>一般而言，我们考虑的玻色弦理论都是基于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%3D1\" alt=\"a=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 且 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D%3D26\" alt=\"D=26\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的，这种弦论称作临界玻色弦理论，相应的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D%3D26\" alt=\"D=26\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 称作其临界维度。而 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%5Cleq1\" alt=\"a\\leq1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 或 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D%5Cleq25\" alt=\"D\\leq25\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的情形称为非临界情形。</p><p><b>References</b></p><p>[1] String Theory (Vol. 1). Green, Schwartz, Witten. Sec. 2.2.</p><hr/><p>征求一下意见（虽然可能根本没有人看到这里），大家是想看弦振幅还是 superstring？下回写完光锥量子化玻色弦概述部分就准备结束了。路径积分量子化不打算写了，因为安宇森前辈的文章已经写得足够完善，基本涵盖了 Polchinski 前三四章的重点内容。不过这两个话题我都超不出教材太多，想看弦振幅我就会从 Polchinski 第五章开始写，但是想看 superstring 的话就先写 supersymmetry，这一部分我就比较熟一点，感谢建议~</p><p>最后，代表逢田姐消灭全天下的梨黑(tui)o(≥▽≤o)</p>",

            "title": "给梨推（hei）的玻色弦概述（三）", 
            "content": "<p>数学部分很多名词我不确定中文翻译，不确定的地方我都写出了英文。另外修正上次结尾说的，这次要谈的不是光锥量子化而是弦的正则量子化。</p><hr/><ul><li><b>Witt 代数</b></li></ul><p>令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k\" alt=\"k\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为任意非零示性数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=p\" alt=\"p\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的一个场，考虑 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k\" alt=\"k\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 构成的代数</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7Bn%7D%3Dk%5BX_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2CX_%7Bn%7D%5D%2F%28X_%7B1%7D%5E%7Bp%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2CX_%7Bn%7D%5E%7Bp%7D%29\" alt=\"A_{n}=k[X_{1},\\cdots,X_{n}]/(X_{1}^{p},\\cdots,X_{n}^{p})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>这是一个可交换环结构（但并不是 Witt 环）。</p><p>Definition 1: 令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V_%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"V_{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为环 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"A_{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k\" alt=\"k\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 阶衍生（k-derivation），可以证明 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V_%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"V_{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是一个单 Lie 代数（2 维情形除外），其中 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V_%7B1%7D\" alt=\"V_{1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 即为 Witt 代数， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=n%5Cgeq2\" alt=\"n\\geq2\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V_%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"V_{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 定义为分裂 Jacobson--Witt 代数（split Jacobson--Witt algebra）。</p><p>即 Witt 代数就是环 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A_%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"A_{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 衍生的 Lie 代数，除此之外也可以定义为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B1%7D\" alt=\"S^{1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上矢量场 Lie 代数的复化。</p><p>Properties:</p><ul><li>Witt 代数的一组基可以表示为矢量场 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7Bn%7D%3D-z%5E%7Bn%2B1%7D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%7D%7B%5Cpartial+z%7D\" alt=\"L_{n}=-z^{n+1}\\frac{\\partial}{\\partial z}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li><li>矢量场之间 Lie 括号为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BL_%7Bm%7D%2CL_%7Bn%7D%5D%3D%28m-n%29L_%7Bm%2Bn%7D\" alt=\"[L_{m},L_{n}]=(m-n)L_{m+n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li><li>若 Witt 代数定义在 Riemann 球面上，仅有两个不动点的场是非全纯的。</li><li>Witt 代数相当于经典的 Virasoro 代数。</li><li>在物理上 Witt 代数的出现是由于规范选取 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=h_%7Bab%7D%3D%5Ceta_%7Bab%7D\" alt=\"h_{ab}=\\eta_{ab}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 无法完全固定重参数化对称性。</li></ul><p>我们之前已经提到 Polyakov 作用量的局域对称变换 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Csigma%5E%7B%5Calpha%7D%5Crightarrow+f%5E%7B%5Calpha%7D%28%5Csigma%29%3D%5Csigma%27%5E%5Calpha\" alt=\"\\sigma^{\\alpha}\\rightarrow f^{\\alpha}(\\sigma)=\\sigma&#39;^\\alpha\" eeimg=\"1\"/>，<img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=h_%7B%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+f%5E%7B%5Cgamma%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial%5Csigma%5E%7B%5Calpha%7D%7D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+f%5E%7B%5Cdelta%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial%5Csigma%5E%7B%5Cbeta%7D%7Dh_%7B%5Cgamma%5Cdelta%7D%28%5Csigma%27%29\" alt=\"h_{\\alpha\\beta}=\\frac{\\partial f^{\\gamma}}{\\partial\\sigma^{\\alpha}}\\frac{\\partial f^{\\delta}}{\\partial\\sigma^{\\beta}}h_{\\gamma\\delta}(\\sigma&#39;)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 以及 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ctilde%7Bh%7D%5E%7Bab%7D%3De%5E%7B%5Cphi%28%5Csigma%29%7Dh_%7Bab%7D\" alt=\"\\tilde{h}^{ab}=e^{\\phi(\\sigma)}h_{ab}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。考虑无穷小对称变换 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Csigma%5E%7Ba%7D%5Crightarrow%5Ctilde%7B%5Csigma%7D%5E%7Ba%7D%3D%5Csigma%5E%7Ba%7D%2B%5Cxi%5E%7Ba%7D%28%5Csigma%29%2B%5Cmathcal%7BO%7D%28%5Cxi%5E%7B2%7D%29\" alt=\"\\sigma^{a}\\rightarrow\\tilde{\\sigma}^{a}=\\sigma^{a}+\\xi^{a}(\\sigma)+\\mathcal{O}(\\xi^{2})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cxi%5E%7Ba%7D\" alt=\"\\xi^{a}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为重参数化时的无穷小参数，令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CLambda\" alt=\"\\Lambda\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 Weyl 重标度化的无穷小参数，有 </p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%281%2B%5CLambda%2B%5Cmathcal%7BO%7D%28%5CLambda%5E%7B2%7D%29%29%5Ceta_%7Bab%7D%3D%5Cleft%28%5Cdelta_%7Ba%7D%5E%7Bc%7D%2B%5Cpartial_%7Ba%7D%5Cxi%5E%7Bc%7D%2B%5Cmathcal%7BO%7D%28%5Cxi%5E%7B2%7D%29%5Cright%29%5Cleft%28%5Cdelta_%7Bb%7D%5E%7Bd%7D%2B%5Cpartial_%7Bb%7D%5Cxi%5E%7Bd%7D%2B%5Cmathcal%7BO%7D%28%5Cxi%5E%7B2%7D%29%5Cright%29%5Ceta_%7Bcd%7D\" alt=\"(1+\\Lambda+\\mathcal{O}(\\Lambda^{2}))\\eta_{ab}=\\left(\\delta_{a}^{c}+\\partial_{a}\\xi^{c}+\\mathcal{O}(\\xi^{2})\\right)\\left(\\delta_{b}^{d}+\\partial_{b}\\xi^{d}+\\mathcal{O}(\\xi^{2})\\right)\\eta_{cd}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>从而</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial%5E%7Ba%7D%5Cxi%5E%7Bb%7D%2B%5Cpartial%5E%7Bb%7D%5Cxi%5E%7Ba%7D%3D%5CLambda%5Ceta%5E%7Bab%7D\" alt=\"\\partial^{a}\\xi^{b}+\\partial^{b}\\xi^{a}=\\Lambda\\eta^{ab}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。  (1)</p><p>显然这条对称性服从之前的规范选取<img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=h_%7Bab%7D%3D%5Ceta_%7Bab%7D\" alt=\"h_{ab}=\\eta_{ab}\" eeimg=\"1\"/>。这便是共形对称，为了将 Witt 代数过渡到 Virasoro 代数，共形场中的代数中心扩张技术是必要的，但这里我们暂不赘述。</p><ul><li><b>Virasoro 代数</b></li></ul><p>限于笔者水平，我们试着从物理上完成中心扩张的过程，之前提到 Virasoro 代数实际上相当于 Witt 代数的量子化版本，而量子化时，我们需要将力学量算符化，对于 Virasoro 代数，自然地需要算符化 Virasoro 生成元 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7Bm%7D\" alt=\"L_{m}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，我们为其赋予正规排序（normal-ordering），</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7Bm%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D-%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%3A%5Calpha_%7Bm-n%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%3A%2C%5Cquad%5B%5Calpha_%7Bm-n%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%2C%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%5D%5Csim%5Cdelta_%7Bm%2C0%7D\" alt=\"L_{m}=\\frac{1}{2}\\sum_{n=-\\infty}^{\\infty}:\\alpha_{m-n}^{\\mu}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}:,\\quad[\\alpha_{m-n}^{\\mu},\\alpha_{n}^{\\nu}]\\sim\\delta_{m,0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>这里的正规排序定义与一般场论中的略有不同，</p><p>Definition 2: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%3A%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%3A%5Cequiv%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%28m%3Cn%29\" alt=\":\\alpha_{m}^{\\mu}\\alpha_{n}^{\\nu}:\\equiv\\alpha_{m}^{\\mu}\\alpha_{n}^{\\nu}(m&lt;n)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>如此一来所有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=m%5Cneq0\" alt=\"m\\neq0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7Bm%7D\" alt=\"L_{m}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 均定义为了量子化算符。而 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B0%7D\" alt=\"L_{0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B0%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D-%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%3A%5Calpha_%7B-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%3A%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5E%7B2%7D%2B%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%2B%5Cinfty%7D%5Calpha_%7B-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"L_{0}=\\frac{1}{2}\\sum_{n=-\\infty}^{\\infty}:\\alpha_{-n}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}:=\\frac{1}{2}\\alpha_{0}^{2}+\\sum_{n=1}^{+\\infty}\\alpha_{-n}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。（2）</p><p>即 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B0%7D\" alt=\"L_{0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的定义中总会出现一任意常数，为了保证其定义良好，我们一般使用 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B0%7D-a\" alt=\"L_{0}-a\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 替代之（ <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a\" alt=\"a\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 亦为一常数，用于补偿任意常数的影响）。</p><p>回到 Witt 代数的基本结构 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BL_%7Bm%7D%2CL_%7Bn%7D%5D%3D%28m-n%29L_%7Bm%2Bn%7D\" alt=\"[L_{m},L_{n}]=(m-n)L_{m+n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/>，不难发现当 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=m%2Bn%3D0\" alt=\"m+n=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时会出现正规排序定义的混乱，这要求我们引入一个复数，</p><p> Definition 3: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BL_%7Bm%7D%2CL_%7Bn%7D%5D%3D%28m-n%29L_%7Bm%2Bn%7D%2BA%28m%29%5Cdelta_%7Bm%2Bn%2C0%7D%2C%5Cquad+A%28m%29%3D%5Csum_%7Bn%7Dc_%7Bn%7DQ_%7Bn%7D%28m%29\" alt=\"[L_{m},L_{n}]=(m-n)L_{m+n}+A(m)\\delta_{m+n,0},\\quad A(m)=\\sum_{n}c_{n}Q_{n}(m)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=Q_%7Bn%7D%28m%29\" alt=\"Q_{n}(m)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是仅与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=m\" alt=\"m\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 有关的多项式， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=c_%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"c_{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为任意复常数。</p><p>为了得到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%28m%29\" alt=\"A(m)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，考虑到 Witt 代数是一个 Lie 代数，具有 Jacobi 等式</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BL_%7Bk%7D%2C%5BL_%7Bn%2C%7DL_%7Bm%7D%5D%5D%2B%5BL_%7Bn%7D%2C%5BL_%7Bm%2C%7DL_%7Bk%7D%5D%5D%2B%5BL_%7Bm%7D%2C%5BL_%7Bk%2C%7DL_%7Bn%7D%5D%5D%3D0\" alt=\"[L_{k},[L_{n,}L_{m}]]+[L_{n},[L_{m,}L_{k}]]+[L_{m},[L_{k,}L_{n}]]=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>当n+m+k= <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=n%2Bm%2Bk%3D0\" alt=\"n+m+k=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 时有</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28n-m%29A%28k%29%2B%28m-k%29A%28n%29%2B%28k-n%29A%28m%29%3D0\" alt=\"(n-m)A(k)+(m-k)A(n)+(k-n)A(m)=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k%3D1\" alt=\"k=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 且 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=m%2Bn%3D-1\" alt=\"m+n=-1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%28n%2B1%29%3D%5Cfrac%7B%28n%2B2%29A%28n%29-%282n%2B1%29A%281%29%7D%7Bn-1%7D\" alt=\"A(n+1)=\\frac{(n+2)A(n)-(2n+1)A(1)}{n-1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>由此递推式可以得到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%28n%29\" alt=\"A(n)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 由 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%281%29\" alt=\"A(1)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%282%29\" alt=\"A(2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的表出式，而 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%281%29\" alt=\"A(1)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%282%29\" alt=\"A(2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的值不难由定义导出，从而</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%28m%29%3Dc_%7B1%7Dm%2Bc_%7B3%7Dm%5E%7B3%7D\" alt=\"A(m)=c_{1}m+c_{3}m^{3}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。（3）</p><p>接下来需要确定未知系数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=c_%7B1%7D\" alt=\"c_{1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 及 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=c_%7B3%7D\" alt=\"c_{3}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，注意到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Clangle0%3B0%7C%5BL_%7B1%7D%2CL_%7B-1%7D%5D%7C0%3B0%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"\\langle0;0|[L_{1},L_{-1}]|0;0\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> （由模式展开得到），而由 Virasoro 代数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Clangle0%3B0%7C%5BL_%7B1%7D%2CL_%7B-1%7D%5D%7C0%3B0%5Crangle%3Dc_%7B1%7D%2Bc_%7B3%7D%5Cquad%28p%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%7C0%3B0%5Crangle%3D0%29\" alt=\"\\langle0;0|[L_{1},L_{-1}]|0;0\\rangle=c_{1}+c_{3}\\quad(p^{\\mu}|0;0\\rangle=0)\" eeimg=\"1\"/>。同样的对于<img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Clangle0%3B0%7C%5BL_%7B2%7D%2CL_%7B-2%7D%5D%7C0%3B0%5Crangle\" alt=\"\\langle0;0|[L_{2},L_{-2}]|0;0\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 由模式展开得</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbegin%7Balign%7D+%5Clangle0%3B0%7C%5BL_%7B2%7D%2CL_%7B-2%7D%5D%7C0%3B0%5Crangle%26%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B4%7D%5Clangle0%3B0%7C%5Calpha_%7B1%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B1%7D%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%7C0%3B0%5Crangle%5C%5C+%26%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B4%7D%5Ceta_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%5Ceta_%7B%5Crho%5Clambda%7D%5Clangle0%3B0%7C%5Calpha_%7B1%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Calpha_%7B1%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%5E%7B%5Crho%7D%5Calpha%5E%7B%5Clambda%7D_%7B-1%7D%7C0%3B0%5Crangle%5C%5C+%26%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Ceta_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%5Clangle0%3B0%7C%5Calpha_%7B1%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Calpha_%7B-1%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%7C0%3B0%5Crangle%5C%5C+%26%3D%5Cfrac%7B%5Ceta_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%5Ceta%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%7D%7B2%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7BD%7D%7B2%7D+%5Cend%7Balign%7D\" alt=\"\\begin{align} \\langle0;0|[L_{2},L_{-2}]|0;0\\rangle&amp;=\\frac{1}{4}\\langle0;0|\\alpha_{1}\\cdot\\alpha_{1}\\alpha_{-1}\\cdot\\alpha_{-1}|0;0\\rangle\\\\ &amp;=\\frac{1}{4}\\eta_{\\mu\\nu}\\eta_{\\rho\\lambda}\\langle0;0|\\alpha_{1}^{\\mu}\\alpha_{1}^{\\nu}\\alpha_{-1}^{\\rho}\\alpha^{\\lambda}_{-1}|0;0\\rangle\\\\ &amp;=\\frac{1}{2}\\eta_{\\mu\\nu}\\langle0;0|\\alpha_{1}^{\\mu}\\alpha_{-1}^{\\nu}|0;0\\rangle\\\\ &amp;=\\frac{\\eta_{\\mu\\nu}\\eta^{\\mu\\nu}}{2}=\\frac{D}{2} \\end{align}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>而由 (3)，<img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Clangle0%3B0%7C%5BL_%7B2%7D%2CL_%7B-2%7D%5D%7C0%3B0%5Crangle%3D2c_%7B1%7D%2B8c_%7B3%7D\" alt=\"\\langle0;0|[L_{2},L_{-2}]|0;0\\rangle=2c_{1}+8c_{3}\" eeimg=\"1\"/>。从而</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=c_%7B1%7D%2Bc_%7B3%7D%3D0%5Cquad2c_%7B1%7D%2B8c_%7B3%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7BD%7D%7B2%7D%5CRightarrow+c_%7B3%7D%3D-c_%7B1%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7BD%7D%7B12%7D\" alt=\"c_{1}+c_{3}=0\\quad2c_{1}+8c_{3}=\\frac{D}{2}\\Rightarrow c_{3}=-c_{1}=\\frac{D}{12}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>代回 (3) 得到中心扩张后的 Virasoro 的显式表达</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BL_%7Bm%7D%2CL_%7Bn%7D%5D%3D%28m-n%29L_%7Bm%2Bn%7D%2B%5Cfrac%7Bc%7D%7B12%7Dm%28m%5E%7B2%7D-1%29%5Cdelta_%7Bm%2Bn%2C0%7D\" alt=\"[L_{m},L_{n}]=(m-n)L_{m+n}+\\frac{c}{12}m(m^{2}-1)\\delta_{m+n,0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> （4）</p><p>这时常数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=c\" alt=\"c\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 实际上就是时空维数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=D\" alt=\"D\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。中心扩张项会与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=c\" alt=\"c\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 成比例关系是一种量子效应（这也是我对于中心扩张最不理解的地方，以前看CFT时也是这种说法，如果有人能告诉我这是怎么回事的话就最好了~）， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=c\" alt=\"c\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 亦称作中心荷，可以看作幺正算符。</p><p>Property:</p><ul><li>注意到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A%280%29%3DA%28%5Cpm1%29%3D0\" alt=\"A(0)=A(\\pm1)=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，不难发现 Virasoro 代数生成元 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B0%7D\" alt=\"L_{0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B%5Cpm1%7D\" alt=\"L_{\\pm1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可构成子代数</li></ul><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BL_%7B%5Cpm1%7D%2CL_%7B0%7D%5D%3D%5Cpm+L_%7B%5Cpm1%7D%2C%5Cquad%5BL_%7B1%7D%2CL_%7B-1%7D%5D%3DL_%7B0%7D\" alt=\"[L_{\\pm1},L_{0}]=\\pm L_{\\pm1},\\quad[L_{1},L_{-1}]=L_{0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>这正是 Lie 代数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7Bsl%7D%282%2C%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%29\" alt=\"\\mathbb{sl}(2,\\mathbb{R})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><ul><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7B-n%7D%3D%28%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%29%5E%7B%2A%7D\" alt=\"\\alpha_{-n}=(\\alpha_{n})^{*}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 且 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ctilde%7B%5Calpha%7D_%7B-n%7D%3D%28%5Ctilde%7B%5Calpha%7D_%7Bn%7D%29%5E%7B%2A%7D\" alt=\"\\tilde{\\alpha}_{-n}=(\\tilde{\\alpha}_{n})^{*}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5CLeftrightarrow%5Cquad+L_%7B-m%7D%3DL_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cdagger%7D\" alt=\"\\Leftrightarrow\\quad L_{-m}=L_{m}^{\\dagger}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</li></ul><p>Corallory 1: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5B%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%2C%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%5D%3D%5B%5Ctilde%7B%5Calpha%7D_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%2C%5Ctilde%7B%5Calpha%7D_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%5D%3Dm%5Ceta%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%5Cdelta_%7Bm%2Bn%2C0%7D\" alt=\"[\\alpha_{m}^{\\mu},\\alpha_{n}^{\\nu}]=[\\tilde{\\alpha}_{m}^{\\mu},\\tilde{\\alpha}_{n}^{\\nu}]=m\\eta^{\\mu\\nu}\\delta_{m+n,0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Corollary 2: 对于闭弦情形，Virasoro 代数的左行波与右行波均包含了 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7Bsl%7D%282%2C%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%29\" alt=\"\\mathbb{sl}(2,\\mathbb{R})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，从而闭弦总包含 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=SL%282%2C%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%29%5Ctimes+SL%282%2C%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%29%5Crightarrow+SO%282%2C2%29\" alt=\"SL(2,\\mathbb{R})\\times SL(2,\\mathbb{R})\\rightarrow SO(2,2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 对称性，如果在此基础上考虑时空的紧致化，我们便可以在弦论中得到一类新的对偶——T对偶。</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha\" alt=\"\\alpha\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 和 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ctilde%7B%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"\\tilde{\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 只是弦的正负模态，为了将理论量子化，我们还需要定义其自伴算子的谱。</p><ul><li><b>正则协变量子化</b></li></ul><ol><li>力学量算符化</li></ol><p>物理上正则量子化要求我们将力学量算符化，对于玻色弦，从经典弦的模式展开已经知道其运动模式由 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=x%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"x^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=p%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"p^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 及 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha%28%5Ctilde%7B%5Calpha%7D%29\" alt=\"\\alpha(\\tilde{\\alpha})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 决定。质心坐标与动量的算符化与一般量子力学相似，仅需将时空几何的影响考虑进来，即 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Bx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%2Cp%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%5D%3Di%5Ceta%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D\" alt=\"[x^{\\mu},p^{\\nu}]=i\\eta^{\\mu\\nu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。正负模态的对易关系已由 Virasoro 代数的 Corollary 1 给出，现在考虑它们的算符化，要注意的是 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ctilde%7B%5Calpha%7D\" alt=\"\\tilde{\\alpha}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 并不是 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha\" alt=\"\\alpha\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的自伴算子，它们各自都有一套算子谱与自伴算子谱。</p><p>Definition 4: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B%5Csqrt%7Bm%7D%7D%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%2C%5Cquad+a_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cdagger%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B%5Csqrt%7Bm%7D%7D%5Calpha_%7B-m%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%28m%3E0%29\" alt=\"a_{m}^{\\mu}=\\frac{1}{\\sqrt{m}}\\alpha_{m}^{\\mu},\\quad a_{m}^{\\mu\\dagger}=\\frac{1}{\\sqrt{m}}\\alpha_{-m}^{\\mu}(m&gt;0)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为正模态的算子与自伴算子。负模态的算符化与其类似。</p><p>Corollary 1: 显然它们相当于正模态或负模态的升降算符。满足对易关系</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ba_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%2Ca_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%5Cdagger%7D%5D%3D%5B%5Ctilde%7Ba%7D_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%2C%5Ctilde%7Ba%7D_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%5Cdagger%7D%5D%3D%5Ceta%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%5Cdelta_%7Bm%2Cn%7D%5C+%28m%2Cn%3E0%29\" alt=\"[a_{m}^{\\mu},a_{n}^{\\nu\\dagger}]=[\\tilde{a}_{m}^{\\mu},\\tilde{a}_{n}^{\\nu\\dagger}]=\\eta^{\\mu\\nu}\\delta_{m,n}\\ (m,n&gt;0)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Corollary 2: 算子谱由 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"a_{m}^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 对基态的作用给出， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%7C0%5Crangle%3D0%5C+%28m%3E0%29\" alt=\"a_{m}^{\\mu}|0\\rangle=0\\ (m&gt;0)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C0%5Crangle\" alt=\"|0\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为基态。</p><p>Anomaly 1: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ba_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B0%7D%2Ca_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B0%5Cdagger%7D%5D%3D%5B%5Ctilde%7Ba%7D_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B0%7D%2C%5Ctilde+a_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B0%5Cdagger%7D%5D%3D-1\" alt=\"[a_{m}^{0},a_{n}^{0\\dagger}]=[\\tilde{a}_{m}^{0},\\tilde a_{n}^{0\\dagger}]=-1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。这意味着只要模态算符有奇数个时间分量出现，物理量的模就将出现负值。</p><p>Example 1: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Clangle0%7Ca_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B0%7Da_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B0%5Cdagger%7D%7C0%5Crangle%3D-1%5Cquad%5Clangle0%7C0%5Crangle%3D1\" alt=\"\\langle0|a_{m}^{0}a_{m}^{0\\dagger}|0\\rangle=-1\\quad\\langle0|0\\rangle=1\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>在物理中出现为负的模长显然是不合理的，否则<b>因果性</b>与<b>幺正性</b>均无法保证。故我们必须在弦论中剔除掉所有负模长的谱，这为我们提供了限制一个自洽弦论的最基本的条件。</p><p>2. 物理态</p><p>对于弦的经典理论（Witt 代数），由弦的运动方程（Jacobi 等式）我们已经知道 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B0%7D%3D0\" alt=\"L_{0}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，但对于量子化的理论（Viraosoro 代数），由中心扩张知道需要添加一项常数项来消除排序导致的反常，定义 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D%7C%5Ctextrm%7Bphys.%7D%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\phi\\rangle=|\\textrm{phys.}\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为一在壳的量子态，中心扩张导致 Witt 代数与 Virasoro 代数中 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7B0%7D%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D0%5CRightarrow0%3D%5Clangle%5Cphi%7C%5BL_%7Bm%7D%2CL_%7B-m%7D%5D%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D%5Cfrac%7Bc%7D%7B12%7Dm%28m%5E%7B2%7D-1%29%5Cneq0\" alt=\"L_{0}|\\phi\\rangle=0\\Rightarrow0=\\langle\\phi|[L_{m},L_{-m}]|\\phi\\rangle=\\frac{c}{12}m(m^{2}-1)\\neq0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的矛盾。故对于量子化弦理论，量子态质壳条件应修正为</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28L_%7B0%7D-a%29%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"(L_{0}-a)|\\phi\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> （开弦）， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28L_%7B0%7D-a%29%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D%28%5Ctilde%7BL%7D_%7B0%7D-a%29%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"(L_{0}-a)|\\phi\\rangle=(\\tilde{L}_{0}-a)|\\phi\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> （闭弦）。</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a\" alt=\"a\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 即用以消除反常的常数项，实际的物理要求还需要其满足一定的限制条件，这与玻色弦的自洽性也是息息相关的，我们将在下一章详细讨论。</p><p>由 (4) 得， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BL_%7Bm%7D%2CL_%7B-m%7D%5D%3D2mL_%7B0%7D%2B%5Cfrac%7Bc%7D%7B12%7Dm%28m%5E%7B2%7D-1%29\" alt=\"[L_{m},L_{-m}]=2mL_{0}+\\frac{c}{12}m(m^{2}-1)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。这意味着 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7Bm%7D\" alt=\"L_{m}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 不再湮灭所有物理态，仅有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=m%3E0\" alt=\"m&gt;0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的一半生成元能够满足 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7Bm%7D%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"L_{m}|\\phi\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。从而可以给出弦论中物理态的定义。</p><p>Definition 5: 对于一在壳的量子态 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\phi\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，给定 Virasoro 代数，若该量子态满足</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7Bm%3E0%7D%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D0%5C+%5Ctextrm%7B%E6%88%96%7D%5C+%5Clangle%5Cphi%7CL_%7Bm%3C0%7D%3D0\" alt=\"L_{m&gt;0}|\\phi\\rangle=0\\ \\textrm{或}\\ \\langle\\phi|L_{m&lt;0}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> (微分同胚不变性导致的能动张量零迹) 且 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28L_%7B0%7D-a%29%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"(L_{0}-a)|\\phi\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> (质壳条件)，</p><p>则<img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle\" alt=\"|\\phi\\rangle\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 称为 Virasoro 代数下的物理态。</p><p>3. 质量谱</p><p>现在讨论量子化后弦的质量谱。对于开弦，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha%27M%5E%7B2%7D%3D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%2B%5Cinfty%7D%5Calpha_%7B-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D-a%3DN-a%5C%5C+%5CRightarrow+M%5E%7B2%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7BN-a%7D%7B%5Calpha%27%7D\" alt=\"\\alpha&#39;M^{2}=\\sum_{n=1}^{+\\infty}\\alpha_{-n}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}-a=N-a\\\\ \\Rightarrow M^{2}=\\frac{N-a}{\\alpha&#39;}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>其中<img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=N%3D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%2B%5Cinfty%7D%5Calpha_%7B-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%3D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%2B%5Cinfty%7Dna_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B%5Cdagger%7D%5Ccdot+a_%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"N=\\sum_{n=1}^{+\\infty}\\alpha_{-n}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}=\\sum_{n=1}^{+\\infty}na_{n}^{\\dagger}\\cdot a_{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/>为数算符 。</p><p>对于闭弦，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B4%7D%5Calpha%27M%5E%7B2%7D%3D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%2B%5Cinfty%7D%5Calpha_%7B-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D-a%3D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%2B%5Cinfty%7D%5Ctilde%7B%5Calpha%7D_%7B-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Ctilde%7B%5Calpha%7D_%7Bn%7D-a%3DN-a%3D%5Ctilde%7BN%7D-a%5C%5C%5CRightarrow+M%5E%7B2%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7BN-a%7D%7B4%5Calpha%27%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B%5Ctilde%7BN%7D-a%7D%7B4%5Calpha%27%7D\" alt=\"\\frac{1}{4}\\alpha&#39;M^{2}=\\sum_{n=1}^{+\\infty}\\alpha_{-n}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}-a=\\sum_{n=1}^{+\\infty}\\tilde{\\alpha}_{-n}\\cdot\\tilde{\\alpha}_{n}-a=N-a=\\tilde{N}-a\\\\\\Rightarrow M^{2}=\\frac{N-a}{4\\alpha&#39;}=\\frac{\\tilde{N}-a}{4\\alpha&#39;}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>同时在闭弦中正规排序的常数项 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a\" alt=\"a\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可以自动消去，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28L_%7B0%7D-a%29%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D%28%5Ctilde%7BL%7D_%7B0%7D-a%29%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D0%5CRightarrow%28L_%7B0%7D-%5Ctilde%7BL%7D_%7B0%7D%29%7C%5Cphi%5Crangle%3D0\" alt=\"(L_{0}-a)|\\phi\\rangle=(\\tilde{L}_{0}-a)|\\phi\\rangle=0\\Rightarrow(L_{0}-\\tilde{L}_{0})|\\phi\\rangle=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>这也意味着 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=N%3D%5Ctilde%7BN%7D\" alt=\"N=\\tilde{N}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，这是自然的结果，因为左行波解必然与右行波解自由度相同。这也是它们之间的唯一独立约束。</p><p>对于 Lorentz 生成元， 我们知道正规排序不会影响其对称性，故无需进行量子修正。对于开弦，</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=J%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%3Dx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7Dp%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D-x%5E%7B%5Cnu%7Dp%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D-i%5Csum_%7Bn%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7Bn%7D%28%5Calpha%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D_%7B-n%7D%5Calpha%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D_%7Bn%7D-%5Calpha_%7B-n%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%29\" alt=\"J^{\\mu\\nu}=x^{\\mu}p^{\\nu}-x^{\\nu}p^{\\mu}-i\\sum_{n=1}^{\\infty}\\frac{1}{n}(\\alpha^{\\mu}_{-n}\\alpha^{\\nu}_{n}-\\alpha_{-n}^{\\nu}\\alpha_{n}^{\\mu})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>我们现在考虑 Virasoro 生成元与 Lorentz 生成元的代数关系，已经知道 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=L_%7Bm%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D-%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5Calpha_%7Bm-n%7D%5Ccdot%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"L_{m}=\\frac{1}{2}\\sum_{n=-\\infty}^{\\infty}\\alpha_{m-n}\\cdot\\alpha_{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，那么</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cbegin%7Balign%7D+%5BL_%7Bm%7D%2Cl%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%5D%26%3D%5BL_%7Bm%7D%2Cx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7Dp%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D-x%5E%7B%5Cnu%7Dp%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5D%5C%5C+%26%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Ceta_%7B%5Crho%5Clambda%7D%5B%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Crho%7D%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5E%7B%5Clambda%7D%2B%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5E%7B%5Crho%7D%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Clambda%7D%2Cx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7Dp%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D-x%5E%7B%5Cnu%7Dp%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5D%5C%5C+%26%3D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7B2%7D%5Ceta_%7B%5Crho%5Clambda%7D%5B%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Crho%7Dp%5E%7B%5Clambda%7D%2Bp%5E%7B%5Crho%7D%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Clambda%7D%2Cx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D-x%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5D%5C%5C+%26%3D-i%28%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D-%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%29+%5Cend%7Balign%7D\" alt=\"\\begin{align} [L_{m},l^{\\mu\\nu}]&amp;=[L_{m},x^{\\mu}p^{\\nu}-x^{\\nu}p^{\\mu}]\\\\ &amp;=\\frac{1}{2}\\eta_{\\rho\\lambda}[\\alpha_{m}^{\\rho}\\alpha_{0}^{\\lambda}+\\alpha_{0}^{\\rho}\\alpha_{m}^{\\lambda},x^{\\mu}p^{\\nu}-x^{\\nu}p^{\\mu}]\\\\ &amp;=\\frac{1}{2}\\eta_{\\rho\\lambda}[\\alpha_{m}^{\\rho}p^{\\lambda}+p^{\\rho}\\alpha_{m}^{\\lambda},x^{\\mu}\\alpha_{0}^{\\nu}-x^{\\nu}\\alpha_{0}^{\\mu}]\\\\ &amp;=-i(\\alpha_{m}^{\\mu}\\alpha_{0}^{\\nu}-\\alpha_{m}^{\\nu}\\alpha_{0}^{\\mu}) \\end{align}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </p><p>而对于 Lorentz 生成元关于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"\\alpha_{n}^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的项，有</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BL_%7Bm%7D%2CJ%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D-l%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%5D%3D%5Cfrac%7B-i%7D%7B2%7D%5Csum_%7Bn%3D-%5Cinfty%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5Csum_%7Bk%3D1%7D%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D%5Cfrac%7B1%7D%7Bk%7D%5Ceta_%7B%5Crho%5Clambda%7D%5B%5Calpha_%7Bm-n%7D%5E%7B%5Crho%7D%5Calpha_%7Bn%7D%5E%7B%5Clambda%7D%2C%5Calpha_%7B-k%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Calpha_%7Bk%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D-%5Calpha_%7B-k%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%5Calpha_%7Bk%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5D%3Di%28%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D-%5Calpha_%7Bm%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%5Calpha_%7B0%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%29\" alt=\"[L_{m},J^{\\mu\\nu}-l^{\\mu\\nu}]=\\frac{-i}{2}\\sum_{n=-\\infty}^{\\infty}\\sum_{k=1}^{\\infty}\\frac{1}{k}\\eta_{\\rho\\lambda}[\\alpha_{m-n}^{\\rho}\\alpha_{n}^{\\lambda},\\alpha_{-k}^{\\mu}\\alpha_{k}^{\\nu}-\\alpha_{-k}^{\\nu}\\alpha_{k}^{\\mu}]=i(\\alpha_{m}^{\\mu}\\alpha_{0}^{\\nu}-\\alpha_{m}^{\\nu}\\alpha_{0}^{\\mu})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>从而 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5BL_%7Bm%7D%2CJ%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%5D%3D0\" alt=\"[L_{m},J^{\\mu\\nu}]=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。即 Virasoro 生成元与 Lorentz 生成元对易。这意味着物理态条件在 Lorentz 变换下是保持不变的（类似的可以计算得到物理态条件在 Poincare 变换下就不是不变的了）。所以物理态必须以 Lorentz 多重态的形式出现（同时也因为我们这里使用的量子化方式已经默认了物理形式总是 Lorentz 协变的）。</p><hr/><p>限于篇幅剔除负模只写了一半，这周会把剩下的部分写完，再下一次就是光锥量子化了，大概就填完最基本的坑了。弦振幅和弦的路径积分量子化要不要写完全看我心情(*/ω＼*)检查的时候突然觉得这回写得又不数学又不物理……望各位见谅</p><p>最后代表逢田姐消灭全天下的梨黑(tui)o(≥▽≤o)</p><p><b>References for
