data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-739391462be432a2f717bd56d000d640_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-739391462be432a2f717bd56d000d640_b.jpg\"/><figcaption>图1 因为懒得到PDF找图所以图片均为手绘(*/ω＼*)字丑手残勿怪</figcaption></figure><p>一般来说，单个图是无法覆盖整个流形的，可以被单个图覆盖的流形我们称之为平凡流形，例如 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5E%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{R}^{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 即为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=n\" alt=\"n\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 维的平凡流形。</p><p>微分流形的定义（2）同时限制了图与图之间必须是相容的，如图2所示，相容的图会给出部分重合的坐标系（定义圆环 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=S%5E%7B1%7D\" alt=\"S^{1}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 即可以有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28-%5Cpi%2C%5Cpi%29\" alt=\"(-\\pi,\\pi)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，也可有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%280%2C2%5Cpi%29\" alt=\"(0,2\\pi)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ），而重叠部分的坐标变换显然都是光滑映射，从而我们说重叠部分的点集集合互相<b>微分同胚</b>（diffeomorphism）。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f2631bc5c4f229d81b48b6f139e6f70e_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"617\" data-rawheight=\"579\" data-size=\"normal\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"617\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f2631bc5c4f229d81b48b6f139e6f70e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;617&#39; height=&#39;579&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"617\" data-rawheight=\"579\" data-size=\"normal\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"617\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f2631bc5c4f229d81b48b6f139e6f70e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f2631bc5c4f229d81b48b6f139e6f70e_b.jpg\"/><figcaption>图2 重叠部分的坐标变换（为了准确我决定还是给出处，几乎所有广相书上讲 manifold 和 chart 的地方都会讲到这张图中的关系，梁书上略有不同）</figcaption></figure><p>Definition 3: 若存在两集合 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%2C+N\" alt=\"M, N\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cexists+C%5E%7B%5Cinfty%7D\" alt=\"\\exists C^{\\infty}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cphi%3AM%5Crightarrow+N\" alt=\"\\phi:M\\rightarrow N\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 及 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cphi%5E%7B-1%7D%3AN%5Crightarrow+M\" alt=\"\\phi^{-1}:N\\rightarrow M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，我们则称 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cphi\" alt=\"\\phi\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为微分同胚， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M%2CN\" alt=\"M,N\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 互相微分同胚。微分同胚是可以对流形间的映射提出的最高要求，一般可以认为互相微分同胚的流形是等价的。</p><p>另外值得注意的一点是，我们利用流形来描述时空（拓扑空间），流形一定是拓扑空间但拓扑空间未必是一个流形，因为流形还要求具有连续可微的性质。</p><ul><li>函数，矢量，对偶矢量与张量</li></ul><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cphi%3AM%5Crightarrow+R\" alt=\"\\phi:M\\rightarrow R\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 称为流形上的<b>函数</b>（Function），其中 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=R\" alt=\"R\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为实数集，这里我们都只讨论实函数。</p><p>Example 4: 坐标 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=x%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"x^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>对于一个具有方向的物理量，我们可以用<b>矢量</b>（Vector）来表示，矢量的定义要求我们首先定义：</p><ol><li>矢量空间</li><li>曲线 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cgamma%28t%29\" alt=\"\\gamma(t)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </li><li>某点 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=P\" alt=\"P\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的切矢量</li><li>切矢空间（切矢场）</li></ol><p>Definition 5: 对于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%2CV%2CW%5Cin%5Cmathbb%7BV%7D\" alt=\"U,V,W\\in\\mathbb{V}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，当且仅当满足下列条件时 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BV%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{V}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 可构成矢量空间：</p><ol><li>结合律： <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%2B%28V%2BW%29%3D%28U%2BV%29%2BW\" alt=\"U+(V+W)=(U+V)+W\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </li><li>封闭性： <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%2BV%5Cin%5Cmathbb%7BV%7D\" alt=\"U+V\\in\\mathbb{V}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> （ <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V%2CW\" alt=\"V,W\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%2CW\" alt=\"U,W\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 同理）</li><li>存在幺元： <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%2B0%3DU\" alt=\"U+0=U\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </li><li>每一个元素都存在逆元： <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=U%2B%28-U%29%3D0\" alt=\"U+(-U)=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </li></ol><p>Definition 6: <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的一条光滑曲线总是光滑映射 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cgamma%3AI%5Crightarrow+M\" alt=\"\\gamma:I\\rightarrow M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=I\" alt=\"I\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的一个区间。</p><p>有了曲线的定义之后，我们需要考虑物理量的作用应如何体现在曲线上，对曲线的一个基本操作自然是求导，对任意函数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f\" alt=\"f\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，有<img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cfrac%7Bd%7D%7Bdt%7D%5Cleft%5B%28f%5Ccirc%5Cgamma%29%28t%29%5Cright%5D%3D%5Cfrac%7Bdf%28%5Cgamma%28t%29%29%7D%7Bdt%7D\" alt=\"\\frac{d}{dt}\\left[(f\\circ\\gamma)(t)\\right]=\\frac{df(\\gamma(t))}{dt}\" eeimg=\"1\"/>，这实际上就是切矢量应遵循的规律。</p><p>Definition 7: 令 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cgamma%3AI%5Crightarrow%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"\\gamma:I\\rightarrow\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为过某点 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=P\" alt=\"P\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的曲线， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cgamma\" alt=\"\\gamma\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=P\" alt=\"P\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 点的切矢量是一个线性映射， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5COmega_%7BP%7D%28f%29%3D%5Cleft%5C%7B%5Cfrac%7Bdf%7D%7Bdt%7D%28%5Cgamma%28t%29%29%5Cright%5C%7D_%7Bt%3D0%7D%28%5Cgamma%28t%3D0%29%3DP%29\" alt=\"\\Omega_{P}(f)=\\left\\{\\frac{df}{dt}(\\gamma(t))\\right\\}_{t=0}(\\gamma(t=0)=P)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 构成了光滑函数 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=f%3AM%5Crightarrow+%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"f:M\\rightarrow \\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的集合空间。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=I%2CM%2C%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D%5E%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"I,M,\\mathbb{R}^{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 之间的关系如图3所示。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0e0881269ae4843dceb0aeb3c5b51363_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"566\" data-rawheight=\"418\" data-size=\"normal\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"566\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0e0881269ae4843dceb0aeb3c5b51363_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;566&#39; height=&#39;418&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"566\" data-rawheight=\"418\" data-size=\"normal\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"566\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0e0881269ae4843dceb0aeb3c5b51363_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0e0881269ae4843dceb0aeb3c5b51363_b.jpg\"/><figcaption>图3 I, M 与 R^{n} 之间的关系（这张画得特别乱……实在抱歉，原图应该是 Wheeler 书上有）</figcaption></figure><p>Claim 1：切矢空间 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7BP%7D\" alt=\"T_{P}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与方向导数（切矢量）构成的空间是等同的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5E%7B%5B5%5D%7D\" alt=\"^{[5]}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Proof 1：欲证明上述结论，我们需证明两点。</p><ol><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7BP%7D\" alt=\"T_{P}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为一矢量空间。考虑过 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=P\" alt=\"P\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 点的两条曲线 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cgamma\" alt=\"\\gamma\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Ckappa\" alt=\"\\kappa\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，相应的有 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5COmega_%7BP%7D%28f%29%3D%5Cfrac%7Bd%7D%7Bdt%7Df%28%5Cgamma%28t%29%29\" alt=\"\\Omega_{P}(f)=\\frac{d}{dt}f(\\gamma(t))\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=w_%7BP%7D%28f%29%3D%5Cfrac%7Bd%7D%7Bdt%7Df%28%5Ckappa%28t%29%29\" alt=\"w_{P}(f)=\\frac{d}{dt}f(\\kappa(t))\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，我们只需证明 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=a%5COmega_%7BP%7D%28f%29%2Bbw_%7BP%7D%28f%29\" alt=\"a\\Omega_{P}(f)+bw_{P}(f)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 也是点 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=P\" alt=\"P\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的切矢量即可。切矢量为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvartheta%28t%29%3D%5Cphi%5E%7B-1%7D%5Ba%28%5Cphi%28%5Cgamma%28t%29%29-%5Cphi%28P%29%29%2Bb%28%5Cphi%28%5Ckappa%28t%29%29-%5Cphi%28P%29%29%2B%5Cphi%28P%29%5D\" alt=\"\\vartheta(t)=\\phi^{-1}[a(\\phi(\\gamma(t))-\\phi(P))+b(\\phi(\\kappa(t))-\\phi(P))+\\phi(P)]\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，显然 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cvartheta%28t%3D0%29%3DP\" alt=\"\\vartheta(t=0)=P\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。此条证毕。</li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7BP%7D\" alt=\"T_{P}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 维数相同。为证明此条我们需要确定 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7BP%7D\" alt=\"T_{P}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的基底（基底的个数决定了该矢量空间的秩，矢量空间的维数与其秩相等）。由链式法则， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5COmega_%7BP%7D%28f%29%3D%5Cfrac%7Bdf%7D%7Bdt%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7Bdx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%7D%7Bdt%7D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+f%7D%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%7D\" alt=\"\\Omega_{P}(f)=\\frac{df}{dt}=\\frac{dx^{\\mu}}{dt}\\frac{\\partial f}{\\partial x^{\\mu}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。即我们可以定义基底为自然基底 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"\\partial_{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。而 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"\\partial_{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的秩正是由 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的维数决定的，从而 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T_%7BP%7D\" alt=\"T_{P}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 与 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=M\" alt=\"M\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 具有相同维数。此条证毕。</li></ol><p>综上，我们只需要以 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"\\partial_{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为基底即可将其构成的空间视作切矢空间。</p><p>现在我们可以给出矢量的定义。</p><p>Definition 8：对一矢量 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V\" alt=\"V\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V%3DV%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Chat%7Be%7D_%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"V=V^{\\mu}\\hat{e}_{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"V^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为矢量在空间中的各个分量， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Chat%7Be%7D_%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"\\hat{e}_{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为矢量的基底，通常取 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5C%7B%5Chat%7Be%7D_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5C%7D%3D%5C%7B%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5C%7D\" alt=\"\\{\\hat{e}_{\\mu}\\}=\\{\\partial_{\\mu}\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。相应的在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V\" alt=\"V\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 所指向的终点 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=P\" alt=\"P\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 存在切矢量 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5COmega_%7BP%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%3D%5Cleft%28%5Cfrac%7Bdx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%7D%7Bdt%7D%5Cright%29_%7Bt%3D0%7D\" alt=\"\\Omega_{P}^{\\mu}=\\left(\\frac{dx^{\\mu}}{dt}\\right)_{t=0}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>注意到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V\" alt=\"V\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是与图无关的，而基底的选取却与图有关（ <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%27%7D%5Cequiv%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%7D%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7B%5Cmu%27%7D%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7B%5Cmu%27%7D%7D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial%7D%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%7D%3DJ_%7B%5Cmu%27%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"\\partial_{\\mu&#39;}\\equiv\\frac{\\partial}{\\partial x^{\\mu&#39;}}=\\frac{\\partial x^{\\mu}}{\\partial x^{\\mu&#39;}}\\frac{\\partial}{\\partial x^{\\mu}}=J_{\\mu&#39;}^{\\mu}\\partial_{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/>，包含坐标变换产生的 Jacobi 行列式）。而既然矢量与图无关，则 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V%3DV%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D%3DV%5E%7B%5Cmu%27%7D%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%27%7D\" alt=\"V=V^{\\mu}\\partial_{\\mu}=V^{\\mu&#39;}\\partial_{\\mu&#39;}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，变换可以得到</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7B%5Cmu%27%7D%7DV%5E%7B%5Cmu%27%7D\" alt=\"V^{\\mu}=\\frac{\\partial x^{\\mu}}{\\partial x^{\\mu&#39;}}V^{\\mu&#39;}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>我们通常约定 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"V^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 就是一个矢量， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmu\" alt=\"\\mu\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的不同值即表示不同的分量，按照上述方式变换的物理量就是矢量。</p><p>与矢量对应的还有<b>对偶矢量</b>（Dual Vector），对偶矢量的集合构成对偶空间，终点曲线由对偶矢量与余切矢构成的余切空间共同决定。比如 Hilbert 空间中的左矢就是一个右矢的对偶矢量。具体性质与矢量类似，这里不再赘述，直接给出定义。</p><p>Definition 9：对于 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的矢量空间 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V\" alt=\"V\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%5Comega%3AV%5Crightarrow%5Cmathbb%7BR%7D\" alt=\"\\omega:V\\rightarrow\\mathbb{R}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 称为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V\" alt=\"V\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的对偶矢量。全体对偶矢量的集合称为对偶矢量空间。一般记做 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V%5E%7B%2A%7D\" alt=\"V^{*}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>矢量 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=x%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"x^{\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 总是以坐标函数的方式变换，而对偶矢量按照基底的方式变换。</p><p>最后到张量，张量是由矢量与对偶矢量的直积构成的多重映射。</p><p>Definition 10： <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T%3DV_%7BP_%7B1%7D%7D%5Cotimes+V_%7BP_%7B2%7D%7D%5Cotimes%5Ccdots%5Cotimes+V_%7BP_%7B1%7D%7D%5E%7B%2A%7D%5Cotimes+V_%7BP_%7B2%7D%7D%5E%7B%2A%7D\" alt=\"T=V_{P_{1}}\\otimes V_{P_{2}}\\otimes\\cdots\\otimes V_{P_{1}}^{*}\\otimes V_{P_{2}}^{*}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，若这个张量的构成中存在 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=k\" alt=\"k\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 个矢量空间， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=l\" alt=\"l\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 个对偶矢量空间，则我们称 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T\" alt=\"T\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为一 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28k%2Cl%29\" alt=\"(k,l)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 型张量。</p><p>Example 5：标量（ <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%280%2C0%29\" alt=\"(0,0)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 张量），矢量（ <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%281%2C0%29\" alt=\"(1,0)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 张量）与对偶矢量（ <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%280%2C1%29\" alt=\"(0,1)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 张量）都是特殊的张量。</p><p>Example 6： <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T%3DT%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%5Crho%5Clambda%7D_%7B%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5Calpha%5Cbeta%7D%28%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cmu%7D%5Cotimes%5Cpartial_%7B%5Cnu%7D%5Cotimes%5Cpartial_%7B%5Crho%7D%5Cotimes%5Cpartial_%7B%5Clambda%7D%5Cotimes+dx%5E%7B%5Calpha%7D%5Cotimes+ax%5E%7B%5Cbeta%7D%29\" alt=\"T=T^{\\mu\\nu\\rho\\lambda}_{\\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\alpha\\beta}(\\partial_{\\mu}\\otimes\\partial_{\\nu}\\otimes\\partial_{\\rho}\\otimes\\partial_{\\lambda}\\otimes dx^{\\alpha}\\otimes ax^{\\beta})\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是一个 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%284%2C2%29\" alt=\"(4,2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 型张量。</p><p>张量的变换方式满足：</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=T%5E%7B%5Cmu_%7B1%7D%5Ccdots%5Cmu_%7Bk%7D%7D_%7B%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5Cnu_%7B1%7D%5Ccdots%5Cnu_%7Bl%7D%7D%3D%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7B%27%5Cmu_%7B1%7D%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7B%5Crho_%7B1%7D%7D%7D%5Ccdots%5Cfrac%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7B%5Csigma_%7Bl%7D%7D%7D%7B%5Cpartial+x%5E%7B%27%5Cnu_%7Bl%7D%7D%7DT%5E%7B%5Crho_%7B1%7D%5Ccdots%5Crho_%7Bk%7D%7D_%7B%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5C+%5Csigma_%7B1%7D%5Ccdots%5Csigma_%7Bl%7D%7D\" alt=\"T^{\\mu_{1}\\cdots\\mu_{k}}_{\\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\nu_{1}\\cdots\\nu_{l}}=\\frac{\\partial x^{&#39;\\mu_{1}}}{\\partial x^{\\rho_{1}}}\\cdots\\frac{\\partial x^{\\sigma_{l}}}{\\partial x^{&#39;\\nu_{l}}}T^{\\rho_{1}\\cdots\\rho_{k}}_{\\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\ \\sigma_{1}\\cdots\\sigma_{l}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><ul><li>度规</li></ul><p>现在我们已经具备了在局域时空中讨论物理量变化的条件，而对于一个弯曲时空而言，想要刻画它的弯曲程度对于物理量的影响，我们需要一个能够描述其弯曲程度并与张量相关的物理量，这要求我们引入<b>度规</b>（Metric）的概念。</p><p>Definition 11：矢量空间上的一个度规 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g\" alt=\"g\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V\" alt=\"V\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 上的一个特殊的 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%280%2C2%29\" alt=\"(0,2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 张量。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g%3Dg_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7Ddx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7Ddx%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D\" alt=\"g=g_{\\mu\\nu}dx^{\\mu}dx^{\\nu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。它具有如下性质：</p><ol><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g\" alt=\"g\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是对称的。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%3Dg%5E%7B%5Cnu%5Cmu%7D\" alt=\"g^{\\mu\\nu}=g^{\\nu\\mu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7Dg%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%3D%5Cmathbb%7BI%7D\" alt=\"g_{\\mu\\nu}g^{\\mu\\nu}=\\mathbb{I}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </li><li><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g\" alt=\"g\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是非退化的。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7D%3D0%5Cforall+u%5Cin+V%5CRightarrow+v%3D0%5Cin+V\" alt=\"g_{\\mu\\nu}=0\\forall u\\in V\\Rightarrow v=0\\in V\" eeimg=\"1\"/> </li></ol><p>度规是一个 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%280%2C2%29\" alt=\"(0,2)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 张量的同时意味着它作用于两个矢量时可以得到一个数。 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7DV%5E%7B%5Csigma%7DV%5E%7B%5Cgamma%7D%5Chat%7Be%7D%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%28%5Chat%7Be%7D_%7B%5Csigma%7D%29%5Chat%7Be%7D%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%28%5Chat%7Be%7D_%7B%5Cgamma%7D%29%3Dg_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7DV%5E%7B%5Csigma%7DV%5E%7B%5Cgamma%7D%5Cdelta%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D_%7B%5Csigma%7D%5Cdelta%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D_%7B%5Cgamma%7D%3Dg_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7DV%5E%7B%5Cmu%7DV%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%3DG\" alt=\"g_{\\mu\\nu}V^{\\sigma}V^{\\gamma}\\hat{e}^{\\mu}(\\hat{e}_{\\sigma})\\hat{e}^{\\nu}(\\hat{e}_{\\gamma})=g_{\\mu\\nu}V^{\\sigma}V^{\\gamma}\\delta^{\\mu}_{\\sigma}\\delta^{\\nu}_{\\gamma}=g_{\\mu\\nu}V^{\\mu}V^{\\nu}=G\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，由此我们发现矢量与对偶矢量可以通过与度规作用互相转换。</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%3Dg%5E%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7DV_%7B%5Cnu%7D\" alt=\"V^{\\mu}=g^{\\mu\\nu}V_{\\nu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> , <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V_%7B%5Cmu%7D%3Dg_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7DV%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D\" alt=\"V_{\\mu}=g_{\\mu\\nu}V^{\\nu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>度规就是从矢量空间到对偶矢量空间的一一映射。</p><p>下面我们利用度规定义广相中的第一个可观测量——<b>距离</b>（Distance）。如图4所示，对于一个平直时空而言， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=A\" alt=\"A\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 点到 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=B\" alt=\"B\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 点的距离即为每一段线元的积分，而每一段线元的长度可以通过切矢量表出，从而有</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=l%3D%5Cint_%7BA%7D%5E%7BB%7Ddt%5Csqrt%7B%5Cfrac%7Bd%5Cvec%7Bx%7D%7D%7Bdt%7D%5Ccdot%5Cfrac%7Bd%5Cvec%7Bx%7D%7D%7Bdt%7D%7D\" alt=\"l=\\int_{A}^{B}dt\\sqrt{\\frac{d\\vec{x}}{dt}\\cdot\\frac{d\\vec{x}}{dt}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><figure data-size=\"normal\"><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-941e4d0b28e58fa83f1daa328b56bb00_b.jpg\" data-rawwidth=\"662\" data-rawheight=\"284\" data-size=\"normal\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"662\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-941e4d0b28e58fa83f1daa328b56bb00_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;662&#39; height=&#39;284&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"662\" data-rawheight=\"284\" data-size=\"normal\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"662\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-941e4d0b28e58fa83f1daa328b56bb00_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-941e4d0b28e58fa83f1daa328b56bb00_b.jpg\"/><figcaption>图4 距离与切矢量的联系</figcaption></figure><p>对于一般的流形，曲线的弯曲变化可以由度规表出，我们可以写出</p><p><img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=dl%3D%5Csqrt%7B%7Cg_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7Ddx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7Ddx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7D%7C%7D\" alt=\"dl=\\sqrt{|g_{\\mu\\nu}dx^{\\mu}dx^{\\mu}|}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，</p><p>定义 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=ds%5E%7B2%7D%3Dg_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7Ddx%5E%7B%5Cmu%7Ddx%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D\" alt=\"ds^{2}=g_{\\mu\\nu}dx^{\\mu}dx^{\\nu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=ds%5E%7B2%7D\" alt=\"ds^{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 称作线元，在实际处理问题时我们会经常碰到它。而对于广义相对论所讨论的4维弯曲时空，定义如下：</p><p>Definition 12：在流形上给定度规场 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g\" alt=\"g\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=%28M%2Cg%29\" alt=\"(M,g)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 称为广义 Riemann 空间。若 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g%3D%5Ctextrm%7Bdiag%7D%28%2B%2C%2B%2C%5Ccdots%2C%2B%29\" alt=\"g=\\textrm{diag}(+,+,\\cdots,+)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，则为 Riemann 空间；若 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g%3D%5Ctextrm%7Bdiag%7D%28-%2C%2B%2C%2B%2C%5Ccdots%29\" alt=\"g=\\textrm{diag}(-,+,+,\\cdots)\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，则叫 Lorentz 空间（也有很多叫伪 Riemann 空间的，自己心里清楚就好~），物理上称作时空。</p><p>Example 7：Euclid 空间： <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=R%5E%7Bn%7D%3D%5C%7B%28x_%7B1%7D%2C%5Ccdots%2Cx_%7Bn%7D%29%5C%7D\" alt=\"R^{n}=\\{(x_{1},\\cdots,x_{n})\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=ds%5E%7B2%7D%3Ddx_%7B1%7D%5Cotimes+dx_%7B1%7D%2B%5Ccdots%2Bdx_%7Bn%7D%5Cotimes+dx_%7Bn%7D\" alt=\"ds^{2}=dx_{1}\\otimes dx_{1}+\\cdots+dx_{n}\\otimes dx_{n}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>Example 8：Minkowski 时空： <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=R%5E%7B4%7D%3D%5C%7B%28x_%7B1%7D%2Cx_%7B2%7D%2Cx_%7B3%7D%2Cx_%7B4%7D%29%5C%7D\" alt=\"R^{4}=\\{(x_{1},x_{2},x_{3},x_{4})\\}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=ds%5E%7B2%7D%3D-%28dx%5E%7B0%7D%29%5E%7B2%7D%2B%28dx%5E%7B1%7D%29%5E%7B2%7D%2B%28dx%5E%7B2%7D%29%5E%7B2%7D%2B%28dx%5E%7B3%7D%29%5E%7B2%7D\" alt=\"ds^{2}=-(dx^{0})^{2}+(dx^{1})^{2}+(dx^{2})^{2}+(dx^{3})^{2}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><p>对于 Lorentz 空间， <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7DV%5E%7B%5Cmu%7DV%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D\" alt=\"g_{\\mu\\nu}V^{\\mu}V^{\\nu}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 的数值为正（负）决定了矢量 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V\" alt=\"V\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 是类空（时）矢量。若 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=g_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7DV%5E%7B%5Cmu%7DV%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%3D0\" alt=\"g_{\\mu\\nu}V^{\\mu}V^{\\nu}=0\" eeimg=\"1\"/> ，则 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=V\" alt=\"V\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 为类光矢量。注意对于类时矢量，距离定义需更改为 <img src=\"https://www.zhihu.com/equation?tex=l%3D%5Cint+dt%5Csqrt%7B-g_%7B%5Cmu%5Cnu%7DV%5E%7B%5Cmu%7DV%5E%7B%5Cnu%7D%7D\" alt=\"l=\\int dt\\sqrt{-g_{\\mu\\nu}V^{\\mu}V^{\\nu}}\" eeimg=\"1\"/> 。</p><hr/><p>好啦~这回先写到这，周五之前把 String 也发出来（如果我能按时完成作业的话orz），文末给了一些参考材料，我的主要记忆都来源于 Carroll 和 Wald，以后就不特别写出来了。认真说一句，想学习还是自己看书是坠吼的0_0</p><p>最后，代表逢田姐消灭全天下的梨黑(tui)o(≥▽≤o) </p><p
